
-----title
开封 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='60917673a0fb4b65a2d5129c02d99d67_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("60917673a0fb4b65a2d5129c02d99d67");'><span id='60917673a0fb4b65a2d5129c02d99d67_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>，出生</div><div id='60917673a0fb4b65a2d5129c02d99d67' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　出生。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='86487866093546cbb79d7f68fd5c91ef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("86487866093546cbb79d7f68fd5c91ef");'><span id='86487866093546cbb79d7f68fd5c91ef_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年</a>，9岁</div><div id='86487866093546cbb79d7f68fd5c91ef' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年</a>　随父返京，出入其舅王雍之家。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='093485afea7c4f8081b5862a3ba4437a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("093485afea7c4f8081b5862a3ba4437a");'><span id='093485afea7c4f8081b5862a3ba4437a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1029')">1028-1029年</a>，21-22岁</div><div id='093485afea7c4f8081b5862a3ba4437a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　苏耆归朝换三司度支使，随父返居京师。以父荫，补太庙斋郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年10月22日</a>　以父荫在京为太庙斋郎，与兄舜元因地震而作联句诗。作品：地动聊句。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年闰2月</a>　对仁宗复制举提出补正意见。作品：投匦疏。<div id='poem_1164373' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164373' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164373?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投匦疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（天圣八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1029年闰2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164373")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164373_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164373'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164373'>某月日，臣冒死万拜疏皇帝阙下：臣昨伏睹陛下发德音，下明诏，广延天下博习之士，以大治本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164373_comment'></div>降诏之日，识者喧然，咸谓陛下张祖宗之基，致亿兆之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164373_comment'></div>虑意有所不逮，政有所未敷，虽硕辅盈庭，谏臣满署，朝访前王之陈迹，夕讲先朝之故事，尚欲亲问刍荛，广采<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>髦哲</span>，此非唯蕴才<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>抱器</span>者幸甚，实亦天下之幸甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164373_comment'></div>臣窃见分四制、限十一科，使官京师者得应贤良体用之目，潜白屋者出赴沈沦高蹈之制，州县判等，限以字数，武举策试，兼之骑射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164373_comment'></div>臣敢谓陛下之诏，体则正矣，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>纲条</span>未至，辄有营穴，愿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>铺白</span>而言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164373_comment'></div>夫贤良之科，肇于汉世，故公孙丞相之徒，多以褐衣射策，而解巾入仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164373_comment'></div>其后居位者日迩帝光，出入禁掖，志或未发，则可囊奏而建言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164373_comment'></div>政有未安，则可排闼而请见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164373_comment'></div>况其身检<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>命敕</span>，已得为朝中官，则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>口钳舌卷</span>，鲜肯言天下事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164373_comment'></div>惟是韦带绳枢之士，义疏礼隔，趋走尘土间，未尝咫尺人主之颜面，加以天阍九重，交戟数里，虽胸文陆离，笔语滂沛，而岂得一达旒纩之下哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164373_comment'></div>脱欲声鼓叩辇，则有司必以狂妄之罪罪之，且身无一命，志气自得，邦家阙政，实亦敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164373_comment'></div>汉世兼采庶士者，深有意于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164373_comment'></div>下至李唐，穿凿前轨，以谓民间不知帝王之动静，俗儒不讲朝廷之经法，专以官士者得应极言科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164373_comment'></div>及我炎统勃兴，不血刃而得天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164373_comment'></div>太祖、太宗，拓树<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>基扃</span>，诞布鸿文，而大变污俗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164373_comment'></div>真宗嗣二后教，信两汉法，笑却唐弊，追还古风，故诏贤良而草莽之士无弃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164373_comment'></div>今陛下之诏，有异于上，是未至者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164373_comment'></div>次则高蹈丘园，沈沦草泽，臣亦谓未至者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164373_comment'></div>尝闻帝者慎器与名，不务虚假，且<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/88/Comments/0")'>遁逸</span>之士，不示见闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164373_comment'></div>今陛下垂诏而杂举之，是欲使之自见闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164373_comment'></div>若出而赴陛下之诏，是其人非沈沦者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164373_comment'></div>若出而求陛下之试，是其人非高蹈者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164373_comment'></div>则皆露己扬才，干时谒进者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164373_comment'></div>非唯失彼之行，恐使人谓陛下设虚名，无精求之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164373_comment'></div>州县判等，亦未折衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164373_comment'></div>夫录人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>罪失</span>，务在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/104/Comments/0")'>浅要</span>，不过数字以见意，数句以成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164373_comment'></div>今限字二百，束之对偶，则皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>漫诞</span>而无功，繁博而寡要，不可施用，是为空言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164373_comment'></div>至如武举策试，兼之骑射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164373_comment'></div>窃观诏旨，既令先进<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/116/Comments/0")'>军机</span>，后即陛试，是陛下取将帅材者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164373_comment'></div>反使张一弓，发数矢，是陛下校一夫之艺，取一人之敌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164373_comment'></div>夫欲练将材而取一夫之技，又何异考编钟堵磬而求郑卫之音？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164373_comment'></div>伏愿贤良之科，使复两汉、真宗之制，不以官士为之限，则国家之得失可闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164373_comment'></div>沈沦高蹈者，则令诸郡守宰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/130/Comments/0")'>根索</span>其名而籍奏之，然后给传续食达辇，会试以文，则蓄响埋照之流，不远而至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164373_comment'></div>书判者削其字限，各罄其才而为之，文识高劣，尽可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164373_comment'></div>武举者去骑射之末，而访以机略之大，则将帅之具鳞集矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164373_comment'></div>若然，则陛下之诏不虚下，天下之人无异议，四条明而十一科正矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164373_comment'></div>臣碌碌者，岂当辄述国家大事，上干天子听览，盖以陛下开言路，塞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/150/Comments/0")'>讳门</span>，采瞽说，纳愚虑，是以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1164373", 1164373, "Clauses/153/Comments/0")'>析肝沥悃</span>而具述之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164373_comment'></div>若陛下责其犯上，罪其错议，臣虽膏钺转壑，不为之怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164373_comment'></div>伏愿俯而察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164373_comment'></div>干冒宸严，无任陨越。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1164373'></div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1164373_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1164373'><span class='label'>题下原注：</span>「时年二十二」，年代据此补。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1164373_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　诣登闻鼓院上疏进谏。作品：火疏。<div id='poem_1164369' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164369' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164369?labeling=true' target='_blank'>火疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（天圣七年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1029年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164369")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164369_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164369'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164369'>某年月日，草茅臣冒死谨拜疏于皇帝阙下：臣闻烈士不避鈇钺而进谏，明君不讳过失而纳忠，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>是以</span>怀策者必吐上前，蓄冤者无至腹诽，则上下之情不郁，政令之出悦随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164369_comment'></div>然言之之难，不如容之之难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164369_comment'></div>容之之难，不如行之之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164369_comment'></div>有能言之，则必容之，则必行之，如此，则欲治之主，三代之迹也，愿陛下留意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164369_comment'></div>臣伏睹今岁自春徂夏，霖雨阴晦，未尝少止，农田受台者几于十九，民情<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>嗷骚</span>，如昏垫焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164369_comment'></div>臣以谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>近位</span>之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/25/Comments/1")'>失人</span>，政令之多缺，赏罚弗公之所致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164369_comment'></div>天之降灾，欲悟陛下，陛下反谓刑狱滥冤之至，故肆赦天下以救之，殊不念如此则杀人者不死，伤人者不抵罪，其为滥冤，则又加甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164369_comment'></div>古者决狱断<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>滞讼</span>，以平水旱，不用赦也，故赦下之后，阴霾及今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164369_comment'></div>前志曰：「积冤生阴，积阴生阳，阳生则火灾见焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164369_comment'></div>乘夏之气，发泄于玉清宫，震雨杂下，烈燄四起，楼观万叠，数刻而尽，诚非慢于御备，乃上天之深戒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164369_comment'></div>陛下当降服减膳，避正寝，责躬罪己，下哀痛之诏，罢非业之作，拯失职之民，在辅弼无裨国体者去之，居左右窃弄威权者去之，精心念政刑之失，虚怀收刍荛之言，庶几变灾以答天意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164369_comment'></div>浃辰之间，不闻有此告谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164369_comment'></div>窃知陛下将计工役，再谋兴脩，都下之人，闻者骇惑，往往聚首横议，咸谓非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164369_comment'></div>皆曰章圣帝勤俭十馀年，天下富庶，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>帑府</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/74/Comments/1")'>流衍</span>，无所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>贮藏</span>，乃作斯宫，及其毕功，而海内为之虚竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164369_comment'></div>陛下即位，未及十年，数岁连遭水涝，虽征赋咸入，而百姓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>颇甚</span>困乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164369_comment'></div>若大兴土木之功，则费用不知纪极，财货耗于内，征役劳于下，内耗下劳，何以济矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164369_comment'></div>况天灾之，己为之，是欲竞天，无省己之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164369_comment'></div>逆天不祥，安己难任，欲祈厚贶，其可得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164369_comment'></div>岂天谴告而陛下弗悟邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164369_comment'></div>岂知而故为之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164369_comment'></div>岂再造祈天之祐邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164369_comment'></div>臣不得反覆而量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164369_comment'></div>今为陛下计者，莫若采吉士，去佞人，姑务脩德，以勤至治，使百姓足给，而宽其征税，则可以谢天意而安民情矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164369_comment'></div>夫贤君见变，能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/111/Comments/0")'>脩道</span>以除凶，乱世无象，天不谴告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164369_comment'></div>今幸得天见之变，是陛下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>脩道</span>之日，岂宜忽哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164369_comment'></div>昔汉元帝三年，茂陵白鹤馆灾，下诏曰：「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/120/Comments/1")'>乃者</span>火灾，降于孝武园馆，朕战慄恐惧，不烛变异，咎在朕躬，群有司又未肯极言朕过，以至于斯，将何寤焉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164369_comment'></div>夫茂陵不及上都也，白鹤馆不大此宫也，彼尚降诏四方，以求己过，是知古帝王急治如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164369_comment'></div>夫火不炎上之罚，正为是焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164369_comment'></div>臣谨按前汉《五行志》云：「贤佞分别，官人有序，帅繇旧章，敬重功勋，如此则火得其性矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164369_comment'></div>若乃信道不笃，或耀虚伪，谗夫昌，邪胜正，则火失其性矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164369_comment'></div>自上而降，及滥炎妄起，灾宗庙，烧宫室，虽兴师众，弗能救也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164369_comment'></div>故鲁成公三年新宫灾，刘向谓成公信三桓子孙之谗，逐父臣之应；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164369_comment'></div>襄公九年春，宋灾，刘向谓宋公听谗，逐其大夫华弱奔鲁之应也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164369_comment'></div>今宫灾，岂得亦有是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164369_comment'></div>愿陛下恭默而内省之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164369_comment'></div>省而既知之，愿陛下悔过而追革之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164369_comment'></div>罢再造之劳役，行古先之典法，非惟大光<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1164369", 1164369, "Clauses/166/Comments/0")'>基构</span>，亦天下之幸甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164369_comment'></div>臣愚妄之言，不足益国体之万一，陛下茍容而行之，三代两汉之风，指顾而可致也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1164369_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年5月</a>　入京献疏。作品：论五事。<div id='poem_1164374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164374?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论五事疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（景祐四年五月七日閤门下）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164374")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164374_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164374'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164374'>臣闻重闭尚设于勇夫，击柝以待乎暴民，是皆前籍立戒，以监后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164374_comment'></div>故国门九阖，梐枑百重，刑人以守阍，下士以拂闑，所以深严帝禁，以备非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164374_comment'></div>古者非有符节，不得辄入君门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164374_comment'></div>降及后来，乃设<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>籍禁</span>，品庶官之高下，限诸门之出入，故东籍而西入者，律令有文焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164374_comment'></div>臣窃见国朝皇城宫门，皆无名籍，往来无间，甚非防微之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164374_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后内城诸门，应分番宿直，诸色人等，各立名籍，仍差中官专切<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>提辖</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164374_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1164374'>一、臣闻事不师古，傅说所讥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164374_comment'></div>必也正名，仲尼之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164374_comment'></div>臣窃以国寺之监，乃卿佐之局；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164374_comment'></div>南省诸曹，皆尚书之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164374_comment'></div>近朝多差京朝官或员外专判，于理不顺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164374_comment'></div>且远方一州一郡，唯使相及仆射以上，方得言判，岂京朝小官，得判省寺重地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164374_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后非有本官者，但称权及句当，不令专判，庶合前规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164374_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1164374'>一、臣谨按前志曰：「白事之吏，民之仇雠」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164374_comment'></div>又云：「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/50/Comments/1")'>急吏缓民</span>，则吏不可纵，政之大功也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164374_comment'></div>臣窃见州县之吏，多是狡恶之人，窥伺官寮，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>探刺</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/56/Comments/1")'>旨意</span>，清白者必多方以误之，贪婪者则啖利以制之，然后<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>析律舞文</span>，鬻狱市令，上下其手，轻重厥刑，变诈奇邪，无所不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164374_comment'></div>茍或败露，立便逃亡，稍候事平，复出行案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164374_comment'></div>设有强明<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>牧宰</span>，督察太严，则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>缔连</span>诸曹，同日亡命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164374_comment'></div>或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>狱讼</span>未具，遂停<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>鞫劾</span>，赋税起纳，无人催驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164374_comment'></div>近年以来，习成此弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164374_comment'></div>官长务从姑息，恐失大计，见其邪滥，不敢以法绳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164374_comment'></div>惟此辈凶人，唯利是嗜，每纠以严宪，尚不悛心，何况纵之使乱正法，实政理之巨蠹，黎民之大害焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164374_comment'></div>人虽切齿，无可柰何，盖缘国家别无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>敕条</span>，以加检束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164374_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后州县曹司有阙，并于第二人户上选差，仍令每五人互相为保，或逃亡者，立差官籍其家，量取以充赏，募人收捉，或遇赦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>首身</span>，亦乞流配别郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164374_comment'></div>如此，则不敢公然作过，以紊正经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164374_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1164374'>一、臣闻矜孤养老，邦家之大政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164374_comment'></div>恤贫宽疾，册书之格言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164374_comment'></div>窃见前代皆置悲田养病坊，唐至在长安中，命使专领，亦选名德僧徒，兼掌其事，县官出钱收利，籍而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164374_comment'></div>开元中，丞相宋璟上言乞罢，中旨不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164374_comment'></div>会昌沙汰僧尼，李德裕以悲田院出于释氏，遂易名而增脩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164374_comment'></div>国家富有四海，生齿实繁，山泽之间，举无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>遗利</span>，赋税之外，复有远仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164374_comment'></div>或水旱为灾，则流亡相属，遇慈惠之吏，必率敛而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/132/Comments/0")'>饲养</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164374_comment'></div>逢茍且之政，必枕籍而死亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164374_comment'></div>本非堕慵，多致歉乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164374_comment'></div>又京兆之内，丐乞者多，饥寒所侵，往往残废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164374_comment'></div>或自折支体，困入泥涂，号呼里闾，呻吟道路，聚为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/145/Comments/0")'>祲厉</span>，甚伤风化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164374_comment'></div>陛下仁被草木，惠及昆虫，惟此夭伤，未沾王泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164374_comment'></div>臣欲乞依有唐故事，创置悲田养病坊，州郡并以曹官领之，仍于高年择信行可称者三两人，与僧官同切管句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164374_comment'></div>三京给田十顷，望镇州七顷，诸州军等第给田，以充粥食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164374_comment'></div>有羡馀官钱，置本收利，以备医药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164374_comment'></div>十岁以下，八十以上，仰州县察访，无家可归者，亦令看养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164374_comment'></div>如此，则大益仁化，无亏国风，颂声喧传，上资圣算，和气浃洽，可召丰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164374_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1164374'>一、臣闻巨壑虽深，兽知所避；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164374_comment'></div>烈火至猛，人无蹈死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164374_comment'></div>故历块而蹶者皆是，玩水而溺者有之，古垂此言，以喻刑辟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164374_comment'></div>昔圣人恶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1164374", 1164374, "Clauses/183/Comments/0")'>残贼</span>之害良民也，故明设严刑，大张宪网，必使易避而难犯，防微而杜原，约之不至烦苛，威之以令畏惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164374_comment'></div>奸凶之辈，翻然革心，固而行之，自然刑省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164374_comment'></div>茍务矜贷，则冒禁者繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164374_comment'></div>窃见官吏多犯赃污，乃由朝廷法制稍宽，贪鄙因缘为弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164374_comment'></div>凡中人之性，本非大凶，皆以禁约不严，是为货利所没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164374_comment'></div>手提刑宪，人不敢言，心恣诛求，下受其困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164374_comment'></div>夫杀人者死，伤人者刑，古今之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164374_comment'></div>杀伤之害，不过数人，今贪人在官，民皆受苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164374_comment'></div>虽有转运提刑，位皆尊崇，罕与民接，询访官吏，鲜得实情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164374_comment'></div>茍无讼端，莫肯发摘，知者或欲陈告，又非干己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164374_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后官典犯入己赃，许诸色人陈论，得实者以其赃充赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164374_comment'></div>如此，则必畏多言之人，亦防十目之视，荀卿所谓「威厉而不试，刑严而不用」，此其得之矣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164374_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1164374'>沈校本校云：「『臣』上疑有『一』字」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1164374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1164374'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_56_1164374_0'>⑴ 《苏学士文集》卷一二。又见《历代名臣奏议》卷一○五、一六五、一九六、二一○，乾隆《中江县志》卷七，同治《绵州志》卷四九。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1164374_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　有诗送家静。作品：送家静及第后赴官清水。<div id='poem_495736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495736?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送家静及第后赴官清水</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495736")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495736_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495736'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495736'>几年尘土客京华，一日春乘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_495736", 495736, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>犯斗槎</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495736'>梦好夜归全蜀道，眼明朝宴上林花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495736'>白头佐邑非为晚，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495736", 495736, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>蓝绶</span>还乡亦可誇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495736'>况有雄图看悟主，莫伤孤宦向天涯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495736'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495736_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　有信上杜衍。作品：上京兆杜公书。<div id='poem_1164386' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164386' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164386?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上京兆公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164386")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164386_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164386'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164386'>某才到阙下数日，闻河东地震，坏庐舍，杀人马畜，不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164386_comment'></div>始闻惊骇不自定，徐念台谏官必有极言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164386", 1164386, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>时病</span>，以救天变者，既而踰旬无闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164386_comment'></div>又以谓河东守土臣必有上陈消杀之策，使朝廷省悟，而有所废置者，及是经月，又无闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164386_comment'></div>某虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164386", 1164386, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>迷暗</span>于事，不通古今，窃谓天地灾异莫大于此，灾异之作，未尝妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164386_comment'></div>今中外循嘿，不以为怪，使陛下忽天戒而不答，民畜横罹其凶，食肉者岂不畏惧而能忍也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164386_comment'></div>时虽可欺之，天孰得而欺之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164386_comment'></div>呜呼，其奈何邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164386_comment'></div>丈人以才业为上所知，自员外郎不六七年擢任至此，天下所共闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164386_comment'></div>虽所历必尽精力，夙夜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164386", 1164386, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>孜孜不懈</span>，然未有赫赫报国之迹，为天下所共闻而称道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164386_comment'></div>今所属有此灾异，故当忧思本朝，建言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164386", 1164386, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>时病</span>以箴之，不可怀忠不发，默默缄口，如常常者所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164386_comment'></div>盖今为上所知、天下所想望号端直者，惟丈人与孔谏议、范吏部耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164386_comment'></div>孔、范皆以言得罪，惟丈人昔在廷中，议论必行，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164386", 1164386, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>擢拜</span>又过二公，度此不言，则他事无足言者，窃恐负陛下任擢之意，而隳天下之望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164386_comment'></div>君子之为，不畏时王之罚，而畏众人之议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164386_comment'></div>或众议喧哗，不可盖塞，则虽终日九迁，亦足羞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164386_comment'></div>茍有献纳，慎无后于他人，实区区之望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164386_comment'></div>至于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164386", 1164386, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>钤束</span>小吏，期会簿书，非大贤事业，幸委之幕府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164386_comment'></div>进谠言以求杀灾异，宜在今日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164386_comment'></div>况忠臣虽在畎亩，不忘其君，无以疏外为词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164386_comment'></div>谨驰此附闻，幸留意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164386_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1164386_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　诣匦上疏。作品：诣匦疏。<div id='poem_1164368' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164368' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164368?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诣匦疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164368")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164368_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164368'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164368'>正月十八日，具官臣某，谨顿首再拜，昧死上疏皇帝陛下：臣昨初到京师，闻河东地大震裂，涌水坏屋庐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>城堞</span>，杀民畜几十万，历旬不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164368_comment'></div>臣始闻惶骇疑惑，窃思自编策所纪，前代衰微丧乱之世，亦未尝有此大变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164368_comment'></div>方今四圣接统，内外平宁，戎狄交欢，兵革偃息，固与夫衰微丧乱之际颇异，是何灾变之作返过之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164368_comment'></div>且妖祥之兴，神实尸之，各以类告，未尝妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164368_comment'></div>臣以为必无是事，是亦传言之滥耳，历问一二朝士，皆曰有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164368_comment'></div>因退思念，天人之应，古今之鉴，大可恐惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164368_comment'></div>凡朝廷政教<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>昏迷</span>，下受其弊，积阴郁不和之气，上动于天，天于是为下变异以警戒之，使君人者回心<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>省修</span>，翻然向道，则民安而灾息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164368_comment'></div>是故古之王者，逢天地之变，则必避正寝，彻乐省馔，询访正议，考求失德而更去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164368_comment'></div>盖以上帝聪明，所作必验，茍弗知惧，则非常之孽随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164368_comment'></div>今此异既告，岂徒然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164368_comment'></div>则王者岂常安于逸豫，信任近狎而不省政事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164368_comment'></div>庙堂之上执事者，岂有非贤才，或专威福而侵君者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164368_comment'></div>其所施设之政，岂有不便于民者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164368_comment'></div>深宫之中，岂有阴教不谨，或以媚道滥进者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164368_comment'></div>西北之夷，岂有窃萌背盟、犯顺之心者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164368_comment'></div>念自从远方来，不知近事，心虽疑而口不敢道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164368_comment'></div>宫禁夷狄之事，固未可知，朝廷已然之失，则听<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>舆论</span>而有闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164368_comment'></div>又讶朝廷知此大异，殊不脩补阙政，以厌天戒而安民心，默然不怪，如平常无事时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164368_comment'></div>谏官、御史亦不闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/75/Comments/1")'>进牍</span>白见，铺陈灾害之端，以开上心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164368_comment'></div>然民情汹汹，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>聚首</span>横议，咸有忧悸之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164368_comment'></div>岂时与古不同，今朝不宜仿古以为事耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164368_comment'></div>又念有天下者，未有不监古而治、弃古而乱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164368_comment'></div>岂上位者务在镇静，不须与民同忧耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164368_comment'></div>则又民为邦本，未有本摇而枝叶不动者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164368_comment'></div>岂民愚暗，不当忧而忧耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164368_comment'></div>则地之震，天之所为也，民虽愚，天岂愚哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164368_comment'></div>反覆思之，不觉惊怛流汗，自以世受君禄，身齿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>国命</span>，涵濡惠泽，以长此躯，便欲尽吐肝胆，以拜封奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164368_comment'></div>又昨见范仲淹以刚直忤奸臣，果罹中伤，言不用而身<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/105/Comments/0")'>窜谪</span>，甚可悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164368_comment'></div>是时降诏天下，不许越职言事，臣今茍务激切，不避权右，必恐横遭伤害，无补于时，因自悲嗟，不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164368_comment'></div>既而孟春之初，雷电暴作，臣以谓国家之失，众臣无有为陛下言者，唯天丁宁以告陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164368_comment'></div>陛下极圣至明，其肯忽之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164368_comment'></div>果能霈发明诏，许臣寮皆得献言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164368_comment'></div>臣初闻之，踊跃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/125/Comments/0")'>欣抃</span>，又谓虽有灾异，陛下能讲求嘉言，革去时弊，故可变化而召善和也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164368_comment'></div>旬馀日来，闻颇有言事者，其间岂无切中时病，而绝不闻朝廷从而行之，是亦收虚言而不根实效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164368_comment'></div>臣闻唯诚可以应上天，惟实可以安下民，今应天不以诚，安民不以实，徒布空文，增人太息耳，将何以谢神灵而救弊乱也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164368_comment'></div>岂大臣蒙塞天聪，不为陛下行之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164368_comment'></div>岂言事者迂阔无所取，不足行也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164368_comment'></div>此则未可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164368_comment'></div>今臣窃见纲纪隳败，政化阙失，其事甚众，不可概举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164368_comment'></div>今条大者二，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>诣匦</span>以闻，伏望陛下少赐观览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164368_comment'></div>茍有所采，乞断自睿意，即时行焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164368_comment'></div>言或狂瞽，乞付臣斧锧，以非所宜言罪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164368_comment'></div>一曰正心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164368_comment'></div>夫治国如治家，治家者先修于己，修己者先正于心，心正则神明集而万务理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164368_comment'></div>今则民间喧传，陛下数年以来，多引俳优贱人于深宫之中，燕乐无节，赐予过度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164368_comment'></div>燕乐无节则志荒荡，赐予过度则心<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/171/Comments/0")'>侈泰</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164368_comment'></div>志荒荡则政事不亲，心<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/173/Comments/0")'>侈泰</span>则用度不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164368_comment'></div>臣窃观国史，见祖宗逐日视朝，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/176/Comments/0")'>旰昃</span>方罢，犹坐于后苑门上，有白事者，立得召对，委曲询访，小善必纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164368_comment'></div>真宗末年不豫，始间日视事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164368_comment'></div>今陛下春秋鼎盛，实宵衣旰食求治之秋，而乃隔日御殿，此政事不亲之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164368_comment'></div>今又府库匮竭，民鲜盖藏，诛敛科率，殆无虚日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164368_comment'></div>三司计度经费，二十倍于祖宗时，此用度不足明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164368_comment'></div>政事不亲而用度不足，斯大可忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164368_comment'></div>伏望陛下脩己以御人，洗心而鉴物，勤于听断，舍其燕安，放弃优谐近习之纤人，亲近刚明鲠直之良士，因此灾变，以思永图，效祖宗之勤劳，惜社稷之广大，则天下之幸甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164368_comment'></div>二曰择贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164368_comment'></div>夫明主劳于求贤而逸于任使，然盈庭之士，不须尽择，在择一二辅臣及御史、谏官而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164368_comment'></div>今陛下用人，似不能择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164368_comment'></div>昨王随自吏部侍郎迁门下侍郎、平章事，超越十资，复为上相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1164368_comment'></div>此乃非常之恩，必待非常之才，而王随虚庸邪谄，非辅相之器，降麻之后，物论<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/223/Comments/0")'>沸腾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1164368_comment'></div>故疾缠其身，灾仍于国，此亦天意爱惜我朝，陛下必鉴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1164368_comment'></div>又石中立顷在朝行，以诙谐自任，士人或有宴集，必置席间，听其语言，以资笑噱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1164368_comment'></div>今处之近辅，不闻嘉谟，物望甚轻，人情所忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1164368_comment'></div>使灾害屡降，而朝廷不尊，盖近臣多非才者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1164368_comment'></div>陛下左右尚如此，天下官吏可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1164368_comment'></div>实恐匈奴轻笑中国，伏望即时罢免，别选贤才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1164368_comment'></div>臣又窃见方今以张观为御史中丞，高若讷为司谏，此二人者，皆登高第，本望以词华进用，素履温和<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1164368", 1164368, "Clauses/251/Comments/0")'>软懦</span>，无刚鲠敢言之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1164368_comment'></div>斯皆执政引拔建置，欲其慎默，不敢举扬其私，时有所言，必暗相关说，旁人窥之，甚可笑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1164368_comment'></div>故御史、谏官之任，臣欲陛下亲择之，不令出执政门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1164368_comment'></div>台谏官既得其人，则近臣不敢为过，乃驭下之策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1164368_comment'></div>臣以谓陛下身既勤俭，辅弼、台谏又皆得人，则天下何忧不治，而灾异何自而生？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1164368_comment'></div>伏望陛下少留意焉，非有难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1164368_comment'></div>臣不胜区区之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1164368_comment'></div>某顿首再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_72_1164368_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='571228441d1945b3a7970457dab3ec0c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("571228441d1945b3a7970457dab3ec0c");'><span id='571228441d1945b3a7970457dab3ec0c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1041')">1040-1041年</a>，33-34岁</div><div id='571228441d1945b3a7970457dab3ec0c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　代杜衍作求罢表。作品：京兆求罢表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年初。）</span><div id='poem_1164375' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164375' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164375?labeling=true' target='_blank'>京兆求罢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164375")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164375_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164375'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164375'>臣某言：臣闻佐机命者以吁谟为先，制<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164375", 1164375, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>兵钤</span>者以多算为胜，盖安危之所系，当议论之必精，苟异于斯，故难全度<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164375_comment'></div>昨者丑虏不庭，斋坛命帅，不能专阃外之事，而乃求幄中之谟，遣吏入朝，列章来上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164375_comment'></div>臣本以孤直，误叨奖知，久留滞于外藩，忽引拔于近列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164375_comment'></div>凡有所见，未尝不言，虽数被于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164375", 1164375, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>沮伤</span>，岂敢思于欺默，报陛下非常之遇，罄下臣无隐之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164375_comment'></div>比者，将以重兵深入贼境，众谓当尔，臣为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164375_comment'></div>既<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164375", 1164375, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>练阅</span>未精，又饷馈不足，士不习山川之险阻，将不知巢穴之浅深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164375_comment'></div>臣两在关中，备见形势，既虞调发，先摇民心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164375_comment'></div>复虑覆军，愈增敌气，向去边鄙卒难支持，是以悉心为图，沥恳上白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164375_comment'></div>虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164375", 1164375, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>渊衷</span>广纳，未欲加罪于瞽言，而卑论弗臧，安可尚居于厚位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164375_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下察其朴拙，曲为哀矜，俾出守于小邦，或投置于散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164375_comment'></div>进退有礼，在国体以诚宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164375_comment'></div>言行无欺，于臣心而自足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164375_comment'></div>叫阍斯切，得请是期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164375_comment'></div>臣无任祈天待命、激切震惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1164375_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　为刘平、石元子弟上书。作品：乞用刘石子弟。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于处斩黄德和之后、刘、石尚未获得恤典之前。）</span><div id='poem_1164372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164372?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞用刘石子弟疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164372")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164372_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164372'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164372'>臣近到阙，闻黄德和以退军及妄奏刘平、石元孙叛逆，朝廷已从军法<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164372", 1164372, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>处分</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164372_comment'></div>然刘平、石元孙以血战<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164372", 1164372, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>陷没</span>，死于贼手，初朝廷未能辨明，即时以兵卒监围其第，及德和既已伏辜，二族未沾恩泽，迁延累日，人颇疑惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164372_comment'></div>古者舍爵策勋，贵其速也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164372_comment'></div>此虽败衄，是亦勤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164372_comment'></div>于是伏望陛下断自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164372", 1164372, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>睿意</span>，诏有司于西郊备礼致祭，陛下出次素服，西向举哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164372_comment'></div>故《礼》云：「军有忧，则素服哭于库门之外，赴军不载櫜韔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164372_comment'></div>盖古者义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164372_comment'></div>即日降册追赠赙其家族，爵其子弟，使死者有知，岂无冥助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164372_comment'></div>生者怀感，必当尽忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164372_comment'></div>烈士<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164372", 1164372, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>义夫</span>，闻之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164372", 1164372, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>震激</span>，人人思为陛下用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164372_comment'></div>刘平子弟，臣虽不识，闻其颇知边事，用敌西寇，必有成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164372_comment'></div>况国耻家雠，异于他将，则吴用子胥，唐拜田布，即其义也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164372_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1164372'>年月原无，据《国朝诸臣奏议》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1164372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1164372'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_1164372_0'>⑴ 《苏学士文集》卷一一。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷九五，乾隆《中江县志》卷七，同治《绵州志》卷四九。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1164372_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　有信上范仲淹。作品：上范希文书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年八月之后。）</span><div id='poem_1164384' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164384' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164384?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上范希文书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164384")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164384_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164384'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164384'>某观古之烈士，受人一言一顾之重，不计己之能否、事之重轻，殒命捐躯，无向而不入，或促其祸败，累于所知者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164384_comment'></div>然史氏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>稗说</span>，皆辍之以称述其事，而警厉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>偷浅</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164384_comment'></div>某窃谓其勇敢敦气节则有馀，至于成就大计，趣道与权，则不足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164384_comment'></div>故某自少小迨于作官，所为不敢妄，必审处己之才能而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>傅会</span>于道，人虽不知，自信甚笃且久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164384_comment'></div>昨者，朝廷以阁下才谋绝世，负天下之重望，倚之以究西事，故阁下开置幕府，收策志虑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>英荦</span>之士以自广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164384_comment'></div>盖以兵者重器，资群材以共举，一失其任，则折衄报之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164384_comment'></div>而阁下误有听采，将引<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>猥琐</span>置于左右，委言垂意，发于颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164384_comment'></div>某非不知依阁下之重，可以取光价而自振起，设临几事不能有所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>建弼</span>，耻也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164384_comment'></div>有所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>建弼</span>而不合于义，不行焉，亦耻也，况于轻挠哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164384_comment'></div>及是，则不惟亏损阁下之望，某终身可废，无所容焉，是以上犯盛意，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>恳激</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/46/Comments/1")'>避辞</span>者，盖在此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164384_comment'></div>然某虽至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>冥愚</span>，内荷阁下之顾，夙夕感慨，思有所报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164384_comment'></div>昨闻阁下以张存不才，自求守延州，物论喧然，以阁下领经略之权，自可往来陕右，进退在己，延州逼近贼锋，而能舍安逸以就<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>危隘</span>，虽古人不逮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164384_comment'></div>又或云阁下居长安，统二于人，不能明白立功名，将高举远去以自异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164384_comment'></div>此二涂未必中阁下之度，以某观之，既白张存，则不得不自请，但裁授之际，有所未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164384_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164384_comment'></div>以阁下为经略，则自陕西以至于边徼，斥候皆可处置；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164384_comment'></div>在延则局守于一州，于他郡不接矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164384_comment'></div>他郡不接或可，不能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>仰制</span>关中事，则可虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164384_comment'></div>盖关中之俗，大抵彊悍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>豪忍</span>，又形势险固，出于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164384_comment'></div>今方尽取乡民，籍之为兵，得操弓兵以自肄习，往来道路，与寇贼不辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164384_comment'></div>小人少思虑，加之气俗，又得此利器，幸而岁常丰，父兄家老<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>聚居</span>可约束，不幸少歉，父兄不能保有其子弟，必将人人依险以自快，则其将柰何邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164384_comment'></div>况朝廷前有意令其自卫，不率以战，今<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/100/Comments/0")'>条约</span>烦细，又迫驱之以向敌，人颇失望，有天下而失人以信，后将何所恃焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164384_comment'></div>昨者延安、镇戎杀害民畜，不可胜纪，死气结戾不判，必能变乱阴阳之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164384_comment'></div>今虽少稔，恐来年宿麦不登，民必<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/111/Comments/0")'>狼顾</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164384_comment'></div>弱者流转，彊者化而为贪贼，则心腹自有疾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164384_comment'></div>阁下居延州，虽能制昊贼之命，系虏其种族，逐之绝漠而遁，亦何救关中之事邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164384_comment'></div>故某谓西羌不足忧于关中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164384_comment'></div>近日窃闻邻郡数胜，颇得马畜，屠其栅垒，火其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/124/Comments/0")'>聚积</span>，朝廷即时越次以赏其劳，使人得自有其所得，军声稍振，士百其勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164384_comment'></div>以某观之，古之善御戎者，岂特是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164384_comment'></div>盖务<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/132/Comments/0")'>训抚</span>吾民，使安其业，不以非义动，扼其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>冲塞</span>，绝其互市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164384_comment'></div>闭之沙漠之外，俟其隙且困则破散之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164384_comment'></div>晨钞夕盗，与竞寸尺之地，非大国之体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164384_comment'></div>某反虑将佐不知此事，锐而少思，狃毫发之胜，中其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/145/Comments/0")'>诡谲</span>而所丧必大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164384_comment'></div>盖兵家之法，必以饵骄人而后取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164384_comment'></div>况羌虏常以伏奇包众胜中国，当此之际，阁下能部勒诸将，分乘险阻，不使习小利以为功，持重其体而死其奸谋，不惮旷日而使之内溃，此孙武所谓善之善者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164384_comment'></div>况夫体<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/156/Comments/0")'>幽静</span>则谋精而威，气张锐则令烦而堕，阁下立谋而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/158/Comments/0")'>首令</span>者也，以身系安危，可不慎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164384_comment'></div>若能去延州之狭以自任，抚关中之人以示信，而又<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/163/Comments/0")'>沈远</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/163/Comments/1")'>变动</span>，则何敌之敢先哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164384_comment'></div>悬料古人所难，况某浅识，而欲上赞远略？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164384_comment'></div>然区区之诚，腷臆于内，万觊一得，以补高明，抚断之馀，特赐省阅，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164384_comment'></div>穷边寒苦，乞加<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/176/Comments/0")'>护练</span>，不任<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1164384", 1164384, "Clauses/177/Comments/0")'>恳激</span>之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1164384_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年11月21日</a>　对圣旨宣谕借宅之事提出意见。作品：论宣借宅事。<div id='poem_1164371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164371?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论宣借宅事疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年十一月二十一日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164371")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164371'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164371'>臣昨于十月二十三日内侍省牒奉圣旨下务，支借小宅一所与司天监杨可久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164371_comment'></div>今月十八日准三司牒传宣旨，指射舍屋三十间已来，与医官副使柳尧卿居止者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164371_comment'></div>窃以赐第之典，于国体至重，前朝将相，非有勋业，则不得赐第京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164371_comment'></div>近刘平血战亡躯，家族无托，朝廷方推此惠，时谓当然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164371_comment'></div>今兹医卜庸流，滥有求请，烦渎天听，侵乱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164371", 1164371, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>邦经</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164371_comment'></div>况赏罚二端，国之名器，所以驱驾豪杰，示信四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164371_comment'></div>若死行陈之家与伎术之辈均用此赏，臣窃恐轻重失宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164371_comment'></div>方今西鄙未宁，暴师塞外，流传四出，何以劝人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164371_comment'></div>伏望特降德音，即时寝罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164371_comment'></div>况柳尧卿自有居第，极为华侈，若以其医药有效，自可以金帛赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164371_comment'></div>上以重恩赏之科，使战伐者尽其死力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164371_comment'></div>下以绝侥觊之望，俾贪冒者萌其耻心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164371_comment'></div>臣事在职司，合有献纳，盖期赏之不僭，非敢文而自营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164371_comment'></div>上渎宸严，无任<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164371", 1164371, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>恳到</span>之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1164371_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　荐王景仁。作品：荐王景仁启。<div id='poem_1164407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荐王景仁启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164407")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164407'>某启：某资虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164407", 1164407, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>颛庸</span>，心辄喜善，敢缘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164407", 1164407, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>世契</span>，上布公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164407_comment'></div>某昨任长垣县，有尉王景仁者，性质惇淳，所向通彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164407_comment'></div>徇公之外，好学不倦，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164407", 1164407, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>才行</span>卓越，可以制事厉俗，其文词有唐梁肃、独孤及之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164407_comment'></div>雅尚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164407", 1164407, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>退默</span>，不高人以声，故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164407", 1164407, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>沈顿</span>贱仕，未为位上者所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164407", 1164407, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>引拔</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164407_comment'></div>阁下服天子之命，专<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164407", 1164407, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>按举</span>之职，寰内之吏，贤不肖得以进退之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164407_comment'></div>敢以斯人置于门下，幸赐荐籍，以为光宠，足使列邑闻之，竦然知劝，亦阁下之所乐行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164407_comment'></div>风威所临，洞鉴不隔，安敢自任愚瞽，上欺高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164407_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164407", 1164407, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>真悫</span>之诚，幸冀采察，不任激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1164407_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　论述对西夏作战的意见。作品：论西事状。<div id='poem_1164370' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164370' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164370?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论西事状</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164370")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164370_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164370'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164370'>臣窃见自西寇逆节，天下言兵者不可胜计，大抵不过训练兵卒、积聚刍粟而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164370_comment'></div>其言泛杂，无所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164370", 1164370, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>操总</span>，又<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164370", 1164370, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>陈烂</span>使人耳厌其闻而笑忽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164370_comment'></div>况清衷近辅，自有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164370", 1164370, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>上算</span>，故不当复有所献也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164370_comment'></div>然臣早居长安，备见西边事体，其要在乎得人，得人则练兵积粟之多，不烦帷幄之议而自集也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164370_comment'></div>惟攻守之策，必须中授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164370_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164370_comment'></div>此事至大，不可轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164370_comment'></div>近闻朝廷将议深讨，覆其巢穴，此盖愤其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164370", 1164370, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>凶悖</span>，勇而不知思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164370_comment'></div>孰不知羌氐之俗，居不常处，兽聚鸟散，本无聚积，若垂军绝漠，则跨历险涂，被甲裹粮，操执兵械，外疲而内惧，一日之行有三日之劳，曾未见敌，先已自病，隘而遇伏，则将不支矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164370_comment'></div>昔赵充国之论兵，详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164370_comment'></div>故中国利守，夷狄利战，从古然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164370_comment'></div>《传》曰：「天子守在四夷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164370_comment'></div>又曰：「荒服者王，不王则脩德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164370_comment'></div>《诗》云：「薄伐猃狁，至于太原」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164370_comment'></div>薄伐，亦谓逐出之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164370_comment'></div>来则逐之，去而勿追，御戎之善策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164370_comment'></div>国朝五路兴师，亦遇败衄，前日刘平不能持重俟隙，务于速战，身罹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164370", 1164370, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>禽获</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164370", 1164370, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>伤剥</span>国威，是知讨之不如守之之利也明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164370_comment'></div>近者，朝廷拜置夏竦、韩琦、范仲淹等，此皆平定外夷，人所属望者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164370_comment'></div>贼昊奸谲，故必<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164370", 1164370, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>疑畏</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164370", 1164370, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>疑畏</span>则将以事验之，以臣窃料，今秋必放兵犯塞，以观我师之方略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164370_comment'></div>当是之时，尤须慎重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164370_comment'></div>若能坚壁清野，勿与之敌，设伏用奇于险塞之地，待其师老粮尽而反覆击之，不劳深讨而可成功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164370_comment'></div>方今之势，不患其来战，患守之之道未至耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164370_comment'></div>议其功者，恐锐而寡谋，败陛下军事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164370_comment'></div>愚者之说，万或一效，以尝预西事，不敢塞默，伏惟圣虑裁察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164370_comment'></div>不胜恳恳之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1164370_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　有状。作品：乞发兵用银牌状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年前后。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　有诗送高怿。作品：送安素处士高文悦。<div id='poem_495672' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495672' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495672?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送安素处士高文悦</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_495672_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495672'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495672'>皇天稔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_495672", 495672, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>巨憝</span>，羌虏稽显戮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495672'>庙算忽小丑，王师数<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495672", 495672, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>倾衄</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495672'>秦民著暴敛，惨惨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495672", 495672, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>生意</span>蹙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495672'>贼气愈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495672", 495672, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>张王</span>，锋锐不可触。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495672'>帷幄监前败，降心问白屋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495672'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_495672", 495672, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>尺诏</span>下中天，公车塞章牍。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495672'>策虑尽颇牧，勇决过贲育。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495672'>先生胸臆大，经术内自足。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495672'>逸韵脱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_495672", 495672, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>滓尘</span>，素节抱冰玉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495672'>独耻论兵战，因时射君禄。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495672'>不唯吾志乖，亦使王道局。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495672'>放怀但文史，散发自溪谷。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495672'>近臣上荐书，天子渴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_495672", 495672, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>高躅</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495672'>旌<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>帛三及门，不免至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_495672", 495672, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>京毂</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495672'>万钟非所好，大议戛钧轴。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495672'>孤鸾入紫烟，网罟安可束。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495672'>天风万里长，沆瀣朝满腹。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495672'>更期下翔集，以为苍生福。<div id='poem_note_495672'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_13_495672_0'>⑴ 原作束、据黄本、陈本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495672_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　代人为吕夷简作寿诗。作品：代人上申公祝寿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年五月吕夷简这次入相之后。）</span><div id='poem_495741' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495741' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495741?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人上申公祝寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495741")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495741_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495741'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495741'>维神祚炎历，发蕴复<span class='inlineComment2'>（原缺，据李本补）</span>含灵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495741'>嶷尔为人瑞，居然出相庭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495741'>舜门登<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495741", 495741, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>夙望</span>，韦氏继先经。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495741'>积学方开隩，当官已发硎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495741'>纯诚贯白日，阔步上青冥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495741'>才力回元气，胸怀纳四溟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495741'>八荒归富寿，万象染丹青。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495741'>恳牍辞魁柄，开藩密帝扃。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495741'>碧旌油重润，苍佩玉明荧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495741'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_495741", 495741, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>舆望</span>知难转，王心几不宁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495741'>西羌动妖孽，秦塞困膻腥。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495741'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_495741", 495741, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>羽奏</span>飞关路，兜烽照浊泾。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495741'>裴公辞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_495741", 495741, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>激烈</span>，袁相涕飘零。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495741'>天为移<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_495741", 495741, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>文象</span>，人思奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_495741", 495741, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>典型</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495741'>欢谣塞归路，召节下宸廷。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495741'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_495741", 495741, "Clauses/30/Comments/1")'>胜算</span><sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>剧破竹，威声如走霆。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495741'>折冲千里定，指画众心醒。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495741'>大议虚怀纳，吁谟前席听。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495741'>玉关收旧地，庙鼎续新铭。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495741'>复耸岩岩石，增辉两两星。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495741'>川源流盛美，岳镇敌长龄。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495741'>有客惭才薄，区区咏德馨。<div id='poem_sentence_21_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_495741'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_495741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495741'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_495741_0'>⑴ 原作等，李本作筹，据黄本、陈本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495741_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　与兄舜元联句。作品：瓦亭联句。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　有信上叶清臣。作品：应制科上省使叶道卿书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年3月内。）</span><div id='poem_1164385' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164385' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164385?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应制科上省使叶道卿书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164385")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164385_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164385'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164385'>三月日，某谨斋祓百拜，献书于省使龙图阁下：某观前古之士，歘然奋起于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>贱庸</span>之地，建名树勋，风采表于当世者，未始不由<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>上官</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>钜公</span>推引而能至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164385_comment'></div>故儒其名者，必奔走贵势之门，以希光宠而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>取重</span>焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164385_comment'></div>然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>有位</span>之德望重轻，亦因收士多少而后定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164385_comment'></div>设国有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>缓急</span>，则审处变故，推择门下士以属任焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164385_comment'></div>或资其策虑以自广，小则补吏，大则同升于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164385_comment'></div>以故士皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>雕琢</span>节行，缘以文采，蔼蔼而进，至使敌国异方闻风畏之，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>厌杀</span>未形之患，此其所以为得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164385_comment'></div>然奔骛誇鬻，扇动流俗，茍窃虚名以自耀高位者，或私其所与，朋比自植，肆然揽爵赏之柄，此又所以为失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164385_comment'></div>本朝监其失，进退天下士，一决于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164385_comment'></div>考艺文则誊书糊名，衡文之学，靡以行实相雄长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164385_comment'></div>公卿亦阖无所顾接，盖蔽贤之罚不及焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164385_comment'></div>上下隔塞不交，忘经远之业，此又今之所以为失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164385_comment'></div>故近年贼羌暴逆节，庙堂图帅西攻，思所以折冲制胜者，惘然乏其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164385_comment'></div>以至诏书数下，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>猝猝</span>求索，而才者未甚出，凡近之器往往入充其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164385_comment'></div>盖朝廷取士之路本狭，在上者不以汲善为意，下士又以造谒为之耻，故骤阅而无得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164385_comment'></div>是古今得失相纠，惟贤者为能折其衷焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164385_comment'></div>某性本迂拙，不喜事人事，名虽在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>仕版</span>，而未尝数当涂之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164385_comment'></div>窃服于道二十年矣，前世之务，当今之宜，粗志其一二，然虽与周旋者，亦弗敢吐以自表见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164385_comment'></div>阁下以高文闳才都盛位，而某以吏属，时得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164385", 1164385, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>趋跄</span>左右，未始敢开词动气，及于局事之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164385_comment'></div>非唯轻肆是惧，亦且束于世教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164385_comment'></div>今幸天子下尺一书，详延四方特起之士，某辄欲以空乏鄙陋之资，冒然自进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164385_comment'></div>窃念科试甚重，朝廷虚伫，以须异人，无似妄作，虞为识者所不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164385_comment'></div>今幸人未暴闻，故敢以私习论五十篇上浼听览，非敢希企奖引之赐，但觊一言以断进退之惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164385_comment'></div>精识所向，洞照不隔，干渎威重，俯伏待教，不任惶恐激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1164385_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　有诗悼石延年。作品：哭曼卿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（石延年卒于庆历元年二月四日，此诗作于此后不久。）</span><div id='poem_495670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哭曼卿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495670")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495670'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495670'>去年春雨<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作风）</span>开百花，与君相会欢无涯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495670'>高歌长吟插花饮，醉倒不去眠君家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495670'>今年恸哭来致奠，忍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>欲出送攀魂车。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495670'>春晖照眼一如昨，花已破蕾兰生芽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495670'>唯君颜色不复见，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495670", 495670, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>精魄</span>飘忽随<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495670", 495670, "Clauses/9/Comments/1")'>朝霞</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495670'>归来<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_495670", 495670, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>悲痛</span>不能食，壁上<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_495670", 495670, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>遗墨</span>如栖鸦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_495673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495673'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495673'>高车大马阗上京，释曰演者何声名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495673'>当年余尝与之语，实亦可喜无俗情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495673'>作诗千篇颇振绝，放意吐出吁可惊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495673'>不肯低心事<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495673", 495673, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>镌凿</span>，直欲淡泊趋杳冥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495673'>落落吾儒坐满室，共论悫若木陷钉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495673'>卖药得钱辄沽酒，日费数斗同醉醒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495673'>伤哉不栉被佛缚，不尔烜赫灶名卿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495673'>雄心瞥起忽四顾，便拟击浪东南行。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495673'><span class='link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年10月</a>　终丧自山阳回京选官，有诗送李端懿。作品：送李冀州诗。<div id='poem_495689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_allusion_495689_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495689'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495689'>冠盖倾动车马稠，都门晓送李冀州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495689'>眼如坚冰腼河<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作珂）</span>月，气劲倢鹘横清秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495689'>不为膏粱所汩没，直与忠义相沈浮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495689'>干戈未定民力屈，此行正解天子忧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495689'>男儿胜衣志四海，实耻坐得万户侯。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495689'>孤云南飞莫回首，下有慈亲双泪眸。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
