id='poem_note_495689_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　在京候选，有诗。作品：城南归值大风雪。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年冬。）</span><div id='poem_495677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>城南归值大风雪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495677")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495677_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495677'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495677'>一夜大雪风喧豗，未明跨马城南回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495677'>四方迷惑共一色，挥鞭欲进还徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495677'>旧时崖谷不复见，纵有直道令人猜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495677'>低头抢朔风，两眼不敢开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495677'>时时偷看问南北，但见白羽之箭纷纷来。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495677'>既以脂粉傅我面，又以珠玉缀我腮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495677'>天公似怜我貌古，巧意装点使莫偕。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495677'>欲令学此儿女态，免使埋没随灰埃。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495677'>据鞍照水失旧恶，容质洁白如婴孩。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495677'>虽然外饰得暂好，自觉面目如刀裁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495677'>又不知胸中肝胆挂铁石，安能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_495677", 495677, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>柔软</span>随良媒。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495677'>世人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_495677", 495677, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>饰诈</span>我尚笑，今乃复见天公乖。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495677'>应时降雪故大好，慎勿改易吾形骸。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495677'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_495677_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　有诗呈欧阳修。作品：城南感怀呈永叔。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年四月前。）</span><div id='poem_137874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_137874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/137874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>城南感怀呈永叔</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_137874")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_137874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_137874'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_137874'>春阳泛野动，春阴与天低。<div id='poem_sentence_0_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_137874'>远林气蔼蔼，长道风依依。<div id='poem_sentence_1_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_137874'>览物虽暂适，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_137874", 137874, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>感怀</span>翻然移。<div id='poem_sentence_2_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_137874'>所见既可骇，所闻良可悲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_137874'>去年水后旱，田亩不及犁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_137874'>冬温晚得雪，宿麦生者稀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_137874'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_137874", 137874, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>前去</span>固无望，即日已苦饥。<div id='poem_sentence_6_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_137874'>老稚满田野，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_137874", 137874, "Clauses/15/Comments/1")'>斲掘</span>寻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_137874", 137874, "Clauses/15/Comments/2")'>凫茈</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（原作芘，据李本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_137874'>此物近亦尽，卷耳共所资。<div id='poem_sentence_8_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_137874'>昔云能驱风，充腹理不疑。<div id='poem_sentence_9_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_137874'>今乃有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_137874", 137874, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>毒厉</span>，肠胃坐<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作生）</span>疮痍。<div id='poem_sentence_10_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_137874'>十有七八死，当路横其尸。<div id='poem_sentence_11_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_137874'>犬彘咋其骨，乌鸢啄其皮。<div id='poem_sentence_12_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_137874'>胡为残良民，令此鸟兽肥。<div id='poem_sentence_13_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_137874'>天岂意如此，泱荡莫可知。<div id='poem_sentence_14_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_137874'>高位厌粱肉，坐论搀云霓。<div id='poem_sentence_15_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_137874'>岂无富人术，使之长熙熙。<div id='poem_sentence_16_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_137874'>我今饥伶俜，悯此复自思。<div id='poem_sentence_17_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_137874'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_137874", 137874, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>自济</span>既不暇，将复奈尔为。<div id='poem_sentence_18_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_137874'>愁愤徒<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>满胸，嵘嵘不能齐。<div id='poem_sentence_19_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_137874'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_137874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_137874'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_137874_0'>⑴ 原作多，据黄本、陈本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_137874_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年5月</a>　有信上范仲淹。作品：上范公参政书并咨目七事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　代杜衍作求退表。作品：杜公求退第一表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年夏秋间。）</span>第二表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年夏秋间。）</span>第三表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年夏秋间。）</span>第四表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年夏秋间。）</span>第五表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年夏秋间。）</span><div id='poem_1164378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164378?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜公求退第一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164378")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164378'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164378'>昨于上春，屡贡丹恳，乞解重柄，以收残骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164378_comment'></div>霈泽过优，俞旨不下，临遣中侍，甫降德音，闻命震惊，不敢烦渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164378_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164378_comment'></div>伏念臣才虽至下，性本不欺，交游朋友之间，必以诚信自守，况于事主，安敢妄言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164378_comment'></div>实以年近从心，体素多病，自忝魁任，于今累年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164378_comment'></div>当万务之烦，为天下之筦，虽健才利刃，犹或不支，而皓发羸躯，安能集事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164378_comment'></div>当一人侧席于上，多士建议于下，臣若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164378", 1164378, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>肆然</span>自处，默无所为，清议不容，素履将丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164378_comment'></div>故尝上犯天听，备写血诚，愿踰诞圣之期，以得退休之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164378_comment'></div>金口曲加于奖慰，玉色已形于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164378", 1164378, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>开从</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164378_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下霈成汤之至仁，廓汉高之大度，或假以近郡，或留之本班，庶使自安，以全<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164378", 1164378, "Clauses/44/Comments/1")'>残息</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（《苏学士文集》卷一二。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164378_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1164378'>尊号：原无，据傅本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1164378_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1164379' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164379' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164379?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜公求退第二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164379")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164379_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164379'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164379'>近以露奏，仰干上聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164379_comment'></div>明旨下颁，过推勿贰之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164379_comment'></div>丹衷内切，敢避再三之渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164379_comment'></div>徊徨失措，启处不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164379_comment'></div>臣本以孤生，滥尘上第，践履藩屏，叨窃事权，循分已逾，被遇太厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164379_comment'></div>不意便升近职，复进枢司，使预幄中之谟，得闻天下之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164379_comment'></div>忧太剧而疾作，福既过而灾生，气衰而步趋已艰，齿堕而语言不正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164379_comment'></div>陟降左右，则常虞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164379", 1164379, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>蹶踣</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164379_comment'></div>议论政事，则莫能开陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164379_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164379", 1164379, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>贻笑</span>外夷，腼颜多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164379_comment'></div>而陛下容此衰废，掩其过失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164379_comment'></div>岂不念国之大计，何必私臣之一身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164379_comment'></div>况今西有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164379", 1164379, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>贪毒</span>之羌，北有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164379", 1164379, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>桀傲</span>之虏，包藏凶计，窥伺中朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164379_comment'></div>当得厌难折冲之才，制胜非常之士，寘之近列，可消奸谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164379_comment'></div>臣也少不如人，老岂足任，故非见险而止，安敢容身而去？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164379_comment'></div>但恐力不足而败事，死有责而堪羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164379_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下垂闵蝼蚁之诚，下霈云霓之泽，免此剧任，赐之残骸，以兹禄廪之优，可待英豪之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164379_comment'></div>休息老物，是惟天地之常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164379_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164379", 1164379, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>登拔</span>俊贤，实曰邦家之盛。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1164379_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1164380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜公求退第三表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164380")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164380'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164380'>近者沓贡囊奏，愿解剧权，伏奉某日批答，未蒙俞旨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164380_comment'></div>葵藿之心，希照于白日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164380_comment'></div>蝼蚁之意，未动于上天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164380_comment'></div>惴然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164380", 1164380, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>危悰</span>，若集乔木<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164380_comment'></div>臣粗知进退，概见古今，卮及满而乃倾，月既盈而当缺，事有必至，理无足疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164380_comment'></div>故前志垂文，以为懿戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164380_comment'></div>后人仰止，期无败身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164380_comment'></div>臣久污枢司，绝无远略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164380_comment'></div>万钟之禄，私情之所爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164380_comment'></div>三旌之位，物理以难当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164380_comment'></div>必量力以自思，敢妨贤而取祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164380_comment'></div>下喧物议，上累主知，既交谪之四来，虽全度而安可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164380_comment'></div>恭惟尊号皇帝陛下以至仁覆物，以普爱牧民，岂今左右之臣，不全终始之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164380_comment'></div>敢缘大义，不避蝼陈，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164380", 1164380, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>据蒺</span>弗遑，裂肝以上，祈回天照，俯悉愚衷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1164380_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1164381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164381?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜公求退第四表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164381")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164381'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164381'>伏蒙宸慈，以臣累表乞罢重任，复降批答不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164381_comment'></div>悫忠莫夺，量分甚明，愿当捍命之尤，再露由衷之请<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164381_comment'></div>臣闻罔上者臣之大咎，饰诈者士之丑行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164381_comment'></div>吏议为深，旧章所禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164381_comment'></div>臣器能甚薄，名爵则崇，既陈必退之言，义无复寝之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164381_comment'></div>十目可畏，群听至明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164381_comment'></div>无疾而抗言，是名罔上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164381_comment'></div>怀禄而伪让，则为饰诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164381_comment'></div>不惟受讥于世，贻诮多方，故当诛夷，以戒奸慝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164381_comment'></div>臣实以量狭而位已过，器重而力不任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164381_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164381", 1164381, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>谟猷</span>若斯，陛下所尽悉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164381_comment'></div>形骸如此，众人所共观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164381_comment'></div>既非侥幸于此身，切恐隳弛于众务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164381_comment'></div>况陛下富有四海，乐育群才，岂无他人，可当此任？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164381_comment'></div>伏望照臣至恳，容臣必去，则纤毫之恩不敢授，内外之任无所择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164381_comment'></div>仰干宸听，俯俟俞旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1164381_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1164382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜公求退第五表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164382")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164382'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164382'>四拜封章，乞罢密职，荐颁明诏，未赐俞旨，诚切意专，不避<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164382", 1164382, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>浼渎</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164382_comment'></div>臣闻天生庶民，爱惜至甚，必立君长，使之教育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164382_comment'></div>故土地之所产，雨露之所生，君得用之，亦不可滥，则必分列名位，以求贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164382_comment'></div>君出爵禄，以养其臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164382_comment'></div>臣竭才智，以牧其众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164382_comment'></div>故庶务交举，群生安业，天则报之以气应，锡之以瑞物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164382_comment'></div>苟异于此，灾害乃生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164382_comment'></div>故前志曰：「王者代天爵人，不敢虚授」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164382_comment'></div>虽是小官，尚思精择；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164382_comment'></div>至于重任，岂宜非才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164382_comment'></div>盖天下治乱之所因，国家安危之所系，古今明效，众所共知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164382_comment'></div>早任外官，粗免旷败，不自揆度，实思进用，以谓前世之陈迹可监，本朝之故事可寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164382_comment'></div>陛下以仁圣之资，任遇兼至，顾太平易致，风俗必移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164382_comment'></div>暨臣召入枢司，复迁上列，数年之内，百事无能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164382_comment'></div>关西之将帅覆亡，京右之盗贼猖炽，陷没士卒，杀伤平民，经岁之间，不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164382_comment'></div>而又地屡震于定襄之野，星相凌于天垣之内，螟蝗交作，水旱不调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164382_comment'></div>故北虏移割地之书，西羌遣求币之使，朝廷卑屈辞意，厚纳金缯，帑藏空虚，诛敛烦费，延寇雠于帷幄之内，陷民吏于汤火之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164382_comment'></div>尚如喂饲饥鹰，豢养乳虎，更开后患，未可偷安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164382_comment'></div>皆由臣谋议弗臧，职业不举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164382_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1164382", 1164382, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>惕然</span>内讼，深愧初心，若挞市朝，如坐涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164382_comment'></div>手足颠倒，而罔知所措，心膂枯竭而莫能为谟，敢玩岁时，日俟谴谪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164382_comment'></div>虽陛下容之如地，爱之欲生，上天之鉴，皎尔不可欺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164382_comment'></div>三圣之灵，赫然在其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164382_comment'></div>岂使臣虚食生民之肝脑，窃弄公朝之威柄，必有大祸，将及私门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164382_comment'></div>设令臣族委沟溪，命挂锋锷，有利于国，敢爱此身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164382_comment'></div>但恐因循，益成颓弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164382_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下察此迫切，俯赐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164382", 1164382, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>开可</span>，以兹重柄，别授奇才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164382_comment'></div>必有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1164382", 1164382, "Clauses/104/Comments/0")'>魁卓</span>之贤，可赞隆平之化，恢复艺祖神宗之业，追还咸平、景德之风，君尊于朝，民乐于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164382_comment'></div>若未容臣去，终无比功，徒尔素餐，但塞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1164382", 1164382, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>贤路</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164382_comment'></div>陛下若责臣无效，坚以疾辞，愿正刑书，放还田里，实为优幸，敢有觊觎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164382_comment'></div>天高听卑，冀委成命，臣不胜激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1164382_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年6月</a>　有序送王规。作品：送王规方叔序。<div id='poem_1164413' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164413' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164413?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王规方叔序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164413")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164413_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164413'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164413'>天之生育于物，运动不竭而无疾者，气一而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164413_comment'></div>人生其间，百骸举止，营营有为者，亦气也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164413_comment'></div>然有喜怒悲忧爱恶之情，变以激其气，故滞逆悖乱，失其经而不平，由是疾痛生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164413_comment'></div>必当外假于物以养之，养得其宜，则无夭阏之患焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164413_comment'></div>先王之制礼也，以饮食夫妇之法为之大，故民未有不谨于礼而能安者，此先王爱民之生也至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164413_comment'></div>今子自幼好学，识所谓先王之礼典，长而不饮酒，不茹荤，无嗣不再娶，九年于兹，果乎人之所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164413_comment'></div>自是而不变，反常好异，以为胜众，予甚嗟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164413_comment'></div>而又闻善而耸，见恶而恶，未能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164413", 1164413, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>寂泊</span>，与天为徒，使其心气<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164413", 1164413, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>郁律</span>不宁，而无所辅养，索索然趋乎病疠之场而不还，欲其保天年而立事功，其可得邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164413_comment'></div>予惜夫亲友不以礼义中庸之道勉之，使移其坚致之心，以学圣人之业，徒奖其所难，以伤厥生，吁，可悲也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164413_comment'></div>予因其行而告之，以破异俗之迷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1164413_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　为杜䜣妻张氏作墓文。作品：奉礼郎杜君妻清河张氏墓文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年初秋。）</span><div id='poem_1164444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉礼郎杜君妻清河张氏墓文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164444")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164444'>妇氏张，静而温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164444_comment'></div>承勖子，文节孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164444_comment'></div>十八龄，妇杜䜣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164444_comment'></div>睦族人，孝所尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164444_comment'></div>才三祀，终长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164444_comment'></div>后四载，封秀原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164444_comment'></div>号庆历，直甲申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164444_comment'></div>秋季初，实令辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164444_comment'></div>地阳翟，此宁魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164444_comment'></div>淑而夭，孰可论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164444_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164444", 1164444, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>乳女</span>一，今始言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164444_comment'></div>石镵文，志沈魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164444_comment'></div></div><div
