id='poem_sentence_3_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495691'>青娥供霜洗夜月，兼以皓露驱纤埃。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495691'>常年此夕或阴晦，今岁澄彻将快哉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495691'>是时呼宾赏此景，渐见照我白玉杯。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495691'>清辉向人若有意，径历窗户犹徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495691'>放歌狂饮不知晓，烂熳酌客山岳颓。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495691'>时节飘流晦朔转，已觉九日来相催。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495691'>北轩隙地破苍藓，带花移得黄金栽。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495691'>倒冠露顶坐狂客，撷香咀蕊浮新醅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495691'>最怜小雨洒疏竹，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_495691", 495691, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>爽籁</span>飒飒吹醉腮。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495691'>君时传诗颇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_495691", 495691, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>精丽</span>，意苦<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>泥淖不得来。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495691'>开缄文采自飞动，欲和但愧顽无才。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495691'>久之黾勉强为答，嫌春爱秋真可咍。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495691'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_495691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495691'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_13_495691_0'>⑴ 原作若，据黄本、陈本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495691_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年9月</a>　为杜诜作墓志铭。作品：大理评事杜君墓志。<div id='poem_1164443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大理评事杜君墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164443")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164443'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164443'>杜君叔温，终于庆历辛巳四月九日，葬于庆历甲申九月二日，许州阳翟县麦秀原，即其地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164443_comment'></div>君始生十馀岁，能通诵五经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164443_comment'></div>稍长学文，精笔翰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164443_comment'></div>效杜子美作诗，其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164443", 1164443, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>劲峭</span>严密，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164443", 1164443, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>指事</span>泛情，时时夐至绝处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164443_comment'></div>常恐以诗见名于世，不肯数为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164443_comment'></div>使之有年而不息，可胜言邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164443_comment'></div>性洒然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164443", 1164443, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>峻拔</span>，少所与合，然外甚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164443", 1164443, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>谦煦</span>，喜评论，终日亹亹不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164443_comment'></div>在平阳幕，郡将有率意放于治者，君必以辨之，虽老黠宿吏，皆竦视莫敢移其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164443_comment'></div>天章吴安道、秘阁石曼卿，皆当世伟人，奉诏籍民兵于两河，独延君计事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164443_comment'></div>君为条其未便安者，二公叹息称道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164443_comment'></div>奄忽之前数月，慨然弃官归膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164443_comment'></div>呜呼，其知命欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164443_comment'></div>享年二十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164443_comment'></div>官至大理评事，签署建雄军节度判官事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164443_comment'></div>讳诜，今枢密使、吏部侍郎京兆公之长子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164443_comment'></div>娶崔氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164443_comment'></div>一子曰振，秘书省校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164443_comment'></div>予以叔温亲，而又以文义相周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164443_comment'></div>辛巳春，予病甚，叔温来，升床执予手，语言而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164443_comment'></div>予时为病所毒，不甚辨尚，意己必死，不复见叔温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164443_comment'></div>才三四日，予稍间，而闻叔温逝矣，不觉震起一恸，予病复作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164443_comment'></div>今予乃独存而无恙，每一念之，令人悲酸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164443_comment'></div>况又见吾叔温大葬，且复志其平生，可胜悲哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1164443_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年9月</a>　代杜衍作让官表。作品：杜公让官表。<div id='poem_1164376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜公让官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164376")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164376'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164376'>伏奉制书，特授臣依前尚书吏部侍郎、同中书门下平章事、兼枢密使、集贤殿大学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164376_comment'></div>承命震惧，精魄播越，俯伏廷陛，进退靡遑<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164376_comment'></div>臣闻朝廷之尊，本乎择吏，使才者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164376", 1164376, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>进拜</span>，拙者伏藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164376_comment'></div>至于小官，必当其任，况乎丞相之位，上邻于国，君命出纳之所先，生民休戚之所系，一失厥授，众罹其殃，比于他官，尤当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164376", 1164376, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>精择</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164376_comment'></div>若臣者，天资浅拙，学无根柢，叨窃廪食，已将三纪，心素知分，得皆踰涯，夙夜忧劳，心膂耗竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164376_comment'></div>早居侍从之列，继承屏翰之任，寻被<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164376", 1164376, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>峻命</span>，入冠中台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164376_comment'></div>出拥西雍之麾，旋更大卤之节，虽极<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164376", 1164376, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>勤瘁</span>，无补涓毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164376_comment'></div>暨乎误进枢庭，久尸重柄，故尝屡拜恳牍，乞收<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164376", 1164376, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>残骸</span>，敢烦渊衷，恐失国体，日企神圣之度，下垂开可之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164376_comment'></div>岂意便升鼎司，复领旧职，内惭枯朽之质，重增贪冒之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164376_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下念授受之至艰，奋刚明之独断，收此成命，别付伟人，用适股肱之宜，以增名器之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164376_comment'></div>古者搜于林薮，下及屠钓，不间微陋，务求贤能，要乎成功，不必次补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164376_comment'></div>况今近列，不至乏才，移于他人，乃合公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164376_comment'></div>刳心沥恳，退俟俞旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1164376_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年9月</a>　代杜衍作谢官表。作品：杜公谢官表。<div id='poem_1164377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜公谢官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164377")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164377'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164377'>两贡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>露奏</span>，乞回命书，沓降玉音，不谅<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>血恳</span>，勉尔玺绂，安敢为荣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164377_comment'></div>切以宰相之任，臣实知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164377_comment'></div>盖以师表外廷，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>丹青</span>万务，天下之所想望，王者之所仰成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164377_comment'></div>上则调阴阳之惨舒，外则镇蛮夷之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>桀猾</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164377_comment'></div>置大器于颠危之外，纳生民于仁寿之中，必惟其人，乃可致此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164377_comment'></div>是故峻其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>名数</span>，宠之等威，黄阁黑幡，葱珩赤绂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164377_comment'></div>或延登受策，或御坐为起，是国之所委者大，则礼之所属也隆，遇任既殊，责望宜厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164377_comment'></div>臣立性<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>褊直</span>，有不可移之资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164377_comment'></div>临事<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>迂疏</span>，必无能成之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164377_comment'></div>尘污近辅，贻诮多方，绩效不扬，讥议上彻，居常悚栗，日俟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>窜投</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164377_comment'></div>而陛下收臣于贱朽之中，拔臣于毁谤之内，以谓石庆老而弥谨，赵禹孤而能立，掩阙失而不问，惟忠鲠之是称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164377_comment'></div>屡于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>中闱</span>，亲被盛指，退自省阅，但增震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164377_comment'></div>日月之光，下烛于蔀室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164377_comment'></div>云雷之泽，遽发于枯荄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164377_comment'></div>虽至糜躯，何报厚渥！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164377_comment'></div>敢不尽疲驽之力，宣宽大之恩，绝纤介之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>私回</span>，讲长久之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164377", 1164377, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>利疚</span>，不敢惜死，唯知自公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164377_comment'></div>茍晚节之或渝，必神明之所殛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164377_comment'></div>上尘天览，安敢空言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1164377_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　有诗答梅尧臣。作品：答梅圣俞见赠。<div id='poem_495694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答梅圣俞见赠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495694")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495694'>自嗟处身拙，与世尝龃龉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495694'>至于作文章，实亦少<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495694", 495694, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>精趣</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495694'>低摧朝市间，所向触谤怒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495694'>夫子兴众殊，琢饰贶佳句。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495694'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495694", 495694, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>将<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作锵）</span>然</span>纸上动，读毕恐飞去。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495694'>自觉异平居，恍忽忘世故。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495694'>迥如出泥涂，熏涤失臭污。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495694'>衣之青霞裾，饮以紫蕊露。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495694'>輶轩驾飞黄，蹀躞上夷路。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495694'>古贵知者稀，流俗岂足顾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495694'>雅意虽可珍，三复未敢报。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495694'>退惭百不堪，尚恐君悔误。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495694'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_495694_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　有诗。作品：串夷。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年冬。）</span><div id='poem_495737' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495737' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495737?labeling=true' target='_blank'>串夷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495737")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495737_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495737'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495737'>区区黠虏敢狂呼，遣使峨冠谒上都。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495737'>辄出封章辞国命，妄传声势困军须。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495737'>闭之塞漠为良策，啖以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495737", 495737, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>民膏</span>是失图。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495737'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495737", 495737, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>淳俗</span>易摇无自挠，每闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495737", 495737, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>流议</span>一长吁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495737'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495737_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　有诗应章岷之求。作品：丹阳子高得逸少瘗鹤铭于焦山之下及梁唐诸贤四石刻共作一亭以“寳墨”名之集贤伯镇为之作记远来求诗因作长句以寄。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年十一月之前。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年11月</a>　为韩亿作行状。作品：推诚保德功臣正奉大夫守太子少傅致仕上柱国开国公食邑三千三百户食实封八百户赐紫金鱼袋赠太子太保韩公行状。<div id='poem_1164430' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164430' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164430?labeling=true' target='_blank'>推诚保德功臣正奉大夫守太子少傅致仕上柱国开国公食邑三千三百户食实封八百户赐紫金鱼袋赠太子太保韩公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164430")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164430_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164430'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164430'>曾祖惟忠，累赠太保；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164430_comment'></div>曾祖母张氏，江国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164430_comment'></div>祖处均，累赠太傅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164430_comment'></div>祖母李氏，舒国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164430_comment'></div>父保枢，累赠太师、中书令、尚书令、信国公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164430_comment'></div>母郭氏，越国夫人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164430_comment'></div>继母周氏，吴国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164430_comment'></div>公讳某，字宗魏，其先世占真定府灵寿县之籍，皇考以明经游京师，遂家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164430_comment'></div>公以咸平五年登进士第，除大理评事，知亳州永城县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164430_comment'></div>其地舟车错出，号剧县，本县吏部铨补令久不治，始廷择京师官宰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164430_comment'></div>公既至，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>刮刬</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/27/Comments/1")'>宿滞</span>，去人所不便安者，又为兴起其利，未数月，一邑驩然从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164430_comment'></div>郡将皇甫选为世吏师，闻公治状，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>叹伏</span>不能已，又贻之书而称美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164430_comment'></div>自是，他邑䜣讼之不决者，必属公平处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164430_comment'></div>匈奴南牧，章圣皇帝狩于澶渊，太尉文正王公奏筦机事，牍章繁委，一出公手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164430_comment'></div>景德二年，外台表公永城之劳，改大理寺丞、通判陈州，寻移通判郓州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164430_comment'></div>未几，信国弃养，护丧归上都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164430_comment'></div>服除，通判许州，再移于陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164430_comment'></div>时郡界河决害民，计其补塞费钜万，公驰至其地，集濒河丁壮，就伐薪稿，亲为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>裁画</span>，一物不取于民，而堤复完坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164430_comment'></div>又去郡数十里有群寇，大浮舰而下，将劫旁邑，公廉知之，自部十馀卒，夜掩至，命匽河绝上流，举火伐鼓以疑之，贼弃舟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>迸走</span>，尽束以付吏，谭者伏其谋勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164430_comment'></div>转运使郑文宝闻之，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>走檄</span>会公于许，既至，叹曰：「急欲识公之面颜耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164430_comment'></div>秩满，上祀汾阴，恩迁殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164430_comment'></div>因进文十卷，上览之加赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164430_comment'></div>欲召试，文正公避嫌，例除远郡守，特召见，改太常博士，知洋州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164430_comment'></div>郡有公校李甲者，豪于里中，诬其兄之子为他姓，赂里妪之貌类者，使夺以为己子，又醉其嫂以嫁之，尽取其赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164430_comment'></div>嫂流离历诉于州及提刑、转运使，每置对，甲辄赂吏，常掠使自诬服，杖而去者前后十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164430_comment'></div>公至，复出诉，察妪色冤甚，遂索旧牍视之，皆未尝引乳医为證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164430_comment'></div>一日，尽召其党，出乳医示之，甲遂伏辜，母子复故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164430_comment'></div>八年，迁屯田员外郎、知相州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164430_comment'></div>时河北蝗旱，转运使因岁计覆不以实闻，诸郡畏莫敢言，公力抗章请蠲赋役，州民赖以全活，诏嘉奖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164430_comment'></div>郡伍伯诱民诈讦以事祷巫于舍者而阴受其赇，公察知之，尽捕系狱，表请御史推鞫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164430_comment'></div>狱成，杖伍伯及同奸，窜海岛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164430_comment'></div>事虽验白，宰相与文正公有隙者言于上，犹下迁公通判大名府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164430_comment'></div>时文节张公镇魏，荐公才中御史，遂召为殿中侍御史，寻擢侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164430_comment'></div>时淮浙蝗旱，民饥殍流散，命公为安抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164430_comment'></div>所至赈廪困菑家，罢诸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/137/Comments/0")'>役作</span>，举良吏以牧养之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164430_comment'></div>合肥有陂可溉田，久为右姓专其利，公决导以济下户，得以衣食者不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164430_comment'></div>未还，上嘉其称职，除开封府判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164430_comment'></div>一日奏事毕，趋出，至屏外，复召赐绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164430_comment'></div>岁馀，除河北转运使，诏留监定故丞相向公诸子分财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164430_comment'></div>丁崖州当国，势慑天下，私所亲谕公，欲市向公长安华严别墅，又讽其子从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164430_comment'></div>公至其家，面戒曰：「土田衣食之源不可弃」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164430_comment'></div>故馀财尽均，而华严独存，不以分，由是忤崖州意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164430_comment'></div>及赴河朔，旧二使并移他道，公先独领其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164430_comment'></div>会章圣御楼宴驾，今上践祚，赏赉重沓，常计不能支，朝廷深以为虑，督责甚急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164430_comment'></div>又定州帅曹玮，威名素著，得士卒心，为崖州所恶，以大将军贬莱州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164430_comment'></div>朝议忧其拒命逗挠为变，诏公驰驿，收其兵柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164430_comment'></div>崖州又欲缘此伺公隙，以危法中之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164430_comment'></div>公从容<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/184/Comments/0")'>优裕</span>，处之甚閒，无不得其宜者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164430_comment'></div>覃恩改司封员外郎，又加直史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164430_comment'></div>天圣二年，移知青州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164430_comment'></div>才数月，召为侍御史知杂事，赐金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164430_comment'></div>三年，判大理寺，迁工部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164430_comment'></div>治台杂几二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164430_comment'></div>时中丞阙，久不补，连鞫诏狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164430_comment'></div>郡将有托所亲纳金于宰相文穆公，又因牙吏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164430_comment'></div>审之，文穆执吏以闻，诏付台鞫焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164430_comment'></div>郡将遂诬吏误以闻所亲之语达文穆，欲灭其迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164430_comment'></div>公平心穷治，果郡将以疾，惧废，求外徙，金未达而言漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1164430_comment'></div>文穆大怨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1164430_comment'></div>时都下有告急变者，中贵人夜开禁门，捕卒百馀人付台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1164430_comment'></div>公一讯情得，悉释其缚，中贵人即付诏督促，自以捕反者有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1164430_comment'></div>及狱具，独坐告者诬罪，诛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1164430_comment'></div>三司更茶法，岁课比不登，公承诏劾前与议者，由丞相而下，轻重有罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1164430_comment'></div>用法持平，不为权贵倾挠，二宫称叹，时议难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1164430_comment'></div>俄兼知审官院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1164430_comment'></div>四年，授龙图阁待制，充北朝国信使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1164430_comment'></div>副介匪人，妄传明肃皇太后旨于虏中寺人，虏主问曰：「太后即有旨，大使宜知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1164430_comment'></div>公应曰：「本朝每遣使，必谓之曰：『继好之事，传示后世，两朝之臣，毋相阻猜』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1164430_comment'></div>此乃平时戒使者语，非欲达于北朝也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1164430_comment'></div>虏主大喜，即以语附公谢上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1164430_comment'></div>时皆美公能以副介失辞，更为恩好之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1164430_comment'></div>还掌贡举，又编近制敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1164430_comment'></div>公晓析条义，众皆咨而后定，仍乞以新书颁天下，许所在条陈其不安者更之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1164430_comment'></div>既而出知亳州，未几，上以审刑案牍之繁，召公领之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1164430_comment'></div>公建言乞促日限，以降断敕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1164430_comment'></div>及刑名当奏禀者，亦乞裁定，中典颁下，自是无滞狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1164430_comment'></div>七年，改兵部郎中，同判吏部流内铨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1164430_comment'></div>八年，授枢密直学士、知益州，留侍郊祀乃行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1164430_comment'></div>明道改元，拜谏议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1164430_comment'></div>居益部二年，值大旱荐饥，力为拯济，他郡流冗者归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1164430_comment'></div>故事：每岁官粜粟六万石与贫民，公为先常期增数以出之，以故民不太乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1164430_comment'></div>久旱水涸，苗枯且死，公询旧老，得九升江口，决以溉田，讫今利之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1164430_comment'></div>又移上供物于他州不饥处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1164430_comment'></div>将代，郡人遮转运使，言愿上白留公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1164430_comment'></div>三年，手诏敦奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1164430_comment'></div>既而有旨召公参知政事，宰相以益部远方，不可亟还，须代归以拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1164430_comment'></div>事缓，遂力援他人补之，故公命中格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1164430_comment'></div>及召还，止授御史中丞，充理检使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1164430_comment'></div>入对，建言维、茂二州地接羌夷，秦陇商贾交易，蕃部驱马至永康军场以卖，尽熟山川夷险，道路所出，宜徙场境上，以绝其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_88_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/316/Comments/0")'>觇觎</span>两川之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1164430_comment'></div>又奏疏言时务者五事，上深嘉纳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1164430_comment'></div>景祐中，杨、尚二美人以罪斥出掖庭，公上章引古事为戒，杜其复入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1164430_comment'></div>及依唐故事，奏置御史里行四员，以广言职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1164430_comment'></div>马季良在贬，赂执政者求致仕，遂遣家人挝登闻鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1164430_comment'></div>命始下，言事者以谓致政所以优贤，季良既以罪废，安可得诏，共劾登闻吏不当通其奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1164430_comment'></div>公以谓事行不行在丞相府，登闻吏无罪，何所劾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1164430_comment'></div>纳敕不奉行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1164430_comment'></div>上韪之，议者以为有体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1164430_comment'></div>不踰年，授工部侍郎、同知枢密院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1164430_comment'></div>公以天下久承平，武备不戒，愿与二府各列武臣才任将率者试用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1164430_comment'></div>又乞纂兵法，以授边将，上遂自集《神武秘略》颁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1164430_comment'></div>岭南蛮寇边，先时必自中发兵，多不及事，至是，公奏置广南东西路钤辖司，委以便宜，专用土兵镇守，北兵不徙瘴疠之地，而有以应猝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1164430_comment'></div>夏贼称藩日久，岁遣人至京师货易，出入民间如家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1164430_comment'></div>公深以为不便，请下诏推恩置馆舍，遣使接引，官为监其货易，若优待远人者，实羁防之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1164430_comment'></div>事既下，会公参知政事，不久且出，不果行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1164430_comment'></div>唂󸲐啰与元昊交兵，󸲐啰来献捷，朝廷议加节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1164430_comment'></div>公独以谓󸲐啰之族俱藩臣，纵不能谕令解仇，又以献捷加赏，是激元昊之怒，而为中国生患，固执不可，遂寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1164430_comment'></div>陕西转运使奏乞迁土兵内郡，以省转饷，公不可，曰：「此兵世为边人，乐自为战，一旦徙去乡里，必怨不可用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1164430_comment'></div>亦罢其议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1164430_comment'></div>景祐四年，授参知政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1164430_comment'></div>占谢之日，召坐，嘉叹西府之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1164430_comment'></div>寻迁户部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1164430_comment'></div>是岁，定襄地大震，星文见变，公方在告，力疾入对，为上陈灾异之端，且虞夷狄内侮，宜下诏求直言消复之术，上欣然从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1164430_comment'></div>有顷，罢知政事，改吏部侍郎、知应天府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1164430_comment'></div>三年，以西羌扰边，复严北备，授公资政殿学士、知成德军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1164430_comment'></div>入境在道中，使赍手诏问攻守方略，公画<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_114_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/413/Comments/0")'>备御</span>之策甚详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1164430_comment'></div>延州陷没，边城中人，诬以降敌，朝廷发兵监其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1164430_comment'></div>公求对，力辨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_116_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/419/Comments/0")'>战格</span>甚苦，无降屈之状，上意释然，去守兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1164430_comment'></div>或谓真定不当北冲，改知澶州，属以控扼之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1164430_comment'></div>数以疾请<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_118_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/426/Comments/0")'>便郡</span>，移亳州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1164430_comment'></div>郡本多盗，公始至，诸邑日有剽劫，民情<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_119_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/431/Comments/0")'>骚然</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1164430_comment'></div>公为设策<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_120_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/432/Comments/0")'>刺取</span>，乃府大吏为之囊橐，以故益滋不败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1164430_comment'></div>密发卒尽捕得百馀人，尸于市，郡中<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_121_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/437/Comments/0")'>震肃</span>，讫公去不复有盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1164430_comment'></div>转运使岁敛，民力不堪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1164430_comment'></div>遣牙校赍轻货即地所有市之，民不知有赋，而军须以给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1164430_comment'></div>庆历元年，迁尚书左丞，拜章固让，有诏褒答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1164430_comment'></div>明年，请老，授太子少傅致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1164430_comment'></div>四年八月十五日，薨于京师之里第，享年七十三，以某年某月葬于许州长社县嘉禾乡之先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1164430_comment'></div>公累阶自将仕郎至正奉大夫，勋自骑都尉至上柱国，爵自伯至公，疏封之宠三加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1164430_comment'></div>公性方严质重，虽笑言不妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1164430_comment'></div>每朝廷有大议论，所持坚正，形于颜色，惟义所在，不恤权忌，一发于言，众莫敢夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1164430_comment'></div>虽燕居，未尝见其惰容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1164430_comment'></div>治家处身，一以素约，起微中至贵，始终无少异者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1164430_comment'></div>训厉诸子，蓁然皆成立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1164430_comment'></div>遇物以诚，不为外饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1164430_comment'></div>视人困厄，必欲力之，葬外亲贫无竁者二家，荫孤藐不自振者四人，使以禄奉其先祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1164430_comment'></div>公前夫人蒲氏，追封安定郡太君也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1164430_comment'></div>再娶王氏，进封太原郡太君，相国文正公之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1164430_comment'></div>男八人：长曰纲，前水部员外郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1164430_comment'></div>次综，太常博士、集贤校理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1164430_comment'></div>次绛，太子中允；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1164430_comment'></div>次绎、次维、次缜，太常寺太祝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1164430_comment'></div>次纬，大理评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1164430_comment'></div>次缅，太常寺太祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1164430_comment'></div>女六人：长适端明殿学士、给事中李淑，次早卒，次适大理评事苏舜宾，次适太常寺太祝王整，二人幼未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1164430_comment'></div>孙男十三人：长宗彦，大理寺丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1164430_comment'></div>次宗道，太常寺奉礼郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1164430_comment'></div>次宗古、次宗哲、宗师、宗弼，将作监主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1164430_comment'></div>馀幼未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1164430_comment'></div>孙女十二人：长适光禄寺丞李寿朋，馀未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1164430_comment'></div>曾孙女一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1164430_comment'></div>舜钦于公族为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_150_1164430", 1164430, "Clauses/519/Comments/0")'>仍亲</span>，故稔公风烈，敢录其实迹，纳于太常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1164430_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_151_1164430'></div><div id='poem_sentence_151_1164430_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年11月</a>　为韩亿继室王氏作墓志。作品：太原郡太君王氏墓志。<div id='poem_1164442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太原郡太君王氏墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164442")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164442'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164442'>太子少傅、赠太子太保、忠宪韩公继室夫人王氏，太尉文正公旦之长女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164442_comment'></div>初，文正公在重位，夫人长矣，久择婿不偶，日有盛族扳求，而文正公辄却之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164442_comment'></div>时忠宪公初第，上谒文正公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164442_comment'></div>公一见，遂有意以夫人归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164442_comment'></div>族间哗然，以谓韩氏世不甚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164442", 1164442, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>显大</span>，而上有亲老且严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164442_comment'></div>又前夫人蒲氏有子，当教训抚育，于人情间实难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164442_comment'></div>以夫人少为族人所宠爱，愿于大家著姓为相宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164442_comment'></div>文正公曰：「以吾女性孝而淑贤，必能尽力于夫族，且其节行易以显，亦足见吾家之法度焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164442_comment'></div>族盛者骄惰恣放，多以侈事相誇逐，是不喜吾女之所向，此非渠辈所晓知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164442_comment'></div>遂以夫人归韩氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164442_comment'></div>果能上承尊嫜，奉忠宪公恂恂然，举动无一不中<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164442", 1164442, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>容礼</span>者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164442_comment'></div>抚蒲之生，若己所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164442_comment'></div>文正公每见，必谓之曰：「尔遂能履践吾言，出<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164442", 1164442, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>家人子</span>所见，使吾无所恨也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164442_comment'></div>忠宪为殿中丞，封太原县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164442_comment'></div>及出守洋川，留夫人寓外舍，经时未尝及闑外，惟文正公召然后见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164442_comment'></div>岁时族人出嬉，夫人亦独留不往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164442_comment'></div>时诸子皆幼，夫人课以诗书，日使诵习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164442_comment'></div>文正薨，召入中闱，赐冠服，名通宫籍，以时献见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164442_comment'></div>夫人以谓因缘遗恩，又非从夫之宠，每称疾不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164442_comment'></div>忠宪守青州，急诏还台，署中夜有声，若盗将发户者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164442_comment'></div>左右骇甚，请呼逻卒入以视，夫人曰：「乃公不家而夜呼卒，非便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164442_comment'></div>设有盗，宁以畏死，卒不可呼也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164442_comment'></div>性本閒约，所衣不过绨纻，经岁未尝有所更制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164442_comment'></div>晚节尤以清澹自乐，日诵浮屠氏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164442_comment'></div>其治家不尚严厉，而事皆密有条记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164442_comment'></div>忠宪教诸子甚严，夫人内以慈爱抚之，间又勖以义理之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164442_comment'></div>尝曰：「乃父方正有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164442", 1164442, "Clauses/82/Comments/1")'>法则</span>，为世所知，汝曹若不效之，外人将以为类我，是彰我不德也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164442_comment'></div>其善训如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164442_comment'></div>忠宪为御史知杂时，卒于京师，享年四十四，天圣五年六月二十日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164442_comment'></div>景祐郊祀，追封太原郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164442_comment'></div>初，夫人之丧，稿葬于国门之南佛庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164442_comment'></div>后十七年，忠宪薨，诸孤遂举夫人之榇，合祔于许之长社县某村之原，以庆历四年十一月五日之吉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164442_comment'></div>所生男子七人：曰综，太常博士、集贤校理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164442_comment'></div>曰绛，太子中允；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164442_comment'></div>曰绎、曰维、曰缜，太常太祝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164442_comment'></div>曰纬大，理评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164442_comment'></div>曰缅，太常寺太祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164442_comment'></div>四登进士科，皆有文闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164442_comment'></div>京师士人论世子姓之盛者，以韩氏为称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164442_comment'></div>非惟忠宪之训肃严，是亦夫人保育善诱之所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164442_comment'></div>女六人：长适端明殿学士、兼翰林院侍读学士、给事中李淑，次早卒，次适大理评事苏舜宾，次适太常寺太祝王整，二幼未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164442_comment'></div>孙男十四人，孙女十二人，曾孙女一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164442_comment'></div>某之皇妣，为夫人之妹，故能详夫人之行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164442_comment'></div>今又为诸孤所托，俾刻石纳于圹中，不敢诬饰，为之铭云<span class='inlineComment2'>（《苏学士文集》卷一五。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164442_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1164442'>公：原阙，据傅本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1164442_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　为杜谊作传。作品：杜谊孝子传。<div id='poem_1164429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜谊孝子传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164429")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164429'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164429'>台之黄岩，有至行之士曰杜谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164429_comment'></div>谊性<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164429", 1164429, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>敦笃</span>不茍，惟信义所在，事父母极其孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164429_comment'></div>其父<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164429", 1164429, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>刚狷</span>，独不良于谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164429_comment'></div>惴惴忧恐不自容，窃伺颜色，更端而进，进则诃逐笞击而后已，日日如是而日益勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164429_comment'></div>康定元年九月丧其母，踰月又丧其父，号恸昼夜不绝，勺水不入者累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164429_comment'></div>卜葬于仙村之山下，徒跣负土为坟，往来十馀里，日渡塘涧，泥冰没于骭，虽大雨雪未尝少止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164429_comment'></div>手足皲裂血流，则以漆涂之，每覆一畚，必三绕坟，号而后去，如是者三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164429_comment'></div>既葬，遂筑舍墓旁，人往视之，辄遣去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164429_comment'></div>日一饭，不荤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164429_comment'></div>暮夜，狼虎之迹交于庐侧，谊独不恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164429_comment'></div>明年，吴越大水，所在山皆发洚，推巨石走十数里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164429_comment'></div>台山于他山为高，而水又至，并山之民，居庐田墓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164429", 1164429, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>畜牧</span>漂坏者众，而独不及谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164429_comment'></div>邑人数千，迹谊所为以诣郡，郡为上闻，天子下诏书，奖慰赐帛粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164429_comment'></div>予谓父严子孝，人之常理，又乌足道之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164429_comment'></div>后世寖薄，乃有孝悌之举，又废礼义之教，不施于下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164429_comment'></div>为下者不相师友，而道义榛焉，所在泯泯，无所取法，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164429", 1164429, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>率情</span>放俗，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164429", 1164429, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>荡轶</span>不还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164429_comment'></div>时或有至焉者，则萧然无所依归，朝廷不用，州县忽不为念，不为世人笑且非者几希矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164429_comment'></div>非自信至明者，故亦自疑其所为而怠焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164429_comment'></div>不若古之士大夫，闻一善则称道而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164429", 1164429, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>标举</span>之，使为善者不怠，下流耸激而慕向，有所信而取正焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164429_comment'></div>越俗浮薄，节行不坚，务以华靡相驰逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164429_comment'></div>谊生于今世，而且又在越，非至性，安能趋就此行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164429_comment'></div>故非教之习之之至者矣，非牵于世尚以酤荣利者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164429_comment'></div>使闻而慕效、笃于亲亲者，教自谊始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164429_comment'></div>余得实于台人，故为作传，以俟史氏之求。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1164429_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　为李尧俞所建照水堂作记。作品：处州照水堂记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（约作于是年。）</span><div id='poem_1164426' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164426' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164426?labeling=true' target='_blank'>处州照水堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164426")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164426_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164426'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164426'>括苍郡署冠前山之椒，林壑蔽翳，故当暑有蒸郁之烦，至者或神明不开，则事务隳废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164426_comment'></div>咸平初，杨文公起凝霜阁，下览平旷，得遥岑远林之赏，当时固已为嘉处矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164426_comment'></div>景祐中，孙公元规以言事南迁，移守此郡，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164426", 1164426, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>考政</span>之始，众务毕举，乃历访雄胜之地，以图<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164426", 1164426, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>燕休</span>，又得西北隅绝巘之颠，刬去丛秽，化出异境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164426_comment'></div>溪山之势，奔放坌来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164426_comment'></div>始规地命名，诏徙他郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164426_comment'></div>后更三守，泯然不寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164426_comment'></div>李君然明之来，刷剔隐滞，纲条一新，吏民晓然，踰年甚便，然后思有所以自适，且将以风迹留遗乎后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164426_comment'></div>景与意并，正获乎元规之地，遂构广厦，且以「照水」题之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164426_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164426", 1164426, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>庨豁</span>虚明，坐视千里，虽甚盛暑，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164426", 1164426, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>洒然</span>如秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164426_comment'></div>有长溪者，源自闽来，趋过槛下，前向南明山，盖王方平之旧隐也，苍峰古刹，阴晴隐见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164426_comment'></div>又于东南创月轩，稍却为燕阁，阁之右又为风亭，亭前启轩曰夕霏，是皆辅于照水，而发于新意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164426_comment'></div>华榱髹楯，下上相焕，易去榛莽，与政俱新，盖基于元规，成于然明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164426_comment'></div>使元规之久，则然明乐其成矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164426_comment'></div>然明之去速，则来者其谓斯何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164426_comment'></div>二君<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164426", 1164426, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>默契</span>，遂亡异趣，是政之所起，故自有乎后先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164426_comment'></div>一日，然明书来，求予文其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164426_comment'></div>予慨然东望，神爽坐驰，恨不能剧饮酣歌，俯仰周览于其上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164426_comment'></div>又不能具道其营建之勤，山水之胜，徒胸中耿耿，终日有所思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164426_comment'></div>然明或能图以为贶，使予对而销忧，尚可更发咏歌，以足其未至者矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1164426_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　为僧惟俨粹隐堂作记。作品：粹隐堂记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（旅居苏州之前作。）</span><div id='poem_1164421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>粹隐堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164421")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164421'>天之生蓄万物，纷纶涣散，虽会四时之变而后成，亦已众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164421_comment'></div>必役之以人，然后无所弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164421_comment'></div>百工众技，机智纤悉，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164421", 1164421, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>海渎</span>之广，山壑之邃，不能以自藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164421_comment'></div>放乎其自然，动乎其无知，秘怪异类，判然一出，则必可羁括而就有为，是生之而不使废于世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164421_comment'></div>至于人也，盖物之大者也，而又自相置次，才者多不得其地，皇皇于用者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164421_comment'></div>此造物之意，不可以理通也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164421_comment'></div>故耿介刚直之士，一不与细合，则飒然远举，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164421", 1164421, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>遁名匿迹</span>，惟恐有闻于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164421_comment'></div>惟俨者，为浮屠，往来京师三十年，独喜吾儒氏之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164421_comment'></div>当年少时，诵数百千言，经营世好，尝欲衣冠儒间，摇撼当世，取高位以开所蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164421_comment'></div>知其聱牙不当，遂闭户不践外庭，谢绝过从，有不乐见者，虽贵势不肯一接与语，务为异众之行，求弃于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164421_comment'></div>自置其室为粹隐堂，虽在穰穰大众之中，一室截然斗清，无纤喧微尘之可入，所与往来相知言笑者不过三二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164421_comment'></div>观其议论，使尽用其才，故将有补于世，今乃退缩没没，以讫其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164421_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164421_comment'></div>其可伤也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164421_comment'></div>余谓造物之意不可理通者，以此道之也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1164421_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　有诗。作品：竹轩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年十一月下狱之前。）</span><div id='poem_495836' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495836' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495836?labeling=true' target='_blank'>竹轩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495836")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495836_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495836'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495836'>君与我同好，数过我不穷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495836'>对之酌绿酒，又为鸣丝桐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495836'>作诗写此意，韵和霜间钟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495836'>清篇与翠干，岁久日益秾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495836'>惜哉嵇阮放，当世已不容。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495836'>吾侪有雅尚，千载挹高踪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495836'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_495836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495836'><span class='label'>按：</span>宋朱弁《风月堂诗话》卷上<br /></div><div id='poem_note_495836_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　因进奏院事件获罪下狱，怀念高怿。作品：诏狱中怀蓝田高先生。<div id='poem_495778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495778?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诏狱中怀蓝田高先生</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495778")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495778'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495778'>自嗟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_495778", 495778, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>疏野</span>性，不晓世涂艰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495778'>仰首羡飞鸟，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495778", 495778, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>冥心</span>思故山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495778'>刚来投密网，谁复为颦颜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495778'>寄语高安素，今思日往还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495778'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495778_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　有诗。作品：杂兴。<span class='inlineComment2'>（姑定为庆历四年得罪后所作。）</span>湘公院冬夕有怀。<span class='inlineComment2'>（似作于是年得罪获释、罢官为民后。）</span><div id='poem_495683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杂兴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495683")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495683'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495683'>虎豹性食人，智者畜为戏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495683'>形影本相亲，愚夫见而畏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495683'>疑同不疑异，远哉愚与智。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495683'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_495683_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_495779' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495779' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495779?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湘公院冬夕有怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495779")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495779_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495779'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495779'>去年急雪洒窗夜，独对残灯观阵图。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495779'>今夕悲风撼轩竹，又来开卷拥寒炉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495779'>禅房<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495779", 495779, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>潇洒</span>皆依旧，世路崎岖有万殊<span class='inlineComment2'>（原注：缺。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495779'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_495779_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　有信与欧阳修。作品：与欧阳公书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年底。）</span><div id='poem_1164408' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164408' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164408?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与欧阳公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164408")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164408_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164408'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164408'>舜钦再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164408_comment'></div>冬凛，伏惟按部外起居安裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164408_comment'></div>前月尝拜书，甚疏略，必已通呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164408_comment'></div>舜钦不晓世病，踏此祸机，虽为知己者羞，而内省实无所愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164408_comment'></div>恐流言奉惑，不辟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164408", 1164408, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>缕述</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164408_comment'></div>自杜丈入相已来，群公日相攻谤，非一端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164408_comment'></div>九月末间，尝与子渐、胜之邸中小饮，之翰、君谟见过，胜之言论之间，时有高处，二谏因与之辨析。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164408_comment'></div>本皆戏谑，又无过言，此亦吾曹常事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164408_comment'></div>不一二日，朝中諠然，以谓谤及时政，吁，可骇也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164408_comment'></div>故台中奏疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（赵祐怒二谏，尝论其不才故也。）</span>，天子辨其诬，不下其削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164408_comment'></div>台中郁然不快，无所泄愤，因本院神会，又意君谟预焉<span class='inlineComment2'>（时君谟与赴会诸君同出馆过邸门。）</span>，于是再削，其削亦留中不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164408_comment'></div>诸台益忿，重以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164408", 1164408, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>秽渎</span>之语上闻，列章墙进，取必于君，知二相胆薄畏事，必不敢开口以辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164408_comment'></div>既而起狱，震动都邑，又使刻薄之吏当之<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，希望沽激，深致其文，枷掠妓人，无所不至，设有自诬者，则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164408", 1164408, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>席宾</span>皆遭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164408", 1164408, "Clauses/52/Comments/1")'>污辱</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164408_comment'></div>且进邸神会，比年皆然，亦尝上闻，盖是公宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164408_comment'></div>台中谓去端闱不远，以榷货务较之孰近<span class='inlineComment2'>（榷务后邸中两日作会甚盛。）</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164408_comment'></div>若谓费用过当，以商税院比之孰多？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164408_comment'></div>舜钦或非时为会，聚集不肖，则是可责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164408_comment'></div>原叔、济叔辈，皆当世雅才，朝廷尊用之人，因事燕集，安足为过？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164408_comment'></div>卖故纸钱，旧已奏闻，本院自来支使，判署文记，前后甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164408_comment'></div>况都下他局亦然<span class='inlineComment2'>（不系诸处帐管。）</span>，比之外郡杂收钱，岂有异也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164408_comment'></div>当时本恶于胥吏辈率醵过多，遂与同官各出俸钱外，更于其钱中支与相兼，皆是祠祭燕会，上下饮食共费之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164408_comment'></div>今以监主自盗定罪，减死一等科断，使除名为民，与贪吏掊官物入己者一同<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164408_comment'></div>阁下观其事，察其情，岂当然乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164408_comment'></div>舜钦虽不足惜，为国计者，岂不惜法乎<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164408_comment'></div>审刑者自为轻重，不由二府，茍务快意，坏乱典刑<span class='inlineComment2'>（丁度怒京兆不逐之翰也。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164408_comment'></div>二相恐栗畏缩，自保其位，心知非是，不肯开言<span class='inlineComment2'>（上有怒意，皆不敢承当。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164408_comment'></div>复令坐客因饮食被刑，斥逐奔窜，衔愤沥血，无人哀矜，名辱身冤，为雠者所快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164408_comment'></div>辇毂之下尚尔，远民冤滥，孰肯更为辨之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164408_comment'></div>近者葛宗古、滕宗谅、张亢所用官钱钜万，复有入己，惟范公横身当之，皆得末减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164408_comment'></div>非范公私此三人，于朝廷大体，实有所补多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164408_comment'></div>国朝本以仁爱抚天下，常用宽典，今一旦台中蓄私憾结党，绳小过以陷人，审刑持深文以逞志，伤本朝仁厚之风，当涂者得不疾首而叹息也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164408_comment'></div>舜钦年将四十矣，齿摇发苍，才为大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164408_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164408", 1164408, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>廪禄</span>所入，不足充衣食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164408_comment'></div>性复不能与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1164408", 1164408, "Clauses/128/Comments/0")'>凶邪</span>之人相就，近今得脱去<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1164408", 1164408, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>仕籍</span>，非不幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164408_comment'></div>自以所学教后生，作商贾于世，必未至饿死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164408_comment'></div>故当缄口远遁，不复更云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164408_comment'></div>但以遭此构陷，累及他人，故愤懑之气不能自平，时复嵘𡵓于胸中，一夕三起，茫然天地间无所赴愬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164408_comment'></div>天子仁圣，必不容奸吏之如此，但举朝无一言以辨之，此可悲也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164408_comment'></div>舜钦素为永叔奖爱，故粗写大概，幸观过而见察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164408_comment'></div>苦寒，伏望保重，不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164408_comment'></div>舜钦再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1164408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1164408'><span class='label'>按：</span>《梁溪漫志》卷八，中华书局一九八五年版。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_1164408_0'>⑴ 陶翼本宪长所举，中人追押席客，皆翼之请也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_1164408_0'>⑵ 外郡于官地种物收利之类甚多，下至粪土柴蒿之物，往往取之以助筵会。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1164408_0'>⑶ 始府中敕断追两官，罚铜二十斤。后六日，府中复遣吏来取出身文字，殊不晓。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1164408_0'>⑷ 自有他条不用，私贷官物有文记准盗论，不至除名，判署者五匹，杖九十，其法甚轻。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_37_1164408_0'>⑸ 掖垣诸君列章论馆中人，此自古未有。唯赵叔平不署，且有削，极言辨之，可重可重！</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1164408_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　携家南下苏州，有诗。作品：离京后作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（是年初春作。）</span><div id='poem_495780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>离京后作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495780")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495780'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495780'>春风奈别何，一棹逐惊波。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495780'>去国丹心折，流年白发多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495780'>脱身离网罟，含笑入<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495780", 495780, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>烟萝</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495780'>穷达皆常事，难忘对酒歌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495780'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495780_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
荥阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='923dd88bd2ae4758bc5c663a7f844c29_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("923dd88bd2ae4758bc5c663a7f844c29");'><span id='923dd88bd2ae4758bc5c663a7f844c29_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　由太庙斋郎调荥阳县尉，写诗告别江休复。作品：别邻几余赋高山诗以见意。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　娶屯田郎郑希甫之女郑氏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年</a>　讽刘太后、宋仁宗崇侈越礼，于东京（河南开封）、南京（河南商丘）、西京（河南洛阳）等地广建神御殿安置祖宗御容而作。作品：感兴。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗作于天圣年间，尤以天圣末可能性为大。）</span><div id='poem_495647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感兴三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1031年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", id='poem_sentence_0_495647'>后寝藏衣冠，前庙宅神主。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495647'>吾闻诸礼经，此制出中古。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495647'>秦嬴蚀先法，乃复祭于墓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495647'>汉衣以月游，于道盖无取。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495647'>宣帝尊祖庙，失制遍九土。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495647'>孝元酌前文，一旦悉除去。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495647'>魏帝乐铜台，遗令置歌舞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495647'>昏嗣竟从之，此事狂夫阻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495647'>唐制益纷华，诸陵锁嫔御。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495647'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_495647", 495647, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>旷女</span>日哀吟，于先亦奚补。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495647'>吾朝三圣人，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_495647", 495647, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>乘云</span>不可睹。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495647'>威灵已霄汉，嗣皇念宗祖。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495647'>绘事移天光，刻象肖神武。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495647'>遍敕旧游地，输材起宫宇。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495647'>阶墄扣以金，墙壁衣之黼。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495647'>功既即奉迎，法仗叠箫鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495647'>玩好择珍奇，目夺不可数。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495647'>三京佛老家，已有十数处。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495647'>朝家虽奉先，越礼古不许。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495647'>君不祭臣仆，父<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作又）</span>不祭支庶。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495647'>丹楹岂非孝，圣贬甚萧斧。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495647'>大祀当以时，寝庙即其所。<div id='poem_sentence_23_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_495647'>苍生何其愚，瞻叹走旁午。<div id='poem_sentence_24_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_495647'>贱子私自嗟，伤时泪如雨。<div id='poem_sentence_25_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_495647'></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_495647_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_495648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495648?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495648'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495648'>在昔帝舜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>日，光宅辟四门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495648'>所宾无凶邪，德教日益敦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495648'>末世多滥奸，九重严大阍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495648'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495648", 495648, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>捍掫</span>主讥察，谁何辨语言。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495648'>唐末稍懈怠，尝值外使<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>奔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495648'>京城凶豪儿，奋剑闯帝藩。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495648'>狂呼啸虎豹，便欲倾乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495648'>赖有宰相在，不然神器翻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495648'>我朝讲制度，门籍反不存。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495648'>近知贱丈夫，突入犯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_495648", 495648, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>赤轩</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495648'>陛官未暇执，呶呶何其諠。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495648'>祖宗创业难，慎重在后昆。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495648'>勇夫犹重闭，况乃天子尊。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495648'>何罗犹宜察，况乃外寇屯。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 原作尧，据黄本、陈本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_495648_0'>⑵ 原作史，据黄本、陈本、李本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495648_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_495649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495649?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1031年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495649'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495649'>瞽说圣所择，愚谋帝不罪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495649'>况乎言有文，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495649", 495649, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>白黑</span>时利害。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495649'>前日林书生，自谓胸臆大。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495649'>潜心摭世病，荣成谓可卖。<div onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_495649", 495649, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>凶星</span>，上帝下警戒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495649'>意若日昏㧻，出处恣蜂虿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495649'>安坐弄神器，开门纳珍贿。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495649'>宗支若系囚，亲亲礼日杀。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495649'>大臣尸其柄，咋舌希<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_495649", 495649, "Clauses/19/Comments/1")'>龙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>拜</span>。<div "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>速速</span>伐虎丛，无使自沈瘵。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495649'>陛下幸察之，聪明即不坏。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495649'>如忽贱臣言，不瞬防祸败。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495649'>一封朝飞入，群目已睚眦。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495649'>力夫暮塞门，执缚不容喟。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495649'>十手捽其胡，如负杀人债。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495649'>幽诸死牢中，系灼若龟蔡。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495649'>亦既下风指，黥而播诸海。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495649'>长途万馀里，一钱不得带。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495649'>必令朝夕閒，渴饥死于械。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495649'>从前有口者，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_495649", 495649, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>蹜脰</span>如气鞴。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495649'>独夫已去除，易若吹糠粺。<div id='poem_sentence_21_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_495649'>奈何上帝明，非德不可盖。<div id='poem_sentence_22_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_495649'>倏忽未十旬，炎官下其怪。<div id='poem_sentence_23_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_495649'>乙夜紫禁中，一燎不存芥。<div id='poem_sentence_24_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_495649'>天王下床走，仓猝畏<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_26_495649'>连延旧寝廷，顿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>失若空寨<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作寒，据黄本、陈本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_26_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_495649'>明朝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_495649", 495649, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>黄纸</span>出，大赦遍中外。<div id='poem_sentence_27_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_495649'>嗟乎林书生，生命不可再。<div id='poem_sentence_28_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 长治
