-----title
太原
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='67c4907b1d6c40fcb3cd3790fa9c41cc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("67c4907b1d6c40fcb3cd3790fa9c41cc");'><span id='67c4907b1d6c40fcb3cd3790fa9c41cc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>，25岁</div><div id='67c4907b1d6c40fcb3cd3790fa9c41cc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年11月16日</a>　随父至河东，新修永济桥成，为之作记。作品：并州新修永济桥记。<div id='poem_1164423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164423?labeling=true' target='_blank'>并州新修永济桥记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年11月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164423")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164423'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164423'>太原地括众川，而汾为大，控城扼关，与官亭民居相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164423", 1164423, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>逼切</span>，每涨怒则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164423", 1164423, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>汩漱</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164423", 1164423, "Clauses/4/Comments/1")'>沙壤</span>，批齧廉岸，势<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164423", 1164423, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>躁豪</span>，颇为人忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164423_comment'></div>今参政陈公前守是郡，修巨防以障之，乃西渐，不复虞溃漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164423_comment'></div>然而当数州之空道，传遽商役，日往来挑达不暇，自朝廷置守馀五十年，无梁构得以直绝，流悍且浅，复不胜方𣻜以为济，行者苦于涉久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164423_comment'></div>往往中道遇暴，不善游则溺焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164423_comment'></div>常岁秋冬之交，阳曲诛民钱近三百万，役农人不翅数千，权为徒杠，犹号便利，春则撤去，以避奔冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164423_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164423", 1164423, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>蠹劳</span>相缠，触寒瘃堕者十八九，吏缘奸求，民则甚病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164423_comment'></div>众谓当然，不可改革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164423_comment'></div>庚午岁，天子辍谏议大夫张公领镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164423_comment'></div>亦既至止，悉条政务，访览物害者，得闻斯，欲兴远谋，默有成算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164423_comment'></div>遣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164423", 1164423, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>牙吏</span>秦谦助浮屠辈以谕郡中，命行众悉，勇输其有，俾归之县官，籍而领其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164423_comment'></div>豪之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164423", 1164423, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>顽啬</span>者，市语于人，以谓边氓骚之则急变生，且碍诏，言寖淫满道路间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164423_comment'></div>公所守益悫，掣摇不解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164423_comment'></div>未几，计其货登徒杠三倍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164423_comment'></div>公曰：「可矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164423_comment'></div>乃卜期，少者献力，老者馈饷，斩北山之材，编连<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164423", 1164423, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>宛委</span>，塞川下流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164423_comment'></div>百选坚直，竖以为楹，长踰六仞半，植水下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164423_comment'></div>巨栋上偃，密楯对走，左右支翼，牢不可拔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164423_comment'></div>中并四轨，直亘百丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164423_comment'></div>人忘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164423", 1164423, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>劬瘽</span>，周岁告就，腾突轩延，蔚若变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164423_comment'></div>民请徙市以落之，弦竹歌谣，舞手相交，稚耋走趋，既过复返，贾贩旁午，以嗟以喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164423_comment'></div>邑之叟用歌曰：「汾流汤汤，不复濡我裘裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164423_comment'></div>汾流汤汤，不复溺我携提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164423_comment'></div>不死不吊，我公之造」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164423_comment'></div>予闻子产为郑，以乘舆济溱洧人，孟子谓惠而不知政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164423_comment'></div>公之力是物也，以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1164423", 1164423, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>佚道</span>使民，绝子产远甚，故予敢琢文于石以监后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164423_comment'></div>明道元年十一月十六日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1164423_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='989d59e2545b435d8f2af9497db20558_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("989d59e2545b435d8f2af9497db20558");'><span id='989d59e2545b435d8f2af9497db20558_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>，27岁</div><div id='989d59e2545b435d8f2af9497db20558' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　从汴京归长安省亲，路经洛阳时作。作品：游洛中内。<span class='inlineComment2'>（春末作。）</span><div id='poem_495734' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495734' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495734?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游洛中内<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本校：疑有脱文）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495734")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495734_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495734'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495734'>洛阳宫殿郁嵯峨，千古荣华逐逝波。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495734'>别殿秋高风淅沥，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495734", 495734, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>后园</span>春老树婆娑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495734'>露凝碧瓦寒光满，日转觚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>棱暖艳多。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495734'>早晚金舆此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495734", 495734, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>游幸</span>，凤楼前后看山河。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495734'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495734'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_495734_0'>⑴ 原作孤，据黄本、陈本、李本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495734_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0110407e13094ff39b739ffb6007a793_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0110407e13094ff39b739ffb6007a793");'><span id='0110407e13094ff39b739ffb6007a793_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1036')">1035-1036年</a>，28-29岁</div><div id='0110407e13094ff39b739ffb6007a793' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年11月</a>　有序送王纬。作品：送王纬赴选序。<div id='poem_1164412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王纬赴选叙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164412")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164412'>王氏世居雍，并郭善田数百顷，开第当衢，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164412", 1164412, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>宏邃</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164412", 1164412, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>靓严</span>，精构琢榱，扣之丹青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164412_comment'></div>前冠园圃，嘉花美木奇石，繁茂嵯峨，实皆可赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164412_comment'></div>地形<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164412", 1164412, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>窊隆</span>，以机激水，上下环回无不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164412_comment'></div>虚堂曲榭，琴觞图史，雅具悉备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164412_comment'></div>中朝士大夫，虽不识者，亦寓章句以道其胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164412_comment'></div>奉亲之馈，腆而不烦营；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164412_comment'></div>资身之术，旷而不须谋，故可任化而无系，陶然天壤间，以足一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164412_comment'></div>顾高轩大冕，安可荡于中邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164412_comment'></div>然而之子处之，拘拘乎未尝自适也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164412_comment'></div>今日幸天子讲盛礼，即时俶装走都下，不畏道涂之苦，庶得投牒吏部，调巴闽边徼九品一职官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164412_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164412_comment'></div>州县之禄，日百钱，月廪脱粟两斛，晨夕趋郡将庭下，与牛马并走，寒暑不避，食息失时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164412_comment'></div>视前佚劳之状，设庸童必知之，吾子舍彼而即是，其亦有意焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164412_comment'></div>予谓凡厥蓄康物之才者，虽湮厄负辱、茍活而不耻，虽靡衣鲜食、宴安衍逸而不恃，是皆思发其蕴，以耀众者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164412_comment'></div>茍若是，则小官何足羞，其有以渐也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1164412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　有文哀穆修。作品：哀穆先生文。<div id='poem_1164448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哀穆先生文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164448")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164448'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164448'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164448_comment'></div>穆伯长以明道元年夏客死于淮西道中，友人苏叔才、子美作诗悼之，遣人驰吊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164448_comment'></div>痛夫道不光，予又次其一二行以鉴于世，为文哀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164448_comment'></div>先生字伯长，名脩，幼嗜书，不事章句，必求道之本原，皆记生徒无意处，熟习评论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164448_comment'></div>性刚峭，喜于背俗，不肯下与庸人小合，愿交者多固拒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164448_comment'></div>议事<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164448", 1164448, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>坚明</span>，上下合古，皆可录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164448_comment'></div>然好诋卿弼，斥言时病，谨细后生畏闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164448_comment'></div>又独为古文，其语深峭宏大，羞为礼部格诗赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164448_comment'></div>咸平中，举进士，得出身，调泰州司理参军，牧守称其才，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164448", 1164448, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>贰郡</span>者恶之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164448_comment'></div>又尝以言忤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164448", 1164448, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>贰郡</span>者，守病告，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164448", 1164448, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>贰郡</span>者私黠吏使诬告先生赂，具狱聚左證，后召先生，使众参考之，由是贬池州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164448_comment'></div>中道窜诣阙下，叩登闻鼓称冤，会<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164448", 1164448, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>贰郡</span>者死，复受谴于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164448_comment'></div>后累恩得为蔡州参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164448_comment'></div>先生自废来，读书益勤，为文章益<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164448", 1164448, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>根柢</span>于道，然耻以文干有位，以故困甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164448_comment'></div>张文节守亳，亳之士豪者作佛庙，文节使以骑召先生作记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164448_comment'></div>记成，竟不窜士名，士以白金五斤遗之曰：「枉先生之文，愿以此为寿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164448_comment'></div>又使周旋者曰：「士所以遗者，乞载名于石，图不朽耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164448_comment'></div>既而亟召士让之，投金庭下，遂俶装去郡，士谢之，终不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164448_comment'></div>常语人曰：「宁区区糊口为旅人，终不为匪人辱吾文也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164448_comment'></div>天圣末，丞相有欲置为学官者，耻诣谒之，竟不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164448_comment'></div>尝客京师南河邸中，往往醉，暮归过之，如不省持者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164448_comment'></div>夜半，邸人犹闻其诵吟喟叹声，因隙窥之，则张灯危坐，苦矉执卷以至曙，用是贷其资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164448_comment'></div>母丧，徒跣自负榇成葬，日诵《孝经》、《丧记》，未尝观佛书、饭浮屠氏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164448_comment'></div>识者怜哀之，或厚遗，则必为盗取去，不然且病，或妻子卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164448_comment'></div>后得柳子厚文，刻货之，售者甚少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164448_comment'></div>踰年，积得百缗，一子辄死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164448_comment'></div>将还淮西，道遇病，气结塞胸中不下，遂卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164448_comment'></div>嘻吁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164448_comment'></div>天之厌文久矣，先生竟以黜废穷苦终其身，顾其道宜不容于今世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164448_comment'></div>然由赋数<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1164448", 1164448, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>踦只</span>，常罹兵贼恶少辈所辱困，其节行至死不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164448_comment'></div>有孤，懦且幼，遗文散坠不收，伯长之道，竟已矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164448_comment'></div>初，先生死，梁坚自解以书走上党遗予，欲访其文，俾予集序之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164448_comment'></div>去年赴举京师，历问人，终不复得一篇，惟有《任中正尚书家庙碑》、《静胜亭记》、《徐生墓志》、《蔡州塔记》，皆平昔所为，又不足成卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164448_comment'></div>今舅氏守蔡，近以书使存其家，且求其所著文字，未至间，作文哀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164448_comment'></div>道不胜于命，命不会于时，吁嗟先生竟胡为<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164448_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1164448'>「售」上原有「值」字，据《皇朝文鉴》、《穆参军遗事》删。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1164448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1164448'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_33_1164448_0'>⑴ 《苏学士文集》卷一五。又见《皇朝文鉴》卷一三二，《河南穆公集》附录《穆参军遗事》，《三续古文奇赏》卷二六，《宋元学案补遗》卷九。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1164448_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年5月28日</a>　冒丧论事。作品：乞纳谏书。<div id='poem_1164367' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164367' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164367?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞纳谏书</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐三年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164367")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164367_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164367'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164367'>五月二十八日，具官臣某，谨上书皇帝阙下：臣闻治平之君，使危亡祸乱之言不离于耳，则天下庶可久安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164367_comment'></div>高位之臣，使颠覆窜殛之祸不绝于心，则百职可以无旷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164367_comment'></div>苟治平而忽危亡，未有不危亡者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164367_comment'></div>高位而忘颠覆，未有不颠覆者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164367_comment'></div>此物理之常势，古今之定分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164367_comment'></div>历观前代圣神之君，好闻乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>谠议</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164367_comment'></div>贤明之辅，不壅乎下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164367_comment'></div>盖以四海至远，民有隐慝，不可以遍照，故无间愚贱之言而择用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164367_comment'></div>万几至烦，事有习弊，不可以独览，故必求众多之议以更张之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164367_comment'></div>然后朝无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>遗政</span>，物无遁情，虽有佞人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>邪谟</span>，莫得而进也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164367_comment'></div>臣昨睹乙亥诏书，戒越职言事者，播告四方，无不惊惑，往往窃议，恐非本于宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164367_comment'></div>盖陛下即位以来，屡诏群下，以求鲠直，故百寮皆得转对；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164367_comment'></div>又置匦函，设<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>直言极谏科</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164367_comment'></div>今诏书如此，是与前事相违，岂非大臣蔽塞陛下聪明，杜塞忠良之口？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164367_comment'></div>不惟亏损朝廷大政，实亦自取覆亡之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164367_comment'></div>夫纳善<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>进贤</span>，宰相之事，蔽君自任，未或不亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164367_comment'></div>今谏官、御史，又多出其门下，但务希旨，即取好官，多士盈庭，噤不得语，陛下拱深宫之内，何由得闻天下之务乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164367_comment'></div>臣前见陛下以孔道辅、范仲淹刚直不挠，致位谏台，后虽改他官，不忘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>献纳</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164367_comment'></div>此二臣者，非不知缄口数年，坐得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>卿辅</span>，盖不敢负陛下委注之意，亏臣子忠荩之节，而皆罹中伤，窜谪不暇，使正臣夺气，鲠士咋舌，目睹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>时弊</span>，口不敢论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164367_comment'></div>昔晋侯问叔向曰：「国家之患孰为大」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164367_comment'></div>对曰：「大臣持禄而不极谏，小臣畏罪而不敢言，下情不得上通，此患之大者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164367_comment'></div>是故汉文感女子之说而肉刑是除，武帝听三老之议而江充以族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164367_comment'></div>肉刑古法，江充近臣，女子老人，愚耄疏隔之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164367_comment'></div>盖以义之所在，贱不可忽，二君从之，后世称圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164367_comment'></div>况国家班设爵位，列陈豪英，故当责其公忠，安可教之循默？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164367_comment'></div>赏之使谏，尚恐不言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164367_comment'></div>罪其敢言，孰肯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/100/Comments/0")'>献纳</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164367_comment'></div>物情闭塞，上位孤危，轸念于兹，可为惊怛！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164367_comment'></div>伏望陛下霈发德音，追寝前诏，勤于采纳，下及刍荛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164367_comment'></div>求睹四海之安危，垂念朝廷之阙失，见所未见，日新又新，故可常守隆平，保全近辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164367_comment'></div>若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>诏榜</span>未削，欺罔成风，则不唯堂下远于千里，窃恐指鹿为马之事，复见于今朝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164367_comment'></div>臣区区以此言达于冕旒者，非不知出口祸从，为众<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1164367", 1164367, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>悯笑</span>，盖欲陛下一悟，则天下蒙福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164367_comment'></div>以臣之躯，负苍生之命，亦已大矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164367_comment'></div>伏望陛下留意焉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164367_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1164367'>负：傅本作「贸」，《国朝诸臣奏议》作「质」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1164367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1164367'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_33_1164367_0'>⑴ 《苏学士文集》卷一一。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷一八，《国朝二百家名贤文粹》卷六八，《太平治迹统类》卷一○，《九朝编年备要》卷一○，《宋史全文续资治通鉴》卷七，《宋史》卷四四二《文苑传》四，《历代名臣奏议》卷一九九。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1164367_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='782559558b8e44108eddc73792fc1e56_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("782559558b8e44108eddc73792fc1e56");'><span id='782559558b8e44108eddc73792fc1e56_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1037')">1036-1037年</a>，29-30岁</div><div id='782559558b8e44108eddc73792fc1e56' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　为宋仲达作墓铭。作品：太常博士宋仲达墓铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年7月之前。）</span><div id='poem_1164439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太常博士宋仲达墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164439")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164439'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164439'>宋君仲达，讳武也，占太原籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164439_comment'></div>祖缙，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164439_comment'></div>父韬，以谋勇称，刘崇窃奄并汾，署为通进使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164439_comment'></div>太平兴国四年，天王平晋，君未冠，侍朝中都，寓于雒，穷困笃学，以文名两京间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164439_comment'></div>性方介远举，嫉非义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164439_comment'></div>与人交，有失必面直之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164439_comment'></div>襟抱轩辟，好树大节，不顾当世，常欲引手取卿相位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164439_comment'></div>景德元年，举进士，首河南荐书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164439_comment'></div>明年登第，授校书郎，知江宁府溧阳县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164439_comment'></div>满，调相州观察推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164439_comment'></div>今吏部侍郎、知枢密院太原王公随，时任御史，早与之游，复嘉其吏材，白见，改著作佐郎，知越州山阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164439_comment'></div>踰年，转秘书，知英州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164439_comment'></div>迁太常博士、通判同州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164439_comment'></div>同之郡将，不谨法度，其属悉媚莫敢言，君独以理折其冲，不能遂行，或先几绝其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164439", 1164439, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>孳萌</span>，以是事多<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164439", 1164439, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>沮逆</span>少合，君亦悒悒不自喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164439_comment'></div>未几，感疾终官下，年五十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164439_comment'></div>有子长矣，郡将以事牵系狱中，私黠吏胁其嫠，娶焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164439_comment'></div>子闻之，号恸抢地，遂以狂失心，乃出之使逸去，死于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164439_comment'></div>义者窃缄君之骨，藏之佛庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164439_comment'></div>后十馀年，天章待制王公沿以都转运使陕西，枢密太原公别而属之曰：「予生平交游，与宋仲达善，不幸死之日，其孥流离，人所闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164439_comment'></div>交所以托死生，今仲达之骨旅而不兆，我则愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164439_comment'></div>敢仗高义，因此行以求之，且使宁魄九原，示予不忘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1164439", 1164439, "Clauses/79/Comments/1")'>雅素</span>也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164439_comment'></div>已而遇临晋主簿颜太初之官，过郡访得之，遂以礼葬于同之某县某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164439_comment'></div>君两娶，前弘农杨氏生一子，亦卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164439_comment'></div>君没于天圣三年夏六月，葬于景祐三年秋七月辛卯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164439_comment'></div>前葬期，太原公自京师疏其族氏，以函命能文者志其圹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164439_comment'></div>铭云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1164439'>无子以似，以藏以祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164439_comment'></div>以直得交，卒敛以义，交乎无腼于后世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1164439_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年12月5日</a>　编定杜甫诗集。作品：题杜子美别集后。<div id='poem_1164415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题杜子美别集后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年12月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164415")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164415'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164415'>杜甫本传云有集六十卷，今所存者才二十卷，又未经学者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164415", 1164415, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>编辑</span>，古律错乱，前后不伦，盖不为近世所尚，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164415", 1164415, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>坠逸</span>过半，吁，可痛闵也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164415_comment'></div>天圣末，昌黎韩综官华下，于民间传得号《杜工部别集》者凡五百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164415_comment'></div>予参以旧集，削其同者，馀三百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164415_comment'></div>景祐侨居长安，于王纬主簿处又获一集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164415_comment'></div>三本相从，复择得八十馀首，皆豪迈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164415", 1164415, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>哀顿</span>，非昔之攻诗者所能依倚，以知亦出于斯人之胸中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164415_comment'></div>念其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164415", 1164415, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>亡去</span>尚多，意必皆在人间，但不落好事家，未布耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164415_comment'></div>今以所得，杂录成一策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164415_comment'></div>题曰《老杜别集》，俟寻购仅足，当与旧本重编次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164415_comment'></div>又本传云：「旅于耒阳，永泰二年，啖牛肉白酒，一夕而卒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164415_comment'></div>此诗中乃有大历三年《白帝城放船出瞿塘将适江陵》之作，及大历五年《追酬高蜀州见寄》，旧集有大历二年「调玉烛」之句，是不卒于永泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164415_comment'></div>史氏误文也，览者无以此为异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164415_comment'></div>景祐三年十二月五日，长安题。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1164415'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1164415_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　答陈尧佐来信。作品：启事上奉宁军陈侍郎。<div id='poem_1164404' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164404' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164404?labeling=true' target='_blank'>启事上奉宁军陈侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164404")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164404_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164404'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164404'>某启：伏自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>台驭</span>东上，颇失<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>依庇</span>，倾想恩德，一食三起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164404_comment'></div>窃念古之烈士，身积道义，而往往伏穷阎之下，栖岩穴之中，虽裘葛不完，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>粝糠</span>几废，亦未尝造谒有位，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>祈望</span>恩奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164404_comment'></div>顾血气心膂，岂异于人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164404_comment'></div>且非乐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>枯槁</span>饿贱而恶荣利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164404_comment'></div>盖以被一顾之厚、一言之饰，虽没齿不可忘，茍不怀报，则夷狄之民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164404_comment'></div>是则知之浅，益自负而道胜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164404_comment'></div>待之厚，必自倾而心劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164404_comment'></div>非局于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>险隘</span>，祸难薄身，不可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>转脱</span>，又安肯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>俛容</span>撙意，求出入门下邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164404_comment'></div>舜钦性不及中庸之道，居常慕烈士之行，幼趋先训，苦心为文，十年馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164404_comment'></div>高位齿牙之论故不及，然未始趋跄其门阑，以翘知己，顾材质虽无似，窃以是自贵重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164404_comment'></div>不幸皇天降凶，罹此大酷，血属百口，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>嗷然</span>无归，濒于沟壑数者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164404_comment'></div>始荷高平侍郎定其侨居之计，未几而有河阳之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164404_comment'></div>暨阁下开府，首传诲言，嗣颁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>饩醴</span>，俄驱旌旆，致奠几筵，慰谕丁宁，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>存暖</span>孤苦，力敦久要，坐变<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>偷风</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164404_comment'></div>自尔家事细微，必为赒给，使举族免于流转，得专孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164404_comment'></div>其为惠<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>浅深</span>，以此可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164404_comment'></div>每抚臆论报，然后知身命之轻于鸿毛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164404_comment'></div>比者，阁下入镇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>近辅</span>，曾未踰旬，而辄辱书教，辞旨稠重，回出常节，益见大君子始终经纬之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164404_comment'></div>感中<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>腷塞</span>，动成长嗥，沥血布言，疏略不则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164404_comment'></div>秋夏之会，气候未调，伏冀精保寝兴，辅以药物，哀情不任<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164404", 1164404, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>倾祝</span>之极。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1164404_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　应崔籍之请作。作品：处士崔君墓铭。<div id='poem_1164438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164438?labeling=true' target='_blank'>处士崔君墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164438")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164438'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164438'>博陵崔籍，初命理狱于平凉，将改葬其先君，以闻得报，遂来求志于舜钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164438_comment'></div>先祖中令之夫人，则驾部郎宪之女，视籍之先君则异母弟，故能详焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1164438_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　有信上杜衍。作品：上杜侍郎启。<div id='poem_1164405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上杜侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164405")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164405'>某启：两获侍坐，辄沐垂誉鄙言，承言愧羞，默不敢谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164405_comment'></div>前又数有人言，阁下称道所联《含元赋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164405_comment'></div>窃惟大君子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164405", 1164405, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>奖擢</span>后进，故不惜溢言以誉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164405_comment'></div>然阁下为世<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164405", 1164405, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>标矩</span>，人所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164405", 1164405, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>仰属</span>，坐镇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164405", 1164405, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>藩屏</span>，列邑承风，举动言论，播为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164405", 1164405, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>仪法</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164405_comment'></div>若舜钦辈才术甚疏，无足称道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164405_comment'></div>或当前时宜，训戒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164405", 1164405, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>开扶</span>，使就成人之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164405_comment'></div>至于谐言短韵，无补于世，不当置于齿牙间，使人传信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164405_comment'></div>盖俗浮易扇，染而难回，非惟损明府之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164405", 1164405, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>雅鉴</span>，实亦隳风化之一节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164405_comment'></div>况提封之下，千里而远，其间抱才行、包道业者甚众，日希明府一言一顾，以为光价，有未获者，盖<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164405", 1164405, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>翘翘</span>焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164405_comment'></div>幸冀移意于彼，以重所褒，则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164405", 1164405, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>蚩陋</span>者甘心自屏，安有所觊望哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164405_comment'></div>所索《崔处士墓铭》，承命不敢隐，谨缮写通上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164405_comment'></div>惶恐惶恐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1164405_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　有信上孙冲。作品：上孙冲谏议书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年前后。）</span><div id='poem_1164387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上孙冲谏议书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164387")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164387'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164387'>某尝谓世之急者，教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164387_comment'></div>教之久则困弊而不流，柄天下者必相宜以救之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164387_comment'></div>救失其宜，则衰削溃败而莫得收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164387_comment'></div>昔者道之消，德生焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164387_comment'></div>德之薄，文生焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164387_comment'></div>文之弊，词生焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164387_comment'></div>词之削，诡辩生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164387_comment'></div>辩之生也害词，词之生也害文，文之生也害道德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164387_comment'></div>夫道<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>也者</span>，性也，三皇之治也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164387_comment'></div>德<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>也者</span>，复性者也，二帝之迹也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164387_comment'></div>文者，表而已矣，三代之采物也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164387_comment'></div>辞者，所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>董役</span>，秦汉之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>训诏</span>也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164387_comment'></div>辩者，华言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>丽口</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>贼蠹</span>正真而眩人视听，若卫之音，鲁之缟，所谓晋唐俗儒之赋颂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164387_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164387_comment'></div>三代之际，救得其宜，故治多焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164387_comment'></div>三代之后，不知所以救，故乱生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164387_comment'></div>然上世非无文词，道德胜而后振故也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164387_comment'></div>后代非无道德，诡辩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>放淫</span>而覆塞之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164387_comment'></div>故使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>厖杂</span>不纯而流风易遁，诚可叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164387_comment'></div>夫文与词失之久矣，乌可议于近世邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164387_comment'></div>况敢言道德者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164387_comment'></div>然而典策之奥，治词之法，不越此有言而又笔之者，斯亦可尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164387_comment'></div>某志此有素，未尝暴发于流俗前，以召<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>笑侮</span>，茍非遇大贤君子，智识度越，则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>缩迹</span>避讪，碌碌走趋之不暇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164387_comment'></div>窃惟阁下宇量<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>拂世</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>业问</span>追古，放言遣怀，刮昏出明，锐然欲掌弘大物，以晓聋众而起前弊，某故敢缮写杂文共八十有五篇，求为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>佐佑</span>，又用此本原论以先之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164387_comment'></div>盖<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1164387", 1164387, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>丛残</span>屑浅之说，不足诡听览也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164387_comment'></div>自公馀閒，乞赐一阅，实区区之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164387_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1164387_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　有序送王靖。作品：送外弟王靖序。<div id='poem_1164411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送外弟王靖叙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164411")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164411'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164411'>古之达者，皆发于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164411", 1164411, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>羁苦</span>饿寒，盖必极困而后起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164411_comment'></div>孔尼之不试，孟、荀之谗，屈平之窜，管夷吾之穷且囚，司马迁之刑，扬雄、王仲淹之乱，皆坎𡒄埋废不自平，然后极心穷精，以入乎道术之渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164411_comment'></div>策书其言，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164411", 1164411, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>播洒</span>奥大，师监于后世，历数千百年外，道其名，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164411", 1164411, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>熇然</span>可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164411", 1164411, "Clauses/17/Comments/1")'>暴炙</span>人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164411_comment'></div>今贵人之胄，以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164411", 1164411, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>缇纨</span>肥味泽厥身，一无达者之困肆焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164411_comment'></div>自以为胜物也，习堕志覆，安久质变，不知诚性之日<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164411", 1164411, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>陷脱</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164411_comment'></div>虽瞬动言息，戴威爵，坐署位，对之殗殗如在九泉之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164411_comment'></div>吁，可悯也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164411_comment'></div>外弟王君瞻叔者，生相家，未龀而官，十岁而孤，资性<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164411", 1164411, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>粹愿</span>，不群戏弄，好学少言，若有所负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164411_comment'></div>今年如长安，逆妇李以归，索言为别，故敢告以古之达者之为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164411_comment'></div>无习安以盗性，庶震摇乃心，起闻于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164411_comment'></div>以为先荣则达，而求用之之荣，不如不用之之达之荣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164411_comment'></div>子其怀也。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1164411'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1164411_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　有信上孔道辅。作品：上孔待制书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于景祐三年或四年。）</span><div id='poem_1164388' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164388' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164388?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上孔待制书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164388")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164388_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164388'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164388'>某月日，某谨再拜献书知府待制阁下：某窃以自夫子没，迄今数千百年，其教<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>混沦</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/4/Comments/1")'>闳诞</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>充格</span>上下，斯须不可亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164388_comment'></div>天地得之，日星光明不斗食，山泽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>棣达</span>而不童涸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164388_comment'></div>幽则治鬼神，显则严君亲，使万物各安其分，而无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>窘暴</span>之心者，诚至矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164388_comment'></div>造物者宜世生哲人，以炽厥后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164388_comment'></div>长国者宜不绝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>侯封</span>，以尊其本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164388_comment'></div>昔汉世韦贤，家传一经，犹继为公相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164388_comment'></div>定国断狱平允，犹高大其门，况圣人之后者邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164388_comment'></div>故阁下幼而淑质，长而令闻，其学<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>奥大</span>而不杂，其言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>谨峻</span>而切事，是天以明粹精刚之气钟于阁下，将令诏述正教而衍大之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164388_comment'></div>天下士人，实有望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164388_comment'></div>观乎自结人主，冠映当世，阔步台阁，端持纪纲，弗<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>显谏</span>以侥誉，弗枉节以求党，奸凶之朋，脰缩面汗，鳃鳃然不敢抗法度，阁下有力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164388_comment'></div>其典吏部也，尽刮宿弊，专以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>白黑</span>善恶为己任，坐束吏手，日隳滥阶，伸贤而屈不肖，虽山公为之，不出于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164388_comment'></div>奈何丑正多徒，害能以谤，既而去职，识者伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164388_comment'></div>其使匈奴也，专对以礼，严乎若神，不妄言而谄笑，不槃辟而雅拜，尊本朝而抑外夷，得古良使之风焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164388_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164388_comment'></div>阁下之事业既已显白，而朝廷之用未充，天下之誉未洽，留滞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>方屏</span>，浸移岁律，某窃惑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164388_comment'></div>得非纳士未广，介洁无助者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164388_comment'></div>夫有助者，庸人可以获声称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164388_comment'></div>无助者，君子必也受訾辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164388_comment'></div>古人诩诩而汲善，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>渠渠</span>而下士，是致德义日益引，望实日益隆，忧患无自入焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164388_comment'></div>如支体之护首目，枝叶之蔽本根，而藩垣之严室庐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164388_comment'></div>《晏子春秋》曰：「夫子居处惰倦，廉隅不正，季路、原宪侍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164388_comment'></div>血气为疚，志意未达，仲弓、卜商侍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164388_comment'></div>德未盛，行未厚，颜回、骞雍侍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164388_comment'></div>又《孔丛子》引夫子之言曰：「吾有四友焉：得回也，门人加亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164388_comment'></div>得赐也，远方之士日至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164388_comment'></div>得师也，前光后辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164388_comment'></div>得由也，恶言不及门」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164388_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164388_comment'></div>是人之助也诚益哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164388_comment'></div>圣人且如是，况不逮者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164388_comment'></div>阁下方以盛年状猷，将康济天下，而良助犹鲜，诚可怃然，设或纤人搆谗，天子投杼，及是也，能为阁下奋不顾身，明目张胆，论列湔洗，破群毁而明忠节者，果何人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164388_comment'></div>阁下其念之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164388_comment'></div>茍能上循先圣之法，下恤愚夫之言，清而容物，介不拒善，则士不远千里而求为助焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164388_comment'></div>助且至，登天阶，跻岩廊，可拱而俟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164388_comment'></div>某无似者，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1164388", 1164388, "Clauses/130/Comments/0")'>想望风采</span>，为日久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164388_comment'></div>敢辄献言，以为谒见之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164388_comment'></div>虽欲自述节行，以干听览，窃闻古谚有之：「虏自鬻，虽哀不售；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164388_comment'></div>士自眩，虽辩不纳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164388_comment'></div>顾惟大君子察其材之淑慝而进退之可也，鄙心无所私幸焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164388_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1164388_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年10月</a>　送别杜衍而作。作品：送杜密学赴并州。<div id='poem_495735' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495735' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495735?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送杜密学赴并州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495735")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495735_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495735'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495735'>维帝私明哲，遥遥世可论。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495735'>风流擅南国，文采续高门。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495735'>才美趋贤路，名雄出帝阍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495735'>雍容初入幕，烜赫已开藩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495735'>黠吏腹心溃，疲民襦裤温。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495735'>谳刑曾揽辔，按俗亦飞轩。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495735'>倚注宸襟切，淹回物论喧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495735'>朔区官益峻，宪府望弥尊。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495735'>除弊朝之急，于时孰肯言。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495735'>议高心不挠，补外众为冤。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495735'>西雍新恩重，中台故事存。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495735'>政行殊有体，化洽密无痕。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495735'>尺诏来丹扆，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_495735", 495735, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>双符</span>换太原。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495735'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_495735", 495735, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>具装</span>明晚野，大旆卷朝暾。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495735'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_495735", 495735, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>惠爱</span>留关辅，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_495735", 495735, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>风威</span>入塞垣。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495735'>安<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>车行急召，想望慰元元。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 原作印，据李本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495735_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　游昇阳殿故址而作。<div id='poem_495651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>升阳殿故址</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495651")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495651'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495651'>昔在开元中，此名升阳殿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495651'>西通大明宫，夹道直如箭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495651'>至尊黄金舆，乘春日<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495651", 495651, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>幸宴</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495651'>翠嫔戛钟鼓，欢呼奏新遍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495651'>巧舞风燕翻，妖<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>歌露莺啭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495651'>酒光射锦幄，上下花会炫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495651'>雕盘堆繁英，艳粉弱自战。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495651'>天欢日无穷，臣谏莫敢献。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495651'>纵火寝庙平，挥戈君臣迸。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495651'>髑髅今成堆，皆昔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_495651", 495651, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>燕赵</span>面。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495651'>每因锄耨时，数得宝玉片。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495651'>今秋雨泽多，谷穗密如辫<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作瓣，据黄本、陈本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495651'>不有失德君，焉为穑夫佃。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　游含元殿而作。作品：览含元殿基因想昔时朝会之盛且感其兴废之故。<div id='poem_495750' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495750' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495750?labeling=true' target='_blank'>览含元殿基因想昔时朝会之盛且感其兴废之故</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495750'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495750'>在昔朝元日，千门动地来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_495750_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　游兴庆池而作。<div id='poem_495654' class='_poem'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　游九龙宫而作。作品：游南内九龙宫。<div id='poem_495743' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495743' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495743?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游南内九龙宫</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495743")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495743_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495743'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495743'>昔帝龙骧后，因池大此宫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495743'>萧笳叠终日，旌仗展无穷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495743'>绘塑神灵集，飞潜爪角雄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495743'>阴轩常隐雾，暗堵亦含风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495743'>巨盗来<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495743", 495743, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>移国</span>，天王遽避戎。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495743'>苍黄狩巴蜀，倏忽陷河潼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495743'>波春荡初月，沙晚发悲鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495743'>世变今无复，人愁杳莫终。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495731'>转圆非雅具，攲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>器有深灾<span class='inlineComment2'>（才翁）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495731'>持满忘前监，相倾自下催。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495731'>流风无以复，视此一裴回<span class='inlineComment2'>（子美）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495731'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_495731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495731'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_495731_0'>⑴ 原作楃，据黄本、陈本、李本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_495731_0'>⑵ 原作燕，据黄本、陈本、李本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_495731_0'>⑶ 原缺，据黄本补，李本作覆</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495731_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　有诗。作品：大风。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于守制长安时，姑系于此。）</span>晚意。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于守制长安时，姑系于此。）</span>老莱子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于守制长安时，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_495680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495680?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大风</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495680")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495680'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495680'>秋半收穫登郊原，攲侧小屋愁夕眠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495680'>是夜大风拔树走，吹倒南壁如崩山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495680'>梦中惊起但呼叫，病仆未动徒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495680", 495680, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>豗喧</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495680'>驱令燃火遍照燎，瓦甓狼藉满我前。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495680'>披衣抱枕欲避去，去此乃是旷野田。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495680'>况时风怒尚未息，直恐泾渭遭吹翻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495680'>露坐不免念禾黍，必已<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_495680", 495680, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>刮刷</span>无完根。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495680'>六事不和暴风作，尝闻洪范有此言。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495680'>昔时大风禾尽偃，上帝盖直周公冤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495680'>方今天子至神圣，惟恐臣下辜其恩。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495680'>是何此风乃震作，吹尽秋实伤元元。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495680'>有能返风起禾者，亦足表异知所存。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495680'>至诚皎洁固不昧，时虽今古同乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495680'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_495680_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_495756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495756?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晚意</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495756")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495756_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495756'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495756'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_495756", 495756, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>晚色</span>微茫至，前山次第昏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495756'>羸牛归径远，宿鸟傍檐翻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495756'>盘喜黄粱熟，杯馀白酒浑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495756'>田家虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495756", 495756, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>澹薄</span>，犹得离尘喧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495756'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495756_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_495685' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495685' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495685?labeling=true' target='_blank'>老莱子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_495685'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495685'>常羡老莱子，七十亲不衰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495685'>飒然双白鬓，尚服五䌽衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495685'>戏游日膝下，弄物心熙熙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495685'>或时暂仆<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>跌，辄作婴儿啼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495685'>清朝万钟禄，不肯卖片时。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495685'>人生有此乐，何暇外慕为。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495685'>伊余生不造，才壮苍天亏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495685'>搏膺念之子，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_495685", 495685, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>叹咏</span>形诸诗。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495685'>想象且三复，苦血下交颐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495685'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_495685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495685'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_495685_0'>⑴ 原作自，据黄本、陈本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495685_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
蓝田
-----detail

id='poem_sentence_2_495748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495748'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495748", 495748, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>隐逸</span>何曾见，孤吟对古松。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495748'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游悟真寺而作。作品：蓝田悟真寺作。<div id='poem_495653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蓝田悟真寺作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495653")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495653'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495653'>旅食长安城，回遑奔走无停行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495653'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495653", 495653, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>清怀</span>壮抱失素尚<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作向，据黄本、陈本改）</span>，胸中堆积尘土生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495653'>偷閒得至玉峰下，为闻悟真之寺之嘉名。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495653'>杖邛赤脚渡蓝水，细流激激心骨清。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495653'>仰看苍山高峰旁，白云明灭藏日光。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495653'>行人遥指置寺处，正在白云之中央。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495653'>逡巡缘栈更险绝，攀萝扪壁随低昂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495653'>朋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>行咫尺乃相失，已与云雾相翱翔。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495653'>时闻啼鸟如吹竹，数步一休还纵目。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495653'>行行未知高则危，下视昏烟覆平陆。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495653'>满岩佳树尤朴樕，赫赤如霞间浓绿。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495653'>是时八月初，路旁已见芬芬菊。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495653'>贪奇恋景不知倦，侧睥又复心瑟缩。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495653'>神魂飞下大壑幽，定省移时进双足。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495653'>寺门高开朝日辉，丹青黯澹唐时屋。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495653'>老僧引我周游看，且云白氏子诗乃实录。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495653'>此诗畴昔予所闻，殷殷<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作勤）</span>更向碑前读。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495653'>按言索像今无复，惟有流泉数道如车辐。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495653'>我嫌世累欲暂居，又云此地无留宿。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495653'>殿宇之后林莽中，日暮尝有虎豹伏。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495653'>凿石龛边崖至深，近有浮屠于此相枨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>触。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495653'>悁<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>心<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_22_495653'>我闻为之久颦蹙，此向期将避烦辱。<div id='poem_sentence_22_495653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_495653'>不为伤生事<span gray;'>▪</span>往王顺山途中作。作品：往王顺山值暴雨雷霆。<div id='poem_495686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495686?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_495686'>苍崖六月阴气舒，一霔<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>淫雨如绳粗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495686'>霹雳飞出大壑底，烈火<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495686", 495686, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>黑雾</span>相奔趋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495686'>人皆喘汗抱树立，紫藤翠蔓皆焦枯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495686'>逡巡已在天中吼，有如上帝来追呼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495686'>震摇巨石当道落，惊嗥时闻虎与䝙。<div
