href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　有诗呈王景仁。作品：静胜堂夏日呈王尉。<div id='poem_495738' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495738' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495738?labeling=true' target='_blank'>静胜堂夏日呈王尉</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495738")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495738_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495738'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495738'>虚堂吏事稀，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_495738", 495738, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>吟卧</span>欲忘机。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495738'>窗静蜂迷出，帘轻燕误飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495738'>烦心倾晚簟，倦体快风衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495738'>更想<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495738", 495738, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>霜云</span>外，同君看翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495738'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495738_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　有诗。作品：己卯冬大寒有感。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年冬日。）</span><div id='poem_495659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己卯冬大寒有感</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495659")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495659'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495659'>延川未撤警，夕烽照冰雪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495659'>穷边苦寒地，兵气相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495659", 495659, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>躔结</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495659'>主将初临戎，猛思风前发。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495659'>朝笳吹馀哀，叠鼓暮不绝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495659'>淹留未见敌，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495659", 495659, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>愁端</span>密如发。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495659'>予闻古烈士，自誓立<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_495659", 495659, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>壮节</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495659'>丸泥封<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_495659", 495659, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>函关</span>，长缨系南越。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495659'>本为朝廷羞，宁计身命活。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495659'>功名非与期，册书岂磨灭。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495659'>然由在遇专，丑类易<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_495659", 495659, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>剪伐</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495659'>训士无他才，赏罚在果决。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495659'>近闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_495659", 495659, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>边方</span>奏，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_495659", 495659, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>中覆</span>多沈没。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495659'>罪者既稽诛，功者不见阅。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495659'>虽使颇牧生，勇智当坐竭。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495659'>或云庙堂上，与彼势<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_495659", 495659, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>相戛</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495659'>恐其立异勋，欻然自超拔。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495659'>不知百万师，寒刮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_495659", 495659, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>肤革</span>裂。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495659'>关中闲诛敛，农产半匮竭。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495659'>我欲叫上帝，愿帝下明罚。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495659'>早令黠虏亡，无为生民孽。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495659'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_495659_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　为刘文质作墓志铭。作品：內园使连州刺史知代州刘公墓志。<div id='poem_1164437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内园使连州刺史知代州刘公墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164437")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164437'>公讳文质，字士彬，世占数于保州保塞县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164437_comment'></div>曾祖延，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164437_comment'></div>祖昌，后唐为平州刺史，幽蓟垦田使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164437_comment'></div>保塞，皇家之故乡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164437_comment'></div>翼祖皇帝之在民间，昌阴知其非常，归以息女，今庙号简穆皇后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164437_comment'></div>父审奇，太祖创业之始，倚以机事，辟署汜水关令，未几卒，今赠左千牛卫大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164437_comment'></div>母张氏，封清河郡太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164437_comment'></div>夫人出入中闱，太宗尝以乡党之旧，赐予颇众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164437_comment'></div>一日，问其为后者，因以公名上之，即特召为供奉官，寄班祗候，入备宿卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164437_comment'></div>雅以清慎自持，上颇信向焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164437_comment'></div>每外廷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164437", 1164437, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>拜免</span>，必閒访之，公悉心谋论，辄中旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164437_comment'></div>时中人窦神福侍，上顾谓曰：「文质，朕之亲旧，言论有足嘉者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164437_comment'></div>因以白金百斤赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164437_comment'></div>至道初，将命二浙按察民事，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164437", 1164437, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>进黜</span>郡县吏数十人，立得报可，议者惬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164437_comment'></div>归，授左藏库副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164437_comment'></div>后以久任<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164437", 1164437, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>省闱</span>，上书愿效死<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164437", 1164437, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>边漠</span>，以报国宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164437_comment'></div>上从容谓曰：「陪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164437", 1164437, "Clauses/54/Comments/1")'>图议</span>于中，所报亦大，庸非其人哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164437_comment'></div>遂掩其奏不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164437_comment'></div>踰年，出为岢岚军使，俄改麟府兵马钤辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164437_comment'></div>戎人犯顺，兵宿塞下，前后俘馘甚众，获马畜铠甲之类，虑一万七千三百馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164437_comment'></div>凡赐金者三，诏奖者五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164437_comment'></div>咸平中，移知庆州，权董泾、原、仪、渭四郡之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164437_comment'></div>时西虏窃入我境，公蒐精甲兵百，以乘其锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164437_comment'></div>寮有碍诏缩忸，不时给军须者，公乃竭私缗二十万以均分之，士感慨增气，大破寇兵而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164437_comment'></div>是岁，充灵州清远军监兵，复与虏骑战于枝子平，逐之绝漠而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164437_comment'></div>玺书褒谕，有锦袍上金带之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164437_comment'></div>移典泾州，为帅臣杨琼之贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164437_comment'></div>寇陷清远，以逗衄谪南海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164437_comment'></div>遇恩放还，起为率府副率，总两浙诸州兵甲，移齐州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164437_comment'></div>封禅岱宗，命引兵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1164437", 1164437, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>逻护</span>岳下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164437_comment'></div>迁礼宾副使、石隰沿边都巡检使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164437_comment'></div>又换秦州兵马钤辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164437_comment'></div>公自负<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164437", 1164437, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>筑版</span>，率<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164437", 1164437, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>枭锐</span>士建小落门寨，开边远甚，诏书嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164437_comment'></div>移知代州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164437_comment'></div>境与胡近，我军之刍牧者，多为诱掠，返称亡命东还以徼赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164437_comment'></div>公原其情，为之上论，报得贳殊死者数百辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164437_comment'></div>转内园使、知代州，佐节度曹玮出环州界，筑保障十馀处，聚劲卒以压虏冲，迄今不敢犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164437_comment'></div>除使持节连州刺史，再知代郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164437_comment'></div>天圣六年正月十六日寝疾，终于位，享年六十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164437_comment'></div>赐赙甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164437_comment'></div>权厝于并之佛庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164437_comment'></div>公作牧训戎，更任者二十有四，乘传操命者又十二焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164437_comment'></div>出处必尽风力，著绩较他将为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164437_comment'></div>能以义断物，以惠役众，所赏赉不可胜计，辄施散，未尝理赀产，性忠鲠嫉邪，喜评刺，无所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1164437", 1164437, "Clauses/133/Comments/0")'>避诎</span>，当涂忌之，故官不大进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164437_comment'></div>章圣帝尝询及保塞之旧，因以简穆事上闻，又用宣祖、太祖赐书五函为献，有诏编在属籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164437_comment'></div>天禧中，章圣初不豫，公恳求赐对，进议数刻，大率以慎任帷幄之臣为意，帝深嗟赏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164437_comment'></div>今上在东宫，凡五以书赐，今藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164437_comment'></div>兄文裕，终容州观察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164437_comment'></div>夫人李氏，保顺军节度使溥之女，封陇西县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164437_comment'></div>生于公族，慎淑有仪，抚育诸子，嫡孽无异心，禀年不遐，没先于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164437_comment'></div>子十五人：长曰涓，早世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164437_comment'></div>曰湛，侍禁、閤门祗候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164437_comment'></div>曰涣，屯田员外郎、知辽州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164437_comment'></div>曰渭，苏州吴江县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164437_comment'></div>曰沪、淳、渊、浚，俱殿直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164437_comment'></div>曰汎、沿、漌，未仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164437_comment'></div>曰沐、泳、泌、源，皆早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164437_comment'></div>女八人：长适伊世昌，次适高日宣，次适田守德，次适李智宝，次适王宥，次适王丰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1164437_comment'></div>二皆夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1164437_comment'></div>屯田君高远有识度，尝上疏乞庄献后归政，由奉礼郎擢拜右正言，庆之所丛，为时闻人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1164437_comment'></div>今自辽阳拜章赐告之太原，扶护公之灵舆归京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1164437_comment'></div>以景祐五年八月某日，葬于雍丘县百家村之先域，举李夫人之榇合袝焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1164437_comment'></div>枉道出长垣，求志于舜钦，谨用笔以铭云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_1164437'>予尝观前史，见王者之兴，其乡党故人，有起耕贩而取将相，世十数不绝者，盖其遇之之异耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1164437_comment'></div>今公才且逢勋旧，较然不殊，而位弗大擢以殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1164437_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1164437_comment'></div>此古人所以委之于数也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1164437_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　有书上段少连。作品：上三司副使段公书。<div id='poem_1164383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164383?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上三司副使段公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164383")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164383_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164383'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164383'>某谓士之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>洁矩</span>厉行，施才业以拯世务者，非祇蹈道以为乐，上者觊声名，次者倖禄赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164383_comment'></div>至于饿寒其体肤，枯槁岩穴之内，犯刀兵，涂裂肝脑，僵于行陈者亦皆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164383_comment'></div>惟知道，所为不妄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164383_comment'></div>其有挺然立事，谢绝世婴，远举而不顾者，几希其人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164383_comment'></div>有诚高矣，亦乌足著为风教哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164383_comment'></div>故朝廷张爵位，君子以名称重轻而沮劝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164383_comment'></div>道行无状，一旦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>射合</span>时利而位可得也，名则逊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164383_comment'></div>盖名之发，惟精识者尸之，不私不隐，不以荣辱迁，为得符天下之正义，虽小人好恶淆其间，不能夺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164383_comment'></div>某何为者，辄有此论？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164383_comment'></div>窃自念幼喜读书，弄笔研，稍长则以无闻为耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164383_comment'></div>尝谓人之所以为人者，言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164383_comment'></div>言也者，必归于道义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164383_comment'></div>道与义，泽于物而后已，至是则斯为不朽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164383_comment'></div>故每属文，不敢雕琢以害正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164383_comment'></div>然而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>法章</span>民事，一未知其牙檗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164383_comment'></div>偶奏赋上前，得及第，命宰以蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164383_comment'></div>才两月，以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>家难</span>离官，下邑民遮道助嗥泣，又叹息有若惜其去者，念政无所及，心颇愧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164383_comment'></div>及幽居长安，百口饥饿，遂假贷苑东之田数顷，躬耕其间，故播敛之早晚，塍畔之出入，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>质契</span>之昏明，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>豪弱</span>之交侵，讼诉之搆，官司之辨，皆亲尝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164383_comment'></div>而又律令诏敕，奇情重复傅比之文无不遍见，虽条目繁滋，皆可类举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164383_comment'></div>静念及之，政必有悖于法不安于民者，居常恻然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164383_comment'></div>及终丧还都下，伯父至自东筦，首言道遇阁下，盛谭蒙邑之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164383_comment'></div>某荒忽自失，伏念阁下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>正峭</span>明察，重其许可，一言之赏，不可妄得，是必有所过听也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164383_comment'></div>尝能窜一巨豪，杖杀一黠吏，此外特庸庸所为耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164383_comment'></div>阁下不以善小弃之，特为置齿牙间，时尚或以谓操使权者，故当察其属之否臧而进退之，私心未甚德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164383_comment'></div>去年夏初，又得京兆司录孙甫所言如伯父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164383_comment'></div>时始至此邑，鄙怀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>耸然</span>，自谓今职在甸内，去京师不数舍，朝有施为而夕闻焉，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>上府</span>多士，如段公之乐道人善者故有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164383_comment'></div>况<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/100/Comments/0")'>法章</span>民政，稍贯于昔，益励精力以事事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164383_comment'></div>迄今踰年，吏民虽信，而当涂之称道蔑闻焉，而又符檄督责，终日憔悴，而救过不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164383_comment'></div>惘然自疑，何智于前而愚于此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164383_comment'></div>会太公弟至，云阁下前过邑，所论如甫书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164383_comment'></div>始闻之，如瞆者之决，得听钟鼓之奏，喜过感极，辄欲泣涕，以知大君子勤勤奖借终始之不懈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164383_comment'></div>李习之云：「知而不能誉，则如勿知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164383_comment'></div>誉而不能久，则如勿誉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164383_comment'></div>阁下既知而又誉之，誉而又久之，夫何幸哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164383_comment'></div>且世有获荐宠推延之赐者，必皆顺颜承辞，亲被<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1164383", 1164383, "Clauses/130/Comments/0")'>指役</span>，隆寒苦暑，趋走左右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164383_comment'></div>未有上下相绝，未尝一拜棱威，乃肯垂慈询察，因片善而称道，久而不渝者，此为难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164383_comment'></div>使某之名一落人耳，不至沈灭于时者，阁下之赐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164383_comment'></div>尔后即举世见毁，不足动怀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164383_comment'></div>尝欲特诣前以写此恳，为邑事所系，不得勇往，故凭文字以谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164383_comment'></div>檗积之抱，万不一宣，倾望恩德，颠沛于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164383_comment'></div>气律兼润，炎暑差早，伏望上为社庙善保兴居。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1164383_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　为父苏耆作墓志铭。作品：先公墓志铭并序。<div id='poem_1164434' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164434' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164434?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164434")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164434_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164434'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164434'>苏，邺之附城，昆吾受封而姓出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164434_comment'></div>其后周司寇忿生徙食河内，汉将军建起杜陵，武葬武功，世遂名其籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164434_comment'></div>隋唐之际多伟人，六叶之内，四至大丞相，袭封邳、许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164434_comment'></div>文宪公之曾孙传素，广明乱，以其孥逊蜀，生三子，捡、拯、振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164434_comment'></div>孟还相唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164434_comment'></div>仲以策擢，官至容管经略使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164434_comment'></div>唐命革，刘岩奄有南海，独完圉不与岩，容民于今祠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164434_comment'></div>季留为铜山令，即我先公之高祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164434_comment'></div>先公讳耆，字国老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164434_comment'></div>曾祖寓，剑州司马，夫人龚氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164434_comment'></div>大父协，中进士甲科，任陵州判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164434_comment'></div>孟氏朝京师，谪怀州司寇参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164434_comment'></div>雍熙中召对，授光禄寺丞，知开封府兵曹事，累赠刑部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164434_comment'></div>大王母薛氏，封河东郡太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164434_comment'></div>皇考易简，太平兴国中，首登进士第，才十年，遂参大政，赠太师、尚书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164434_comment'></div>母崔氏，封广平郡太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164434_comment'></div>公生七龄，以父任宣节校尉，左千牛备身，俄加振武副尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164434_comment'></div>踰年，大令薨，恩授通直郎、秘书省正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164434_comment'></div>未冠，谒文正王公旦，公器之，以息女归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164434_comment'></div>章圣帝即位，改奉礼郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164434_comment'></div>既冠，举进士，时试条至严，两中优等，廷校不得在高第，诎所素志，辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164434_comment'></div>后一年，以文奏御，诏试玉堂，赐及第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164434_comment'></div>东封，转大理评事，从祀汾阴，迁丞，赐绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164434_comment'></div>出知湖之乌程，以文正公当国，凡五载，未尝求代迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164434_comment'></div>时吴越大水，平泉行舟，既涸，农尽以失畔讼，公按籍收判质，悉履邑田书而揭之，狡豪宿隐，摘以给下户失职者，民乐兴颂，无复诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164434_comment'></div>群牧制置使陈公尧叟荐充判官，改殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164434_comment'></div>任终，知开封县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164434_comment'></div>既省政，恶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1164434", 1164434, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>民物</span>之薄，且多贵人善田宅，操势威、豪夺无告，一切以法绳之，皆帖帖俛首，不敢相干犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164434_comment'></div>因上书曰：「京师诸夏本根、宜为化首，今流风甚微，臣窃耻之，谨条七事以闻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164434_comment'></div>迁太常博士、三司户部判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164434_comment'></div>是岁，以谏议大夫充契丹国信使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164434_comment'></div>将行，太夫人寝疾，公露奏牢辞，未报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164434_comment'></div>夫人弃平居，廷议以名业北走，不可易，公哀恸感疾，还上信币，曰将死请，遂改命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164434_comment'></div>终丧，复除三司判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164434_comment'></div>明年，转尚书祠部员外郎、知明州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164434_comment'></div>郡有湖号广德，古钟水以溉旱，唐季坏漏不补，披为田，公复而浚之，防四百里，自是境无凶年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164434_comment'></div>郊庆，叙阶升朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164434_comment'></div>归朝，换度支，充长宁接伴使，既又判户部案，召入考进士第，复诏使契丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164434_comment'></div>初出疆，每舍必作诗，山漠之险易，水荐之美恶，备然尽在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164434_comment'></div>归而集上之，人争布诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164434_comment'></div>出为京西转运使，赐三品服，就改兵部，又加直集贤院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164434_comment'></div>踰年，移使河东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164434_comment'></div>两河荐丁旱蝗，所在艰食，公案行属部，不专计利，务以息民为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164434_comment'></div>汰冗兵，罢非业之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164434_comment'></div>代之庾陈，不能饲军，始廪者皆猖獗聚噪，欲扇为变有期矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164434_comment'></div>公遽往焉，列校先马首以诉，徐语之曰：「国之储非久，何以备凶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164434_comment'></div>若不食腐，将谁食之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164434_comment'></div>尔见殍尸枕藉道上，曾不得是而生耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164434_comment'></div>命拘而鞭之，以语钳其帅，卒不敢动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164434_comment'></div>迁工部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164434_comment'></div>籍田叙勋，至上柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164434_comment'></div>移使陕西，未几，洛守移来求粟赒其饥，公计调二十万斛输焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164434_comment'></div>寮不可，曰：「边宜实之，移中以自速困，非谋也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164434_comment'></div>公曰：「臣民系于君，无内外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164434_comment'></div>忍知其垂死亡，不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164434_comment'></div>以奇赢赈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164434_comment'></div>他日茍无馈，期不诿君」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164434_comment'></div>以是遂定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1164434_comment'></div>景祐二年正月十有二日得疾，药祷遍及而不逮，翌日夜漏下二刻终于位，春秋四十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1164434_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1164434_comment'></div>以先公之德之才，天资诚敏，而不遐其年，顿于中仕，利不布天下，使有志于时者，嗟痫而陨涕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1164434_comment'></div>孤舜元等恸踊泣血，扶卫我公之灵舆归上都，考龟筮得宝元二年十月二十七日之吉，葬于开封县宰辅乡中书村之先域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1164434_comment'></div>舜钦幼尝戏祖母之几下，闻语：公初能言，大令特爱之，始令诵诗，必自题之于果上，踰时占数十百篇，果终不食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1164434_comment'></div>八岁侍官穰下，据鞍吟咏，不废编而置于褚中，大令密取视之，骇其辞，致前抚首而命以名，又用是以字之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1164434_comment'></div>明年，罹大令丧，至性过人，号恸不绝声，行路为之哀伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1164434_comment'></div>公雅好观书，经史禅说，手钞者数千卷，无不尽诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1164434_comment'></div>所著《计录》三篇，《开谈录》五卷，《次翰林志》、《续文房四谱》、并文集二十卷，并藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1164434_comment'></div>公六居内外计，未尝建言聚敛，有语<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1164434", 1164434, "Clauses/244/Comments/0")'>逸利</span>者辄却之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1164434_comment'></div>襟度<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1164434", 1164434, "Clauses/245/Comments/0")'>轩辟</span>，不屑细务，处事若不施虑，其间无不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1164434", 1164434, "Clauses/248/Comments/0")'>妙当</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1164434_comment'></div>所至必尉荐才器，未始案吏，虽无状者，能使谨前无犯患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1164434_comment'></div>性钟孝友，丧太夫人，体形瘠枯，杖而后能兴，每临必绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1164434_comment'></div>以弟叟久没铨调，上书乞彻官予之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1164434_comment'></div>嫁三孤侄，匮所有，资送不足，又举倍息钱，必丰后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1164434_comment'></div>平居晏晏，以图史自愉，虽家无宿储，终不及资产事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1164434_comment'></div>兄寿，终水部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1164434_comment'></div>二弟：宿，终大理评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1164434_comment'></div>叟，终溧阳令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1164434_comment'></div>夫人雅尚惇素，不喜与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1164434", 1164434, "Clauses/277/Comments/0")'>游侈</span>者相从，专以孝承严姑，礼弼先公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1164434_comment'></div>二十有八岁，封太原县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1164434_comment'></div>明年召见，赐冠服，出入中掖，进谒有规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1164434_comment'></div>子舜元，大理寺丞，知开封府咸平县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1164434_comment'></div>舜钦，光禄主簿，知长垣县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1164434_comment'></div>舜宾，光禄主簿，知太康县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1164434_comment'></div>俱登进士第，得以艺升，不为家羞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1164434_comment'></div>盖积是训厉，使去怠傲而自进立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1164434_comment'></div>女三人：长适大理评事雍扶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1164434_comment'></div>次适太常寺太祝韩维；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1164434_comment'></div>次幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1164434_comment'></div>孙十人，渊、浑、注、泂，馀幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1164434_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1164434_comment'></div>昊天不吊，下此酷凶，尚宾宾徇礼经，以嗣祭为大，茍延喘息，不获躬执杖履，侍于九原，已至于今矣，忍复以鄙略不伦之词，上识宰壤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1164434_comment'></div>静念古人述先，或以为孝，况斯言不敢诬，传可后信，虽不足阐扬我先公之辉光，庶尽人子之志焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1164434_comment'></div>衔此巨创，缀之铭云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1164434'>世之望兮，于铄严考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1164434_comment'></div>清风再张兮，立于稚妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1164434_comment'></div>学根源兮不务剽，造次之言兮卒蟠于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1164434_comment'></div>擢节义以贯中兮，诚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_95_1164434", 1164434, "Clauses/333/Comments/0")'>精光</span>而外照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1164434_comment'></div>哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1164434_comment'></div>不隮高龄兮，神于何而能劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1164434_comment'></div>瘅诸孤兮，攀灵基而莫劭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1164434_comment'></div>号苍苍之高兮，曷余家之不造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1164434_comment'></div>心脍膈裂兮，血下涂于野草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1164434_comment'></div>冈隰外巩兮，浚渠旁绕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1164434_comment'></div>哀哀我公之灵兮，宁此佳兆。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_102_1164434'></div><div id='poem_sentence_102_1164434_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　为亡妻郑氏作墓志铭。作品：亡妻郑氏墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年秋。）</span><div id='poem_1164436' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164436' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164436?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亡妻郑氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164436")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164436_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164436'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164436'>苏舜钦之妻荥阳郑氏，其父屯田郎中讳希甫，母天水县君赵氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164436_comment'></div>生十四年而天水夫人殁，又三年父丧，又三年归于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164436_comment'></div>甲戌岁，予登第，授光禄主簿，知亳州蒙城，归宁长安，是年冬十月，堂帖促之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164436_comment'></div>一日，泣相语曰：「子其携三子以往，愿留以待姑嫜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164436_comment'></div>言寖布，家人皆谕之，曰：「凡仕无留孥，所以典闑中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164436_comment'></div>遂偕至官下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164436_comment'></div>才两月，皇天降祸，得先君之凶讣，即日衰绖与之西走，昼夜奔号，登顿失食寝节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164436_comment'></div>方妊，以马骇坠地者三，伤左股焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164436_comment'></div>起即强自支，不肯少休，曰：「早得一恸于舅之柩前，遂死无恨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164436_comment'></div>若或殒灭，重为姑忧，大甚为不孝也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164436_comment'></div>三月十三日至于家，是暮产一子，疾起所伤，七日而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164436_comment'></div>时景祐二年三月十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164436_comment'></div>哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164436_comment'></div>堂有寿母，室有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164436", 1164436, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>乳稚</span>，藉以奉育，遽失其助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164436_comment'></div>余时<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164436", 1164436, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>待尽</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164436", 1164436, "Clauses/50/Comments/1")'>苫次</span>，退而又哭于室中，亦血气者，非勉徇于礼，乌能胜而至是耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164436_comment'></div>间月，火其榇于万年栖凤原，缄骨归京师，以年月日从于先域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164436_comment'></div>子曰泌，一女幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164436_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1164436'>奄然不起，怛然此止<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164436_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1164436'>三月十六日：传本作「年二十六矣」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1164436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1164436'><span class='label'>沈校本案：</span>「据上文推算，十六当作二十。」<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_1164436_0'>⑴ 《苏学士文集》卷一四。又见光绪《潼川府志》卷三○，民国《中江县志》卷一九。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1164436_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　为叔苏叟作墓志铭。作品：江宁府溧阳令苏府君墓志铭并序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年秋。）</span><div id='poem_1164435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江宁府溧阳令苏府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164435")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164435_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164435'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164435'>季父讳叟，字蟠叟，先大令之少子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164435_comment'></div>免乳而大令薨，既冠犹褐衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164435_comment'></div>大中祥符初，授太庙斋郎，选岳州华容尉、阆州阆中主簿、陕府平陆令、杭州录事参军、江宁府溧阳令，所历未尝有过谪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164435_comment'></div>然数命少会，知己者辄死窜，不及荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164435_comment'></div>天圣末，先公任兵部员外郎，尝上书曰：「臣闻手足偏废，是谓笃疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164435_comment'></div>人生之苦，莫此为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164435_comment'></div>臣有隐痛，顾切如之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164435_comment'></div>天高听卑，伏暨垂闵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164435_comment'></div>臣先父早以才业擢列近辅，未及强仕，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164435", 1164435, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>奄沦</span>盛朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164435_comment'></div>尝有治命，不令以遗札任子，故臣之弟叟，冠为白丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164435_comment'></div>祥符行庆，始补太庙斋郎，自尔效官，十有三考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164435_comment'></div>蹉跌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164435", 1164435, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>颜发</span>，泪嗢寒饿，贱位所束，自拔无由，每一疚中，如伏沈瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164435_comment'></div>臣今幸以年绩例当改秩，欲乞以所奉新恩，回授叟一京官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164435_comment'></div>伏望天皇厚德，哀闵此怀」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164435_comment'></div>以例格遂罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164435_comment'></div>溧阳任终，贫不能族归，寓家京口；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164435_comment'></div>入选得疾，力判试，不如格，不得调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164435_comment'></div>气益失卫，结涩乘于胸，胃不防饮，滥于肤络之下，血化而并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164435_comment'></div>既亟，舟沿还家而终，享年四十五，时景祐四年七月十日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164435_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164435_comment'></div>本朝执政子未有在铨调者，又何独<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1164435", 1164435, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>湮塞</span>若是之久耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164435_comment'></div>世皆悲怜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164435_comment'></div>季父亦不甚痛，尝语人曰：「天地气数，差变不可一，其间才而厄于无津，则无可为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164435_comment'></div>每出门，逢者十人，八九不吾过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164435_comment'></div>一二愈者，乌足动哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164435_comment'></div>故常放意杯酒，不喜间关于进取之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164435_comment'></div>娶周、吴、张三夫人，皆无子，女嫁阳翟主簿杨组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164435_comment'></div>以宝元二年十月二十七日，归葬开封县宰辅乡凤池原先祖兆下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164435_comment'></div>铭云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1164435'>神之司，祸福是宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164435_comment'></div>吾先力善，季父何奇！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164435_comment'></div>仆于贱仕，虽世之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164435_comment'></div>嗣覆而夭，岂神宜为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164435_comment'></div>周号而冥，其谁赖之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164435_comment'></div>噫吁已而，柰何乎哀思！</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1164435_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
镇江

class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495669' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495669?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨子江观风浪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495669_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495669'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495669'>晚至瓜州渡，击舟泊西湾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495669'>日落暴风起，大浪得纵观。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495669'>凭凌积石岸，吐吞天外山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495669'>霹雳左右作，雪洒六月寒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495669'>吁嗟至柔物，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495669", 495669, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>威壮</span>不可干。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495669'>若为神龙凭，气势非一端。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495669'>大舰失所操，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_495669", 495669, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>翻覆</span>如转丸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495669'>高山虽有路，辙险马足酸。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495669'>居朝号安逸，重禄多忧患。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495669'>争得清静交，共骑双翔鸾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495669'>矫翅入赤霄，不见此险难。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495669'>奈何蚩蚩众，共处天壤间。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495669'>因知古圣人，立法万世安。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495669'>济川作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_495669", 495669, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>舟梁</span>，铸鼎穷神奸。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495669'>朝廷布礼度，粲粲莫可删。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495669'>后来渐破坏，所向行路难。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495669'>凶邪得骋志，物命遭摧残。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495669'>视此念古昔，杖藜空盘桓。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495669'></div><div DetailSwitch("08b77acfc74c4967ac82eb93ffbf87e3");'><span id='08b77acfc74c4967ac82eb93ffbf87e3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>，38岁</div><div id='08b77acfc74c4967ac82eb93ffbf87e3' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，往游润州，有诗。作品：晚出润州东门。<div id='poem_495764' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495764' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495764?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晚出润州东门</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495764")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495764_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495764'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495764'>京口古<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_495764", 495764, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>雄处</span>，昔年尝此过。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495764'>风流看石兽，人事共江波。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495764'>河转路疑尽，日斜山更多。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495764'>城楼郁天半，回首恣吟哦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495764'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495764_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游润州，有诗。作品：游招隐道中。题花山寺壁。金山寺。<div id='poem_495815' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495815' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495815?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_495815'>扬鞭望招隐，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_495815", 495815, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>尘思</span>漠然收。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495815'>云接青林合，泉兼碧草流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495815'>疏钟传别壑，晚日动前楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495815'>嘉遁平生志，吁嗟得暂游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495719'>阴壑滀风云，阳厓产金碧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495719'>离披万年树，根抱太古石。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495719'>修廊围峻阁，窈窕压山脊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495719'>偃蹇互出没，日此饱馀食。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495719'>又有翠羽禽，群飞喜宾客。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495719'>口衔绀蒂花，近我若相识。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495719'>开轩心旷绝，上下无异色。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495719'>予心本<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_495719", 495719, 扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d808735f8fde471f91cb6ef819c72f67_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d808735f8fde471f91cb6ef819c72f67");'><span id='d808735f8fde471f91cb6ef819c72f67_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，34岁</div><div id='d808735f8fde471f91cb6ef819c72f67' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　南下奔母丧，途中有诗。作品：扬州城南延宾亭。<div id='poem_495816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495816?labeling=true' target='_blank'>扬州城南延宾亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495816")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495816'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495816'>乱蝉咽咽柳霏霏，独上危亭俯落晖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495816'>江外山从林下见，城中人向渡头归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495816'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495816", 495816, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>风烟</span>远近思高遁，豺虎纵横难息机。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495816'>出处两乖空自挠，伤哉吾道欲何依。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495816'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495816_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2c349ddb7aeb45b190d5d868a7a505dc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2c349ddb7aeb45b190d5d868a7a505dc");'><span id='2c349ddb7aeb45b190d5d868a7a505dc_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>南下奔母丧，途中有诗。作品：过苏州。中秋夜吴江亭上对月怀前宰张子野及寄君谟蔡大。<div id='poem_137867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_137867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_137867")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_137867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_137867'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_137867'>东出盘门刮眼明，萧萧疏雨更阴晴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_137867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_137867'>绿杨白鹭俱自得，近水远山皆有情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_137867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_137867'>万物盛衰天意在，一身<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_3_137867'>无穷好景无缘住，旅棹区区暮亦行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_137867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_137867'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_137867_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_137871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_137871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/137871?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_137871'>独坐对月心悠悠，故人不见使我愁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_137871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_137871'>古今共传惜今夕，况在松江亭上头。<div id='poem_sentence_1_137871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_137871'>可怜节物会人意，十日阴雨此夜收。<div id='poem_sentence_2_137871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_137871'>不惟人间重此月，天亦有意于中秋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_137871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_137871'>长空无瑕露表里，拂拂渐渐<span id='poem_sentence_5_137871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_137871'>自视直欲见筋脉，无所逃遁鱼龙忧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_137871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_137871'>不疑身世在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_137871", 137871, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>地上</span>，祗恐槎去触斗牛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_137871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_137871'>景清境胜返不足，叹息此际无交游。<div id='poem_sentence_8_137871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_137871'>心魂冷烈晓不寝，勉为笔此传中州。<div id='poem_sentence_9_137871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_137871'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　在苏州会见刘公尤，因有此作。作品：邂逅刘公尤于平望之西联舟夜语走笔叙意。<div id='poem_495835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邂逅刘公尤于平望之西联舟夜语走笔叙意</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495835")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495835'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495835'>昔别蘋初生，离讴发清商。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495835'>契阔几何时，遗啭犹在梁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495835'>我亦宦游者，吴会非我乡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495835'>三考一瞬息，扁舟引徜徉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495835'>邂逅通夕语，弭棹水中央。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495835'>淡景月照户，遥音雁南翔。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495835'>摅意良未尽，讵及罗酒浆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_495835'><span class='label'>按：</span>同上书卷四九<br /></div><div id='poem_note_495835_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c1888395e14f43d78f7dbc86f4c09c44_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>，38岁</div><div id='c1888395e14f43d78f7dbc86f4c09c44' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>到达苏州与陆经、关永言游山。<div id='poem_495714' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495714' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495714?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495714")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495714_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495714'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495714'>上春游南峰，出<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>自阊扉西。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495714'>崎岖缘田塍，时又涉狭溪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495714'>午初至峰下，先读烂古碑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495714'>僧庐颇新鲜，丹青见<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>朝曦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495714'>云昔支公居，石迹有马蹄。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495714'>踰岭到天平，上观石屋危。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495714'>苍壁泻白泉，对之已忘疲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495714'>西岩列窗户，玲珑漏斜晖。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495714'>嵌<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作嵚）</span>然似饾饤，人力安可施。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495714'>朝餐下木渎，市物俗所宜。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495714'>琴台昔尝游，回首忆旧题。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495714'>南向又渡岭，盘屈麋鹿蹊。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495714'>摺身趋宝华，未到闻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>法鼙。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495714'>松间见广路，平如隐金锤。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495714'>寺压两山脚，三面张屏帏。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495714'>夜阑宿虚堂，清甚无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_495714", 495714, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>梦思</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495714'>西南<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>登尧峰，俗云尧所基。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495714'>洪川不能没，上有万众栖。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495714'>中道舍篮舆，从者亦汗衣。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495714'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_495714", 495714, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>关陆</span>巧步趋，健马莫可追。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495714'>自伤干躯大，两股酸不随。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495714'>岩雨洒磴滑，惟赖枯筇支<span class='inlineComment2'>（钱校：《吴都文粹》作支）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_21_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_495714'>四顾物象殊，虽困强自持。<div id='poem_sentence_22_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_495714'>竹木互<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_495714", 495714, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>支撑</span>，小阁架险梯。<div id='poem_sentence_23_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_495714'>凌晨过横山，蹴蹋云霞低。<div id='poem_sentence_24_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_495714'>身如插翅翼，下见<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_26_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_495714'>童童或行列<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>，春发绿<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_28_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_495714'>右顾万顷湖，东与天相迷。<div id='poem_sentence_29_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_495714'>日炙白烟开，风驱银山移。<div id='poem_sentence_30_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_495714'>旁过折腰塔，铁轮尽颠堕<span id='poem_sentence_32_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_495714'>未知天之意，摧此将何为。<div id='poem_sentence_33_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_495714'>迤逦瞰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑻</sup>荐福，爱此路侧池。<div id='poem_sentence_34_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_495714'>北渡千丈桥，柱袅阑倾敧。<div id='poem_sentence_38_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_495714'>子履<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑾</sup>阅奇怪，瞪视<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑿</sup>惟嗟咨。<div id='poem_sentence_42_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_495714'>及还城中居，城人殊未知。<div id='poem_sentence_43_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_495714'>自疑身被留，暂此梦寐归。<div id='poem_sentence_48_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_495714'>清泉与白云，终老得自怡。<div id='poem_sentence_49_495714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_495701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天平山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495701")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495701'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495701'>吴会括众山，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_495701", 495701, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>戢戢</span>不可数。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495701'>其间号天平，突兀为之主。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495701'>杰然镇西南，群岭争拱辅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495701'>吾知造物意，必以屏大<span class='inlineComment2'>（钱校本作天）</span>府。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495701'>清溪至其下，仰视势飞舞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495701'>伟石如长人，坚立欲言语。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495701'>扪萝缘险磴，烂漫松竹古。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495701'>中腰有危亭，前对绀壁举。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495701'>石窦落<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作迸）</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_495701", 495701, "Clauses/16/Comments/1")'>玉泉</span>，泠泠四时雨。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495701'>源生白云间，颜色若粉乳。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495701'>旱年或播洒，润可足九土。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495701'>奈何但泓澄，未为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_495701", 495701, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>应龙</span>取。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495701'>予方弃尘中，岩壑素自许。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495701'>盘桓择<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_495701", 495701, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>雄胜</span>，至此快心膂。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 末二句钱校作养内聊自清，终胜甘于虎</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495701_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>有诗。作品：夏热昼寝感詠。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年夏。）</span><div id='poem_495710' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495710' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495710?labeling=true' "poem_title_495710")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495710_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495710'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495710'>盛夏日苦永，解带坐小轩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495710'>对案不能食，挥汗白雨翻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495710'>轧轧过午景，宛转无由昏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495710'>偃卧一榻上，既觉复梦魂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495710'>恬然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495710", 495710, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>世虑</span>寂，时被苍蝇喧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495710'>睡味胜仙去，忽恍难具<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>论。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495710'>晨事如隔日，半杂梦寐言。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495710'>人生贵壮健，及时取荣尊。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495710'>夏禹惜寸阴，穷治万水源。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495710'>栉沐风雨中，子哭不入门。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495710'>况复庸下者，不出强趋奔。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495710'>奈何耽昼寝，懒惰守坏垣。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495710'>念昔年少时，奋迅期孤骞。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495710'>笔下驱古风，直趣圣所存。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495710'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_495710", 495710, id='poem_sentence_15_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495710'>文章竟误身，大议谁周爰。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495710'>法吏使除籍，其过祗一飧。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495710'>宾朋四散逐，投窜向僻藩。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495710'>九虎口牙恶，便欲膏其蹯。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495710'>上赖天子明，不使钳且髡。<div id='poem_sentence_21_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_495710'>此身自流浪，岂能济元元。<div id='poem_sentence_22_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_495710'>天下无所归，泛舟旅江村。<div id='poem_sentence_23_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_495710'>春雨看秧稻，落日自灌园。<div id='poem_sentence_24_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_495710'>閒困尚有待，不忍沈湘沅。<div id='poem_sentence_27_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_495710'>大暑昼闭户，一径恶草繁。<div id='poem_sentence_28_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_495710'>出嫌乌啅噪，行见蛇蜿蜒。<div id='poem_sentence_29_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_495710'>蠹书徒盈箧，浊醪徒盈樽。<div id='poem_sentence_30_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_495710'>谈笑谁可共，道义孰与敦。<div id='poem_sentence_31_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_495710'>终日对稚立<span "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>肃爽</span>，朝政不复浑。<div id='poem_sentence_40_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_495710'>万物宇宙间，共被阳和恩。<div id='poem_sentence_41_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_495710'></div><div id='poem_sentence_42_495710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495710'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_495710_0'>⑴ 原作贶难俱，据黄本、陈本、李本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495710_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>陆经离苏州赴袁州时，舜钦有诗送别。作品：送子履。<div id='poem_495790' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495790' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495790?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送子履</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495790")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495790_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495790'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495790'>一舸风前五两飞，南迁今去别慈闱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495790_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495790'>人生多难古如此，吾道能全世所稀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495790_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495790'>幸有江山聊助思，莫随鱼鸟便忘归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495790_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495790'>君亲恩大须营报，学取三春寸草微。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495790_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495790'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495790_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2bad554535cd422796128587e54b80c3_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>，38岁</div><div id='2bad554535cd422796128587e54b80c3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年8月</a>　有诗酬李绚。作品：奉酬公素学士见招之作。<div id='poem_495702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉酬公素学士见招之作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495702")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495702'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495702'>人生交分耻苟合，贵以道义久可要。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495702'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495702", 495702, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>薄俗</span>盈虚逐势利，清风绵邈日已凋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495702'>长吟宇宙独引领，浩浩万古与我遥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495702'>安得此身有两翅，飒然远举随<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495702", 495702, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>风飙</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495702'>近逢公素我同好，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495702", 495702, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>厌愤</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495702", 495702, "Clauses/9/Comments/1")'>偷俗</span>常郁陶。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495702'>君方调<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作谪）</span>官镇京口，我以重罪废本朝。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495702'>身虽俱在大江外，不得会合烦相邀。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495702'>秋风八月天地肃，千里明回<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作迥）</span>草木焦。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495702'>夕霜惨烈气节劲，激起<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_495702", 495702, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>壮思</span>冲斗杓。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495702'>岂如儿女但悲感，唧唧<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_495702", 495702, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>吟叹</span>随螳蜩。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495702'>拟攀飞云抱明月，欲踏海门观怒涛。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495702'>念君治<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>所近不远，江山<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_495702", 495702, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>蟠辟</span>气象豪。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495702'>楼<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>头阴明变霞雾，槛下日夕斗蜃蛟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495702'>便将一往刷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_495702", 495702, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>滞闷</span>，去兴草茁不可薅<span class='inlineComment2'>（原缺，据李本补）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495702'>呼儿襆衣办舟楫，一日百里岂惮劳。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495702'>君方酒酣亦思我，奔墨纸上为长谣。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495702'>上言风物丽复壮，下述宴集乐且遨。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495702'>意我羁愁正无赖，欲以此事相誇招。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495702'>此篇笔绝墨未渗，我舟适到范老桥。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495702'>古人千里有神会，以兹可信非相辽。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495702'>倜然不以穷见弃，旷然不以位自骄。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495702'>开缄朗咏毛发竦，通夕噤痒<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>睫不交。<div id='poem_sentence_21_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_495702'>病膜谁将宝篦刮，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_495702", 495702, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>痒背</span>恰得仙人抓。<div id='poem_sentence_22_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_495702'>长川奔浑走一气，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_495702", 495702, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>巨镇</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_495702", 495702, "Clauses/47/Comments/1")'>截嶭</span>上赤霄。<div id='poem_sentence_23_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_495702'>又如阴云载雷电，光怪迸漏不可包。<div id='poem_sentence_24_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_495702'>惊呼叹伏已不暇，焉敢有意急其高。<div id='poem_sentence_25_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_495702'>却疑欺我老困顿，故作大句来相鏖。<div id='poem_sentence_26_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_495702'>近罹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_495702", 495702, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>罪辱</span>舌虽在，每避嫌谤口已胶。<div id='poem_sentence_27_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_495702'>更遭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_495702", 495702, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>掀搅</span>岂不畏，欲取笔砚俱焚烧。<div id='poem_sentence_28_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_495702'>既承嘉命敢无报，将吐复茹移昏朝。<div id='poem_sentence_29_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_495702'>留连日日奉杯宴，殊无閒隙吟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_495702", 495702, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>风骚</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_30_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_495702'>看君岸帻卷大白，有似巨浸吸百潮。<div id='poem_sentence_31_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_495702'>宾从<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_495702", 495702, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>倾颓</span>尚未厌，直恐溃烂肠与脬。<div id='poem_sentence_32_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_495702'>神迷耳热眼生缬，嚼尽宝墨狂酲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>消。<div id='poem_sentence_33_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_495702'>欢流乐极古所戒，不免厌旦潜遁逃。<div id='poem_sentence_34_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_495702'>还家数日却愁寂，梦中犹奉笑与嘲。<div id='poem_sentence_35_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_495702'>强为短篇答高谊，鄙事<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_495702", 495702, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>轧轧</span>空自挠。<div id='poem_sentence_36_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_495702'>览之捧腹定绝倒，幸为投弃无传抄。<div id='poem_sentence_37_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_495702'>相思复拟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>往相会，予今岂复如系匏。<div id='poem_sentence_38_495702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_495702'>行看雪夜景清绝，更乘逸兴飞轻舠。<div id='poem_sentence_38_495702_0'>⑸ 原作思，据李本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495702_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　有诗和李绚。作品：和丹阳公素学士晚望见怀。<div id='poem_495789' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495789' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495789?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和丹阳公素学士晚望见怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495789")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495789_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495789'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495789'>古郡登临足胜游，使君才调更风流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495789'>过云送雨海山暗，斜日催蝉江树秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495789'>屡辱嘉招嗟放弃，又传新咏慰淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495789'>霜天乘兴当西谒，共醉城尖四望楼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495789'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495789_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f4d81a1fc5dc4269958a68475925de6c_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1046')">1045-1046年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='f4d81a1fc5dc4269958a68475925de6c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　有诗。作品：独酌。迁居。<div id='poem_495837' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495837' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495837?labeling=true' target='_blank'>独酌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495837")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495837_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495837'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495837'>一酌浇肠俗虑奔，鴳微鹍大岂堪论。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495837_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495837'>楚灵当日能知此，肯入沧江作旅魂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495837_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495837'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495837_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495837'><span class='label'>按：</span>宋费衮《梁溪漫志》卷八<br /></div><div id='poem_note_495837_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_495703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迁居</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495703")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495703'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495703'>前岁旅淮楚，去年还上都。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495703'>上都一岁内，前后七徙居。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495703'>岁暮被重谪，狼狈来中吴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495703'>中吴未半岁，三次迁里闾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495703'>京师重<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495703", 495703, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>腾移</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495703", 495703, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>长物</span>动数车。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495703'>江湖亦稍便，一舟乐有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495703'>破坏新器皿，散亡旧图书。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495703'>家人颇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_495703", 495703, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>倦烦</span>，行路亦叹呼。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495703'>吾知人之生，天壤乃蘧庐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495703'>其间暂寄寓，一世还须臾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495703'>纵游极南北，所历足自娱。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495703'>犹恨苦濡滞，带动摧妻孥。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495703'>安得<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>出八<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>极，浩与元气俱。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495703'>仰首羡日月，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_495703", 495703, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>晨夕</span>苦奔趋。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495703'>二物本无情，亦为气所驱。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495703'>况我有血肉，又生名利区。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495703'>手足日不闲，在地无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_495703", 495703, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>根株</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495703'>流宕固宜矣，何必厌道涂。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495703'>此身亦外物，安用伤羁孤。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
