ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　有信答韩维。作品：答韩持国书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年夏秋间。）</span><div id='poem_1164390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答韩持国书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164390")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164390'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164390'>近得京信，长姊奄逝，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>中怀</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>殒裂</span>，不堪其哀，更承慰问，重增号绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164390_comment'></div>且蒙见责，以兄弟在京师，不以义相就，以尽友悌之道，独羁外数千里，自取愁苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164390_comment'></div>持国，予之素所畏者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164390_comment'></div>今言如是，疑非出于持国也，然笔迹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>趣尚</span>皆持国，又不足疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164390_comment'></div>是持国知其一，未知其他，予不得不为持国班班而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164390_comment'></div>予亦人也，非翼而飞、蹄而驰者也，岂无亲戚之情，岂不知会合之乐也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164390_comment'></div>虽是禽兽，亦安肯舍安逸而就愁苦哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164390_comment'></div>此语去离物情远矣，岂当出于持国之口邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164390_comment'></div>昨在京师官时，不敢犯人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>颜色</span>，不敢议论时事，随众上下，心志<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>蟠屈</span>不开，固亦极矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164390_comment'></div>不幸适在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>疑嫌</span>之地，不能决然早自引去，致不测之祸，捽去下吏，无人敢言，友雠一波，共起谤议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164390_comment'></div>被废之后，喧然未已，更欲寘之死地然后为快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164390_comment'></div>来者往往钩赜言语，欲以传播，好意相存恤者几希矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164390_comment'></div>故闭户或密出，不敢与相见，如避<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>兵寇</span>，惴惴然惟恐累及亲戚耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164390_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>偷俗</span>如此，安可久居其间？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164390_comment'></div>遂超然远举，羁泊于江湖之上，不惟衣食之累，实亦少避其机阱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164390_comment'></div>况血属之多，持国见之矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164390_comment'></div>屋庐之隘，持国亦见之矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164390_comment'></div>资入之薄，持国又见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164390_comment'></div>常相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>团聚</span>，不衣与食可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164390_comment'></div>不可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164390_comment'></div>衣食虽足，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>闭关</span>常不与人相接可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164390_comment'></div>亦不可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164390_comment'></div>既与人接，不与之言可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164390_comment'></div>又不可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164390_comment'></div>既与之言，不与之往还可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164390_comment'></div>又不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164390_comment'></div>既与之言语往还，人人皆如持国则可，今持国尚有此说，况亲也义也识也不迨持国者多矣，使之加酿恶言，喧布上下，不能自明，则前日之事，未为重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164390_comment'></div>便都无此事，亦终日劳苦，应接之不暇，寒暑奔走尘土泥淖中，不能了人事，羸马敝仆，日栖栖取辱于都城，使人指背<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>讥笑</span>哀悯，我亦何颜面，安得不谓之愁苦哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164390_comment'></div>此虽与兄弟亲戚相远，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/96/Comments/0")'>伏腊</span>稍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/96/Comments/1")'>充足</span>，居室稍宽，又无终日应接奔走之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164390_comment'></div>耳目<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>清旷</span>，不设机关以待人，心安閒而体舒放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164390_comment'></div>三商而眠，高舂而起，静院明窗之下，罗列图史琴尊以自愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164390_comment'></div>踰月不迹公门，有兴则泛小舟出盘、阊二门，吟啸览古于江山之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164390_comment'></div>渚茶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>野酿</span>，足以消忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164390_comment'></div>莼鲈稻蟹，足以适口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164390_comment'></div>又多高僧隐君子，佛庙胜绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164390_comment'></div>家有园林，珍花奇石，曲池高台，鱼鸟留连，不觉日暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164390_comment'></div>昔孔子作《春秋》而夷吴，又曰：「吾欲居九夷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164390_comment'></div>观今之风俗，乐善好事，知予守道好学，皆欣然愿来过从，不以罪人相遇，虽孔子复生，是亦必欲居此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164390_comment'></div>则持国以彼此较之，孰为愁苦哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164390_comment'></div>人生内有自得，外有所适，故亦乐矣，何必<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>高位厚禄</span>，役人以自奉养，然后为乐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164390_comment'></div>今虽侨此，亦如仕官南北，安可与亲戚常相守邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164390_comment'></div>持国明年终丧，昆仲亦必游宦，何以尽友悌之道也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164390_comment'></div>况予窘迫，势不得如持国之意，必使我尸转沟洫，肉喂豺虎而后可也，何其忍邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164390_comment'></div>常观《棠棣》之诗云：「凡今之人，莫如兄弟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164390_comment'></div>谓兄弟以恩，当有急难之时，必相拯救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164390_comment'></div>后章云：「丧乱既平，既安且宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164390_comment'></div>虽有兄弟，不如友生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164390_comment'></div>谓友朋尚义，及安宁之时，以礼义相琢磨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164390_comment'></div>予于持国，外兄弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164390_comment'></div>当急难之时，不相拯救，今又于安宁之际，欲以义相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1164390", 1164390, "Clauses/168/Comments/0")'>琢刻</span>，虽古人所不能受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164390_comment'></div>予欲不报，虑浅吾持国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164390_comment'></div>前得子华诗，意亦然，未暇缕述，今并此以达子华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164390_comment'></div>予非躁而忉，咄者察之！</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1164390'></div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1164390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　有信答范仲淹。作品：答范资政书。<div id='poem_1164392' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164392' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164392?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答范资政书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164392")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164392_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164392'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164392'>道远且阻，不得上记以候起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164392_comment'></div>家兄封到闰月所赐手教一通，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164392", 1164392, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>训爱</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164392", 1164392, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>切至</span>，情义并隆，怀感益深，不可言喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164392_comment'></div>某昨得罪后，都下沸腾未已，其谤皆出人情之外，而往往信而传之，自念非远引深潜，则不能快雠者之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164392_comment'></div>又以世居京师，坟墓亲戚所在，四方茫然无所归，始者意亦重去，不得已遂沿南河，且来吴中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164392_comment'></div>既至，则有江山之胜，稻蟹之美，衮州有租田数顷，郡中假回车院以居之，亲友分俸，伏腊似可给，岂敢更求赢馀，以足所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164392_comment'></div>日甚閒旷，得以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164392", 1164392, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>纵观</span>书策，及往时著述有未备者，皆得缀缉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164392_comment'></div>治《易》颇有所得，时苦奥处无人商论，乃知君子理身格物之道，自有本也，险难以萌而不之见，宜其悔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164392_comment'></div>况某性疏且拙，疏则多触<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164392", 1164392, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>时忌</span>，不能防闲小人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164392_comment'></div>拙则临事不敏，无所施为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164392_comment'></div>因此遂得退藏，盖亦自幸，茍致之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164392", 1164392, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>剧地</span>，责其功绩，徒自劳困，而无补于时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164392_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164392", 1164392, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>衣食</span>之分，祇此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164392_comment'></div>今得心<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164392", 1164392, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>安舒</span>而身逸豫，坐探圣人之道，又无人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164392", 1164392, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>讥察</span>而责望之，何乐如是！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164392_comment'></div>摄生事素亦留意，今起居饮食皆自适，内无营而外无劳，斯庄生所谓遁天之刑者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164392_comment'></div>岁馀来能饮冷而少病，此其效欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164392_comment'></div>某既废于世，本当于江湖之上，与鱼鸟麋鹿同乐，不欲使声问踪迹，一至于人间，因阁下之教，丁宁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164392", 1164392, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>委折</span>，不得不具道所怀，幸闵察焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1164392_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　有记。作品：沧浪亭记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年秋亭成后。）</span><div id='poem_1164424' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164424' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164424?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沧浪亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164424")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164424_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164424'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164424'>予以罪废无所归，扁舟南游，旅于吴中，始僦舍以处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164424_comment'></div>时盛夏蒸燠，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164424", 1164424, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>土居</span>皆褊狭，不能出气，思得高爽虚辟之地，以舒所怀，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164424_comment'></div>一日过郡学，东顾草树郁然，崇阜广水，不类乎城中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164424_comment'></div>并水得微径于杂花修竹之间，东趋数百步，有弃地，纵广合五六十寻，三向皆水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164424_comment'></div>杠之南，其地益阔，旁无民居，左右皆林木相亏蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164424_comment'></div>访诸旧老，云钱氏有国，近戚孙承佑之池馆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164424_comment'></div>坳隆胜势，遗意尚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164424_comment'></div>予爱而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164424", 1164424, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>徘徊</span>，遂以钱四万得之，构亭北埼，号沧浪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164424_comment'></div>前竹后水，水之阳又竹，无穷极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164424_comment'></div>澄川翠干，光影会合于轩户之间，尤与风月为相宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164424_comment'></div>予时榜小舟，幅巾以往，至则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164424", 1164424, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>洒然</span>忘其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164424_comment'></div>觞而浩歌，踞而仰啸，野老不至，鱼鸟共乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164424_comment'></div>形骸既适则神不烦，观听无邪则道以明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164424_comment'></div>返思向之汩汩荣辱之场，日与锱铢利害相磨戛，隔此真趣，不亦鄙哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164424_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164424_comment'></div>人固动物耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164424_comment'></div>情横于内而性伏，必外寓于物而后遣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164424_comment'></div>寓久则溺，以为当然，非胜是而易之，则悲而不开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164424_comment'></div>惟仕宦溺人为至深，古之才哲君子，有一失而至于死者多矣，是未知所以自胜之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164424_comment'></div>予既废而获斯境，安于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1164424", 1164424, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>冲旷</span>，不与众驱，因之复能见乎内外失得之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164424_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1164424", 1164424, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>沃然</span>有得，笑闵万古，尚未能忘其所寓目，用是以为胜焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1164424_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　有文祭王雍。作品：祭舅氏文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年9月。）</span>两浙路转运使司封郎中王公墓表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年秋。）</span><div id='poem_1164449' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164449' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164449?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭舅氏文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164449")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164449_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164449'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164449'>维年月日，甥苏某，谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于大舅按察郎中之灵：某放废于朝，旅泊胥台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164449_comment'></div>殊乡寡知，动成嫌猜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164449_comment'></div>始未踰月，舅以漕来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164449_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164449", 1164449, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>连牵</span>巨艘，旆旌徘徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164449_comment'></div>拜舅官亭，羁颜一开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164449_comment'></div>语言煦煦，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164449", 1164449, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>闵慰</span>兼该。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164449_comment'></div>处以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164449", 1164449, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>行署</span>，拔于荆柴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164449_comment'></div>异俗改眼，驩然相陪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164449_comment'></div>曾不两月，遘兹凶灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164449_comment'></div>讣闻始至，肝心裂摧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164449_comment'></div>百感恻恻，淋漓泪腮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164449_comment'></div>慈帏之掩，再更律灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164449_comment'></div>触事殒绝，不能彊排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164449_comment'></div>惟吾舅亲，他亲莫偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164449_comment'></div>如母之存，实慰此怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164449_comment'></div>不意忽奄，孤心顿乖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164449_comment'></div>相阀令器，朝家淑才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164449_comment'></div>不登年龄，岂天所差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164449_comment'></div>执纤西送，长江之隈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164449_comment'></div>丹旐的的，素帆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1164449", 1164449, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>皠皠</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164449_comment'></div>死生隔绝，今又独回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164449_comment'></div>致此薄奠，庶将告哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164449_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1164449_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1164445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164445?labeling=true' target='_blank'>两浙路转运使司封郎中王公墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164445")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164445'>公讳雍，字子肃，世为魏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164445_comment'></div>自烈祖祐历职中禁，始有第京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164445_comment'></div>太尉文正魏国公遭时奋庸，相章圣皇帝，著在国史，此不复书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164445_comment'></div>公即文正公之长子，幼而惇懿，不妄言笑，以文正公任为秘书省校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164445_comment'></div>久之，改大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164445_comment'></div>时年已三十馀，未始从政，盖文正公以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>清慎</span>训诸子，而公亦恬于进取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164445_comment'></div>文正公薨，恩授光禄寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164445_comment'></div>服除，特授大理寺丞，俄又迁太子中允、同判太府寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164445_comment'></div>故无同，皆异恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164445_comment'></div>乾兴中，荣国夫人忧，终丧入对，赐五品服，勾当马步军专勾司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164445_comment'></div>尝以疾闻两宫，命中贵人劳问，将太医以诊视之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164445_comment'></div>改殿中丞、通判郑州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164445_comment'></div>代还，召升陛，占对甚久，上嘉叹之，擢为群牧判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164445_comment'></div>累更主客、金部、司勋员外，充开封府界提点。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164445_comment'></div>踰年上计，赐金紫，判盐铁案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164445_comment'></div>宝元初，升祠部郎中、京西转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164445_comment'></div>丁母永康郡太君张氏丧，既阕，再领盐铁，又判理欠凭由司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164445_comment'></div>庆历三年，出为淮南转运按察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164445_comment'></div>赐对便坐，上美公效官保家之才，翌日，特迁度支郎中，诏留不行，寻判户部句院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164445_comment'></div>明年，又迁司封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164445_comment'></div>又明年春，充两浙转运按察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164445_comment'></div>是岁秋七月甲子，考终于钱塘之官舍，春秋五十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164445_comment'></div>九月，其子奉丧还都；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164445_comment'></div>十月甲子，葬于开封县大边村之先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164445_comment'></div>公生平仕宦，所为必罄风力，未尝有一毫过差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164445_comment'></div>每改秩，必<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>抗章</span>辞避，若不胜任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164445_comment'></div>明道中为府界提点，时岁旱虫孽，近甸艰食，中出缣帛五十万，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>科卖</span>民间，取赀以市粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164445_comment'></div>公曰：「岁凶，当发而歛，民将不堪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164445_comment'></div>建议封帛中帑，易缗钱，坐仓以籴，众以为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164445_comment'></div>明年，陨雹杀桑，缕蚕弗孳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164445_comment'></div>公又上白，用所封之缣，以充常赋，俾民纳镪以代焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164445_comment'></div>许西之顿固，岁诛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>旁民</span>出薪木五万馀，以缮斗门，公命伐官堤之树以足用，民是以休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164445_comment'></div>又时有馀税不能输者，吏甚急之，公请对，具述京师天下根本，当休养丰息之，今不蠲贷，是趣其流亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164445_comment'></div>上悉从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164445_comment'></div>郡吏有捕蝗而暍死者，公为出赙给其家属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164445_comment'></div>提荐才吏，未尝言按人，当世号为长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164445_comment'></div>其在计省也，以都下府藏主吏岁辄一易，往往匿其簿领，用赂更他局，新至者视物之浩繁，弗能究知，因循积十数任，败没欺攘，不可胜纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164445_comment'></div>公奏择他官按籍，以察其交承，以故物之耗登，吏之奸廉尽可明，不复如故时，迄今以为通制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164445_comment'></div>又天下尝输之货，郡吏部至京府，有司必巧訾以动之，至有荡产伏辟而不能偿之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164445_comment'></div>公建言，使定其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>窳滥</span>逋欠之当理者，令三司本判官覆察面辨之，遂绝其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164445_comment'></div>民有贷息钱，户已绝而籍不除，有司阅籍，责息不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164445_comment'></div>及久年之逋，皆锢其子孙，什保数百辈寒窭愁痛，愿以死偿而未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164445_comment'></div>公条陈其状，乞一切纵去，朝廷从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164445_comment'></div>公之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/149/Comments/0")'>区理</span>事物，穷奸恤隐，如是者甚众，不可具道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164445_comment'></div>予自幼出入公之家，接侍公之起居，迄于今踰三十年，其久且详，可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164445_comment'></div>窃观其举动饮食，皆有常度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164445_comment'></div>不妄评论，莫见好恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164445_comment'></div>终日高拱危坐，冠服端整，虽对近习，未尝有骄惰之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164445_comment'></div>人或以事挠之，终不愠见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164445_comment'></div>间或语言，皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/169/Comments/0")'>郁然</span>有条，以慎靖仁厚为之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164445_comment'></div>作事有本末，不尚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/172/Comments/0")'>铦锐</span>，久而必立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164445_comment'></div>自文正公薨后数年，文靖公入政府，内外姻族之盛，冠于当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164445_comment'></div>公悫守家政，以清约先己，不为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/180/Comments/0")'>浮侈</span>隳其世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164445_comment'></div>呜呼，其有常德之君子者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164445_comment'></div>国朝丞相子稍有立，虽无他才，朝廷必擢之美官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164445_comment'></div>若公者，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/187/Comments/0")'>绩效</span>著白，而雅意冲退，复不喜缘家世亲戚，以取恩泽，故间关计府，没于郎署，士大夫为之叹息焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164445_comment'></div>公二弟：冲，任太子赞善大夫而卒，宇量闳厚，伟人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164445_comment'></div>素，见任刑部郎中，知汝州，刚峭善议论，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/203/Comments/0")'>才敏</span>过人，临事敢决无所屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1164445_comment'></div>予谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/205/Comments/0")'>资赋</span>虽殊，各得文正公之一体，而公渊然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1164445", 1164445, "Clauses/207/Comments/0")'>澄泊</span>，议者为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1164445_comment'></div>二夫人皆先公殁：前李氏，大理卿湘之女；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1164445_comment'></div>后吕氏，即文靖许国公之女也，始封东平县君，许公薨，进封安康郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1164445_comment'></div>二子：恰，大理丞，整，太常寺太祝，皆向学闻道，久未可涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1164445_comment'></div>一女，适殿中丞、通判郑州吕希杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1164445_comment'></div>公视予为姊子，公之亡，予适在江外，二弟以予知公之行，驿求予文表于墓，故为直述，以见世焉。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1164445'></div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1164445_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　为王质作行状。作品：朝奉大夫尚书度支郎中充天章阁待制知陕州军府事平晋县开国男食邑三百户上护军赐紫金鱼袋王公行状。<div id='poem_1164431' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164431' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164431?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝奉大夫尚书度支郎中充天章阁待制知陕州军府事平晋县开国男食邑三百户上护军赐紫金鱼袋王公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164431")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164431_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164431'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164431'>曾祖某，左拾遗，累赠太师、尚书令、鲁国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164431_comment'></div>祖某，兵部侍郎，累赠太师、尚书令、晋国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164431_comment'></div>父某，兵部郎中，赠户部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164431_comment'></div>公讳质，字子野，其先占籍大名，由晋公贵，始居京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164431_comment'></div>自幼好学，不群儿嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164431_comment'></div>太尉文正公，即公之伯父，祥符中为大丞相，荫公为太常寺奉礼郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164431_comment'></div>稍长，向学益笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164431_comment'></div>一日，以所著献于文正，文正览之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>惊嗟</span>，亲为作诗以美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164431_comment'></div>改大理丞，尚未冠，又以文闻奏御，召试学士院，考入进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164431_comment'></div>刘尚书筠在翰林，与诸公交荐，遂充馆阁校勘，转中丞、太常博士，迁集贤校理，改祠部员外郎，时年始二十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164431_comment'></div>风韵高洒，喜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>辨论</span>，所交皆当世豪英，未始敢以贵势少年遇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164431_comment'></div>俄丁尚书忧，旅于南都，与诸弟饭脱粟茹蔬，至性孝睦，族无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164431_comment'></div>服除，同判苏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164431_comment'></div>郡守黄公宗旦，前辈有才望，任气自雄长，以公齿未壮，初未甚礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164431_comment'></div>公事之至恪，虽被讥嘲，绝不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>雠应</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164431_comment'></div>官事有未便者，必乘间以白之，不听，则力为辨其枉直，必于行而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164431_comment'></div>黄公初忿恨，终感悟而加礼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164431_comment'></div>还朝，赐绯鱼，改度支，同判尚书刑部；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164431_comment'></div>又判吏部南曹，改司封，知蔡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164431_comment'></div>蔡之圭田颇瘠，民岁输租，甚苦之，公至郡，悉蠲除不取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164431_comment'></div>俗旧祠吴元济，公曰：「安有逆丑而庙食者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164431_comment'></div>长吏不能革旧俗之滥，民何观焉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164431_comment'></div>于是毁元济之像，以狄梁公、李太尉有功于唐，而德及蔡人，遂建二公之祠，号双庙，率群吏往拜而祀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164431_comment'></div>转祠部郎中，召为开封府推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164431_comment'></div>公兄雍时亦为三司判官，公曰：「是皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/91/Comments/1")'>剧职</span>，吾兄弟并命，妨寒士之进」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164431_comment'></div>遂恳辞之，出知寿州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164431_comment'></div>郡素号多讼，而邑所部送囚，虽重辟，往往伪窜其名以上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164431_comment'></div>公摘其滥奸，擒邑吏坐鞭而黥之，自是肃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164431_comment'></div>又多豪姓，五等之籍久废，每敛率无科，吏以赂为轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164431_comment'></div>公将定其籍，不关吏手，吏窃相笑语曰：「是乌能周知吾民之产乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164431_comment'></div>公一日会官吏坐府中，自为檄，召隐豪面谕之，皆稽首叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164431_comment'></div>馀之登耗，纤悉无差，一府震骇，号为神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164431_comment'></div>又移庐州，巨盗张雄杀其党，并所赀而遁，逻者获之，公以法诛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164431_comment'></div>牍下大理，法官引近诏盗杀其徒者原之，雄不当死，吏当坐罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164431_comment'></div>公曰：「法所以戢奸，而断实原情，今雄本罪当死，而又杀人以取赀，既非自首而捕得之，盗无悛恶之状，法无破奸之术」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164431_comment'></div>疏三上，不省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164431_comment'></div>公曰：「吾不胜法吏矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164431_comment'></div>又上疏自劾，愿不坐群吏，又不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164431_comment'></div>愿自为首，乃听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164431_comment'></div>遂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/145/Comments/0")'>左降</span>监舒州灵仙观，他吏得减一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164431_comment'></div>公襟上高爽，有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/148/Comments/0")'>仙风道格</span>，日与二三逸人，放意于江山之间，笑歌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/151/Comments/0")'>盘嬉</span>，洒然得方外之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164431_comment'></div>夙有羸病，药剂未尝去手，既至舒数月，而旧疾颇愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164431_comment'></div>因采古今练形摄生之术，著《宝元总录》一百卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164431_comment'></div>逾年，今资政殿学士、给事中韩公琦知审刑院，上言前法颇滥，因申明旧制，请盗杀其徒者不首不原，朝廷从之，如公往者之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164431_comment'></div>又今资政殿大学士郑公戬，翰林侍读学士叶公清臣，皆荐公才可大用，而以非辜久黜，遂起知泰州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164431_comment'></div>岁中，改度支郎中，入朝授荆湖北路转运使，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164431_comment'></div>自西方用武，领是职者，务先掊下以为事，又争以羡馀为名，贡于朝以助军需，其实诛于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164431_comment'></div>朝廷往往擢之好官，号为称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164431_comment'></div>公深嫉之，常赋之外，无一毫横敛，远民赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164431_comment'></div>富公弼为资政殿学士，常带史馆修撰，平生未尝识公面，而素慕之，荐公有贤业而恬不喜进，愿召还代修撰，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164431_comment'></div>又命同判吏部流内铨，俄拜天章阁待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164431_comment'></div>是时，上方登用俊良，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/198/Comments/0")'>刬革</span>夙弊，公雍容侍从之列，以清风峻节为一时所畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164431_comment'></div>或以公少所献纳为议者，君子谓使子野于朝，虽恬然不言，士大夫仰其风采，亦当竞廉让而忘鄙俗之心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164431_comment'></div>为吏部未一岁，号为称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164431_comment'></div>尝谓同列曰：「官局之设，若权衡然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164431_comment'></div>险者妄自高下，非器之弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164431_comment'></div>茍遇物持平，轻重判然于中矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164431_comment'></div>故贵豪者毋倖请，孤远者毋废劳，老吏手束胁息，不敢摇动其法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1164431_comment'></div>州县巧黠吏，有以贿得举者，于格当迁，公廉知之，遂为密启，使使从中罢者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1164431_comment'></div>俄出知陕州，才一年，寝疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1164431_comment'></div>庆历五年，终于官舍，享年四十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1164431_comment'></div>累阶为朝奉大夫，勋为上护军，爵平晋县开国男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1164431_comment'></div>公少以师礼事杨文公亿，文公深器之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1164431_comment'></div>尝以书誉于刘翰林曰：「子野<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/237/Comments/1")'>英妙</span>，不衒文干进，当世佳士也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1164431_comment'></div>又以公诗句手写扇上，众争玩之，由是名称益大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1164431_comment'></div>公<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/243/Comments/0")'>刚峭</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/243/Comments/1")'>介洁</span>，而性仁厚，果于义断，论者谓有烈祖之风操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1164431_comment'></div>静退不喜进趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1164431_comment'></div>或与公同在馆阁者，皆去为达官，当涂数诱，公终不为屈，以是益不见用，公亦自适无所憾，朝议嗟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1164431_comment'></div>公有女当嫁，遂求庐州，例得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/257/Comments/0")'>装钱</span>二十万，将以为资送，执政者谕意，欲公往谒之，公终不往，遂不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1164431_comment'></div>公谪官灵仙，至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/264/Comments/0")'>窘匮</span>，乃举族蔬食，数年未尝食肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1164431_comment'></div>每得俸入，辄厚享宾客，数日而竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1164431_comment'></div>公年三十八为尚书郎，每授命，则惕然惊悸曰：「吾先君寿六十有八，终于省郎，吾今亦已老矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1164431_comment'></div>性纯孝，每道先君事，则霶然泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1164431_comment'></div>公弟素，自淮南按察使被召帅泾原，命下之日，公通夕不寐，召诸子谓曰：「吾弟母老且病，子至幼，讵可以御戎穷边乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1164431_comment'></div>吾无亲忧，而汝辈长矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1164431_comment'></div>明日，遂上言乞留素而自代，愿死节以报国，弗从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1164431_comment'></div>又命其子规曰：「朝廷不免吾弟之行，吾所忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1164431_comment'></div>汝其往侍，无怠焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1164431_comment'></div>公特爱于规，以其多病，未尝使离膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1164431_comment'></div>又幼弟端，力学勤官，十馀年未出州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1164431_comment'></div>公当迁官，拜章乞端召试，遂赐进士出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1164431_comment'></div>公智识<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_81_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/307/Comments/0")'>闳远</span>，善谭名理，虽庸人之善，终身不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1164431_comment'></div>为郡先<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/311/Comments/0")'>化导</span>，不尚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/312/Comments/0")'>威罚</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1164431_comment'></div>主漕荆南也，尝权府事，有媪诉其妇之见逐，无所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1164431_comment'></div>公召而诘之，妇曰：「舅始亡，姑即嫁去，既穷而归，奉养甚谨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1164431_comment'></div>后取吾金，又嫁，今复穷而归，故不敢舍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1164431_comment'></div>公曰：「姑虽不良，独不念若夫邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1164431_comment'></div>又谓其妇之子曰：「尔母薄于姑，尔独不念父邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1164431_comment'></div>遂切责媪，谕以改行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1164431_comment'></div>又取家人之衣以衣之，与妇孙廪粟，使以归养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1164431_comment'></div>于是皆感泣而去，孝爱如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1164431_comment'></div>大凡民有犯法诋欺者，虽末事必竟，过误虽大必贷之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1164431_comment'></div>或良顽共罪，顽虽辞胜若真可信者，公必直指其隐，善恶立决，众伏其明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1164431_comment'></div>所至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_93_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/348/Comments/0")'>横猾</span>屏迹，畏公之明，不敢犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1164431_comment'></div>外台非其人，多暴敛于民者，公悉不承命，与之讲辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1164431_comment'></div>或不决，闻之于朝，每多见从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1164431_comment'></div>故数为恶吏摭事以中，公亦浩然不校，然不能害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1164431_comment'></div>公治家严明有法度，以道义训子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1164431_comment'></div>初，文正为中书舍人，家至窭，与昆弟贷息钱，约违期，以所乘之马偿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1164431_comment'></div>公阅书得券，召子弟而示之，曰：「此吾家清风，尔曹当毋忘此事」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1164431_comment'></div>又得颜鲁公为尚书时，乞米于李大夫墨帖，亲摹于石，遍遗亲友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1164431_comment'></div>公喜士好施，凡遇人危急，平生仇恶，皆一视若己，未尝问家有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1164431_comment'></div>唯聚书数千卷，古琴数张，出处未尝舍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1164431_comment'></div>公既卒，陕人哀哭塞道，朝野无贤愚，皆相吊出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1164431_comment'></div>家贫，柩不能还先茔，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_104_1164431", 1164431, "Clauses/392/Comments/0")'>朋旧</span>在要官者皆力之，遂得还京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1164431_comment'></div>尝语人曰：「吾思世故无所为，忽忽欲熟醉以死，幸矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1164431_comment'></div>屡以后事属家人，且笑曰：「人世一吷耳，安可久期哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1164431_comment'></div>公之生也，以七月二十六日，亦以是日而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1164431_comment'></div>娶周氏，封褒信县君，故礼部侍郎起之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1164431_comment'></div>男三人：曰毖，将作监主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1164431_comment'></div>曰规，前明州奉化县主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1164431_comment'></div>曰复，将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1164431_comment'></div>女二人：长适太常寺太祝范纯仁，资政殿学士仲淹之子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1164431_comment'></div>次尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1164431_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_114_1164431'></div><div id='poem_sentence_114_1164431_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有诗谢赵概来访。作品：郡侯访予于沧浪亭因而高会翌日以一章谢之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此“郡侯”可能是赵概。）</span><div id='poem_495707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郡侯访予于沧浪亭因而高会翌日以一章谢之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495707")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495707'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495707'>荒亭俗少游，迁客心自爱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495707'>绕亭植梧竹，私心亦有待。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495707'>昨朝十骑来，䟃𧽼拥林外。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495707'>水禽骇笳鼓，野老瞻车盖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495707'>公馀喜静境，宾至因高会。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495707'>跋石已行厨<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作庖）</span>，临流聊褫带。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495707'>优游鄙情通，放旷未礼杀。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495707'>酒醇引易釂，肉<span class='inlineComment2'>（钱校作䏑）</span>美举必嘬。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495707'>千蹠恣食鸡，二螯时把蟹。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495707'>开颜閒善谑，倾耳得嘉话。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495707'>暮夜欢未厌，裴回意将再。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495707'>跋已见<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>懵腾，跨鞍极倒载。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495707'>明日尚狂酲，嘉贶不遑拜。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495707'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_495707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495707'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_495707_0'>⑴ 黄本、陈本作见跋已</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495707_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有诗和欧阳修。作品：和永叔琅琊山庶子泉阳冰石篆诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年春。）</span><div id='poem_495712' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495712' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495712?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和永叔琅邪山庶子泉阳冰石篆诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495712")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495712_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495712'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495712'>一气破散万事起，独有篆籀含<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>其真。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495712'>周鼓秦山坏已久，下至唐室始有人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495712'>宗臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495712", 495712, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>转注</span>得天法，质虽浑厚气乃振。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495712'>人间所存十数处，丰疏异体世共珍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495712'>其中琅邪石泉记，比之他法殊不伦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495712'>铁锁关连玉钩壮，曲处力可持万钧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495712'>复疑蛟虬植爪角，隐入翠壁蟠未伸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495712'>近来欲眼苦不赏，惟有风月时相亲。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495712'>紫微仙人谪此守，此地胜绝旧喜闻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495712'>公馀往观领宾从，猎猎画隼摇青春。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495712'>远休车骑步泉侧，酌泉爱篆移朝昏。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495712'>挥弄潺湲玩点画，情通恍惚疑前身。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495712'>作诗缄本远相寄，邀我共赋意甚勤。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495712'>昨承见教久阁笔，压以大句尤难文<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：永叔近以书戒予作诗。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495712'>高风胜事日倾倒，安得身寄西飞云。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495712'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_495712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495712'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_495712_0'>⑴ 原作舍，据黄本、陈本、李本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495712_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有诗。作品：醉翁亭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有诗答王素。作品：答仲仪见寄。<div id='poem_495800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495800?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答仲仪见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495800")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495800'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495800'>前岁京都吏议諠，劲弓摧翮两连翩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495800'>男儿穷困终归道，世路倾危自有天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495800'>云壑已通尘外意，茅斋仍得日<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>高眠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495800'>寄声吾舅无相念，今作江湖<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495800", 495800, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>九馆仙</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495800'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495800'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_495800_0'>⑴ 日原作自，据黄本、陈本、李本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495800_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='60d59e4ef1b84b7ca51cfc6324dff60c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("60d59e4ef1b84b7ca51cfc6324dff60c");'><span id='60d59e4ef1b84b7ca51cfc6324dff60c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1047')">1046-1047年</a>，39-40岁</div><div id='60d59e4ef1b84b7ca51cfc6324dff60c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有诗。作品：寄题丰乐亭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年夏或秋。）</span><div id='poem_495709' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495709' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495709?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题丰乐亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495709")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495709_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495709'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495709'>神物藏胜地，深林隐苍峰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495709'>威夷渡浅岭，爱此泉一钟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495709'>古今未见赏，荒然草苔封。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495709'>公来辟一径，疏凿随指踪<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作纵，据黄本、陈本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495709'>挥洗落尘虑，甘凉洒烦胸。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495709'>搆亭于其间，四面开轩墉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495709'>名之丰乐者，此意实在农。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495709'>使君何所乐，所乐惟年丰。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495709'>年丰讼诉息，可使风化醲。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495709'>游此乃可乐，岂徒悦宾从。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495709'>野老共歌呼，山禽相迎逢。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495709'>把酒谢白云，援琴对孤松。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495709'>境清岂俗到，世路徒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_495709", 495709, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>冲冲</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495709'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_495709_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　为赵概之母作墓志铭。作品：广陵郡太君高氏墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年秋。）</span><div id='poem_1164447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广陵郡太君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164447")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164447'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164447'>庆历六年秋七月，刑部郎中、知制诰赵公槩之寿母，终于苏之官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164447_comment'></div>踰月，菆涂于佛庙，卜以明年某月某日之吉，护<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164447", 1164447, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>神舆</span>还南都，祔先侍郎之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164447_comment'></div>公疏其族氏，见属为文，识诸圹云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164447_comment'></div>夫人姓高氏，世居青州之益都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164447_comment'></div>祖辇，后唐为王府记室，以诗名于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164447_comment'></div>父某，少喜孙吴兵法，事杨光远为帐下吏，阴知光远有异志，遂逸去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164447_comment'></div>后光远以逆诛，乃閒居不复出仕宦，东人高之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164447_comment'></div>生二子及夫人，每叹曰：「此女若为男子，吾门户复何忧邪」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164447_comment'></div>夫人幼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164447", 1164447, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>敏悟</span>，闻人诵诗书，一过耳尽记不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164447_comment'></div>性澹泊，不衣组绣，不喜茹荤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164447_comment'></div>初，侍郎通判密州，夫人归焉，典训闱中，事皆有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164447", 1164447, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>条绪</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164447_comment'></div>始封千乘县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164447_comment'></div>侍郎先娶张氏，有男女六人，夫人煦育教诱，过于己之所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164447_comment'></div>生四子：长曰明允，博学有器识；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164447_comment'></div>季即公也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164447_comment'></div>馀皆先夫人而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164447_comment'></div>侍郎既没，家资尽窭，夫人每闻诸子之宾至，必解衣为贳酒脯，使延之，从容以讲习道义，故七子皆举进士，有闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164447_comment'></div>公最幼，自初能言，夫人日自课以书，使调四声作诗赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164447_comment'></div>十七岁举进士，既孤二十四年，公登甲科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164447_comment'></div>后三年为著作郎、直集贤院，以恩封渤海县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164447_comment'></div>又十年，公知制诰，拜章乞以一官及封爵食邑换夫人以郡封，诏从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164447_comment'></div>爵邑之请，自是遂为著例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164447_comment'></div>进封广陵郡，时年八十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164447_comment'></div>明年，召中外亲族当为昏姻者，为处理办给之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164447_comment'></div>又谓公曰：「尔当于近郡市居第，以安族人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164447_comment'></div>及夏寝疾，涉冬稍閒，因思食笋，且曰：「可求补外，南方地湿，笋得早出也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164447_comment'></div>十二月，公即屡削章，诏守吴郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164447_comment'></div>二月，侍夫人东下，夏以霖晦卑湿，感疾甚笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164447_comment'></div>一日，指旁室曰：「此可作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1164447", 1164447, "Clauses/96/Comments/1")'>孝堂</span>，吊者至，尔哭于某处，居丧之礼当然也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164447_comment'></div>后数日，食饮如平时，忽曰：「今日中元，吾其逝矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164447_comment'></div>俄即瞑目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164447_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164447_comment'></div>夫人有子如是，妇节母道，为时所师，非以文而不朽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164447_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1164447'>少爱于家，择贤以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164447_comment'></div>宾祭洁恭，壸仪辉辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164447_comment'></div>寡居教子，卒观雄飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164447_comment'></div>睦族周乏，褚无兼衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164447_comment'></div>先识远鉴，审如神蓍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164447_comment'></div>疾虽沈绵，不考筮医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164447_comment'></div>绪言泠泠，事物尽宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164447_comment'></div>琢文<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1164447", 1164447, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>阴壤</span>，庶永后希。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1164447_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有诗答陆经。作品：寒夜十六韵答子履见寄。<span class='inlineComment2'>（是年冬作。）</span><div id='poem_495820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寒夜十六韵答子履见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495820")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495820'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495820'>风雨夜寒新，空斋感慨频。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495820'>诗书穷不放，灯火静相亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495820'>眺听时怀土，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495820", 495820, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>低摧</span>动畏人<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：魏文诗云客子常畏人。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495820'>漫书成咄咄，远吠厌狺狺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495820'>念昔罹忧患，唯君共苦辛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495820'>漂流数千里，会合十馀旬。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495820'>各闵伤弓翼，聊同煦沫鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495820'>谁知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_495820", 495820, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>公冶罪</span>，众笑伯龙贫。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495820'>隔绝今一水，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_495820", 495820, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>暌离</span>将再春。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495820'>喜篇数为贶，尺牍亦相珍。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495820'>倚伏时难定，屯亨理亦循。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495820'>剑埋犹有气，蠖屈尚能伸。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495820'>邦国方登俊，江湖且<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_495820", 495820, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>放神</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495820'>不忧知在命，任重莫如身。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495820'>白首襟期远，青云志业均。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495820'>陶然任元化，慎勿损天真。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495820'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_495820_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　得杜衍诗感而作。作品：病中得杜丞相见寄诗感而有作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑为是年秋作。）</span><div id='poem_495796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>病中得杜丞相见寄诗感而有作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495796")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495796'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495796'>易毁唯迁客，难谐<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作谙）</span>是俗情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495796'>愁多怯秋夜，病久厌人生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495796'>委顺闻之旧，衰羸见者惊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495796'>新诗如接侍，吟罢涕淋缨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495796'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有诗和欧阳修。作品：和菱溪石歌。<div id='poem_495726' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495726' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495726?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和菱溪石歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495726")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495726_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495726'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495726'>滁州信至诧双石，云初得自菱水滨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495726'>长篇称夸语险绝，欲使来者不复言。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495726'>画图突兀亦颇怪，张之屋壁惊<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495726", 495726, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>心魂</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495726'>麒麟才生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495726", 495726, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>头角</span>异，混沌虽死<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495726", 495726, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>窍凿</span>存。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495726'>琅邪之郡偏且僻，得石固可骇众观。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495726'>予尝飞帆入震泽，穷探异境登龟鼋<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：太湖二山名，最出怪石。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495726'>居民百户石为业，日夜采琢山不贫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495726'>山前森列战白浪，犹似万百铁马群。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495726'>雨昏浪打岁月古，千株万穴僵复奔。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495726'>自嗟才力本衰弱，安敢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_495726", 495726, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>抵敌</span>为之文。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495726'>况兹出产极易致，乡俗见惯不甚尊。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495726'>彼以至少合贵重，胡为久弃如隐沦。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495726'>偶逢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_495726", 495726, "Clauses/24/Comments/1")'>积<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作精）</span>识</span>见奖拔，众目今乃称奇珍。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495726'>百人拥持大车载，城市观走风涛翻。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495726'>立于新亭面幽谷，共为澡刷泥沙痕。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495726'>凉泉下照嘉树阴，翠影<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_495726", 495726, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>澄澹</span>留烟云。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495726'>褒以篇章绘缣素，积岁汨没一旦伸。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495726'>苟非高贤独赏激，终古<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_495726", 495726, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>弃卧</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_495726", 495726, "Clauses/35/Comments/1")'>穷津</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495726'>世人爱憎逐兴废，使我吟叹伤精神。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495726'></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_495726_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有诗哭尹洙。作品：哭师鲁。<div id='poem_495711' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495711' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495711?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哭师鲁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495711")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495711_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495711'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495711'>前年子渐死，予哭大江头。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495711'>今年师鲁死，予方旅长洲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495711'>初闻尚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495711", 495711, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>疑惑</span>，涕泪已不收。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495711'>举杯欲向口，荆棘生咽喉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495711'>忆初定交时，后前穆与欧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495711'>君颜白如霜，君语清如流。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495711'>予年又甚少，学古众所羞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495711'>君欲举拔萃，声耦日<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_495711", 495711, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>抉搜</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495711'>不鄙吾学异，推尊谓前修。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495711'>今踰二十年，迹远心甚稠。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495711'>后会国南门，夜谈雪满楼。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495711'>青灯照素发，酒阑气益遒。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495711'>昨君握兵柄，节制关外侯。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495711'>予才入册府，俄作中都囚。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495711'>飞章立<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_495711", 495711, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>辨雪</span>，危言动<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_495711", 495711, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>前旒</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495711'>时虽不见省，凛凛压众媮。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495711'>旋闻君下狱，六月送渭州。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495711'>渭州旧治所，昔拥万貔貅。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495711'>堂中坐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_495711", 495711, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>玉帐</span>，堂下森<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>蛇矛。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495711'>令严山石裂，恩煦春色浮。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495711'>衅生无根芽，众言起愆尤。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495711'>返来入狴犴，吏对安可酬。<div id='poem_sentence_21_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_495711'>法官巧追拍，刺骨不肯抽。<div id='poem_sentence_22_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_495711'>削秩贬汉东，驱迫日置邮。<div id='poem_sentence_23_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_495711'>穷途无一簪，百口谁相赒。<div id='poem_sentence_24_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_495711'>诸子继死亡，清血渍两眸。<div id='poem_sentence_25_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_495711'>贸然几丧明，愤苦结不瘳。<div id='poem_sentence_26_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_495711'>君性本刚峭，安可小屈柔。<div id='poem_sentence_27_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_495711'>暴罹此冤辱，苟活何所求。<div id='poem_sentence_28_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_495711'>人间不见容，不若地下游。<div id='poem_sentence_29_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_495711'>又疑天憎善，专与恶报仇。<div id='poem_sentence_30_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_495711'>二坚潜膏肓，众鬼来揶揄。<div id='poem_sentence_31_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_495711'>弃局奔南阳，后事得所投。<div id='poem_sentence_32_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_495711'>心胆尚卓荦，精明已弥留。<div id='poem_sentence_33_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_495711'>生平经纬才，萧瑟掩一丘。<div id='poem_sentence_34_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_495711'>青天自茫茫，长夜何悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_35_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_495711'>万物孰不死，死常在严秋。<div id='poem_sentence_36_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_495711'>君齿方<span class='inlineComment2'>（顾交作况）</span>盛壮，众期树风猷。<div id='poem_sentence_37_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_495711'>二边方<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_495711", 495711, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>横猾</span>，四海皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_495711", 495711, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>疮疣</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_38_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_495711'>斯时忽云亡，孰为朝廷忧。<div id='poem_sentence_39_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_495711'>予方编吴氓，日自亲锄耰。<div id='poem_sentence_40_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_495711'>无缘匍匐救，兀兀空悲愁。<div id='poem_sentence_41_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_495711'>时思庄生言，所乐唯髑髅。<div id='poem_sentence_42_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_495711'>物理不可诘，此说诚最优。<div id='poem_sentence_43_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_495711'></div><div id='poem_sentence_44_495711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495711'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_18_495711_0'>⑴ 原作生，据黄本、陈本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495711_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有诗寄赵概。作品：寄题赵叔平嘉树亭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于庆历六、七年间。）</span><div id='poem_495829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495829' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495829?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题赵叔平嘉树亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495829")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495829_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495829'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495829'>嘉树名亭古意同，拂檐围砌共青葱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495829'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495829", 495829, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>午阴</span>闲淡茶烟外，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495829", 495829, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>晓韵</span>萧疏睡雨中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495829'>开户常时对君子，绕轩终日是清风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495829'>盘根得地年年盛，岂学春林一晌红。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495829'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495829_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有记。作品：浩然堂记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于庆历六、七年间。）</span><div id='poem_1164427' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164427' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164427?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浩然堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164427")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164427_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164427'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164427'>曾君将之杭官，旅于苏，尝登于沧浪之亭，览景四顾，慨然有弃绋冕相从之意，予始未以其言为信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164427_comment'></div>君遂周访城中物境之嘉者，又得阊南之圃焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164427_comment'></div>罄囊中所有，日夜自营缉，筑堂其间，取孟子养浩然之气以命名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164427_comment'></div>一日，会予于堂，求予文以道其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164427_comment'></div>予观世之仕禄者，奔趋竭蹶，皇皇乎病日月之速，亡须臾之閒以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164427", 1164427, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>自放</span>，顾安肯弃其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164427", 1164427, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>赀装</span>，易清泠深僻之地而为适也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164427_comment'></div>又将均其志虑，包蓄诚议以自广，不亦庶乎君子之道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164427_comment'></div>至于环池以步，乘城以观，则竹树江山之胜，萧然满前，表里风物，不可胜道，至者其将自得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164427_comment'></div>予但嘉名堂之意，且能实其言，故文以镵于石。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1164427_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有信答李锐。作品：答李锐书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于庆历六、七年间。）</span><div id='poem_1164394' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164394' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164394?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答李锐书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164394")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164394_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164394'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164394'>去年五月中，足下相过遗书，始爱文藻之美，未甚悉其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164394_comment'></div>退而寻绎，乃谓予以道自公，失而不忧，有至高至难之节，其言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164394", 1164394, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>褒美</span>过甚，不敢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164394", 1164394, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>领览</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164394_comment'></div>但一诣门奉谢，又不相见，迄今将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164394", 1164394, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>逾年</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164394_comment'></div>尝谓足下以予不相酬对，见怒而绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164394_comment'></div>前日复蒙相访，又贶之书，乃以声名不见称道于士大夫间为愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164394_comment'></div>予欲以道相训，而又誉之，文义稠重，敢又不报其所说焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164394_comment'></div>夫道无古今，但时有用舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164394_comment'></div>有志之士，不计时之用舍，必趋至极之地，以学探求圣贤之意而迹其所行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164394_comment'></div>本原既明，则将养其诚心而泯去异端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164394_comment'></div>当其未知于人、用于世，则修之益勤，守之益坚，内自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164394", 1164394, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>贵珍</span>而有待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164394_comment'></div>盖先能置身名爵禄于虑外，然后乃能及此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164394_comment'></div>故君子虽被<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164394", 1164394, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>贼害</span>，颠沛其身，不更所守，岂虑外之物足顾哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164394_comment'></div>今足下所为之文，皆希慕贤哲之业，背众人之所向，取今世之所舍而反求声名于其间，不亦异乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164394_comment'></div>是亦非予之所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164394_comment'></div>茍志于彼，必失于此，故莫得而两全也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164394_comment'></div>心既<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164394", 1164394, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>淆乱</span>，将求合之不暇，岂道之能专乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164394_comment'></div>孟子谓修天爵而人爵从，此非必至之论，乃诱众人之说，急于教耳，志士乌能以声利动之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164394_comment'></div>予所以废弃于时，而晏然无闷者，此所得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164394_comment'></div>以足下问之之勤，安敢藏所得而不告也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164394_comment'></div>足下试思之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1164394_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　有诗祭滕宗谅。作品：滕子京哀辞二首。<div id='poem_495807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>滕子京哀辞<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495807")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495807'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495807'>云霓收壮气，星象卷英魂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495807_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495807'>贤去人何赖，才亡世不尊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495807_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495807'>论兵虚玉帐，问俗失朱轓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495807_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495807'>自为知音绝，低回恸寝门。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495807_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495807'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495807_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_495808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495808?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495808'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495808'>忠义平生事，声名夷翟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>闻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495808'>言皆出诸老，勇复冠全军。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495808'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495808", 495808, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>冥莫</span>知谁主，贤愚岂更分。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495808'>江头送丹旐，哭向九华云。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495808'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495808'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_495808_0'>⑴ 原作敌，据黄本、陈本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495808_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　有文悼滕宗谅。作品：祭滕子京文。<div id='poem_1164450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭滕子京文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164450")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164450'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164450'>维庆历七年丁亥，二月丙午朔，二日丁未，武功苏某等，谨以清酌庶羞之奠，恭致祭于知府待制学士之灵：惟灵禀之刚明，精于义断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164450_comment'></div>学有根柢，才无涯岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164450_comment'></div>往在谏列，谠论侃侃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164450_comment'></div>屡触权要，卒就贬窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164450_comment'></div>提兵穷边，策画贯穿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164450_comment'></div>士奋乐死，戎詟而散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164450_comment'></div>谤起南逐，曾不愁叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164450_comment'></div>改麾于吴，忽此凶变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164450_comment'></div>人亡师保，国失蕃翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164450_comment'></div>月照公庭，屡奉谈宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164450_comment'></div>今哭而趋，循视敛棺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164450_comment'></div>光仪精爽，烂烂如见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164450_comment'></div>无以宣哀，是用酌荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164450_comment'></div>灵其来下，歆此微奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164450_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1164450_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ff483cad6b674cb990707f7439ad6f42_label'><a
