ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　有诗寄曹琰。作品：独游曹氏园馆因寄伯玉。<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑伯玉为曹琰字。）</span><div id='poem_495821' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495821' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495821?labeling=true' target='_blank'>独游曹氏园馆因寄伯玉</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495821")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495821_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495821'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495821'>去年把酒共徘徊，今日寻幽独此来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495821'>竹密似嫌闲客入，梅含应待主人开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495821'>赞谋<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495821", 495821, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>盛府</span>方投刃，捍患长堤正展才。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495821'>早晚得归如旧约，伴君池上倒尊罍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495821'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495821_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　有诗和刘彝。作品：秋宿虎丘寺数夕执中以诗见貺因次元韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年前后。）</span><div id='poem_495806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋宿虎丘寺数夕执以诗见贶因次元韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495806")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495806'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495806'>生事飘然付一舟，吴山萧寺且淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495806'>白云已有终身约，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495806", 495806, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>醁酒</span>聊驱万古愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495806'>峡束苍渊深贮月，岩排红树巧装秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495806'>徘徊欲出向城市，引领烟萝还自羞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495806'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495806_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　有信答范仲淹。作品：又答范资政书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于庆历六、七年。）</span><div id='poem_1164393' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164393' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164393?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又答范资政书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164393")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164393_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164393'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164393'>去冬捧策问，条目甚备，深明忧患之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164393_comment'></div>置之坐右，一食三诵，严然如临师保之前，虽未能尽其要处，而粗忘陨穫之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164393_comment'></div>专人至，又承亲笔，伏审坐镇之暇，体力<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164393", 1164393, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>平裕</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164393_comment'></div>且谓某穷道著书，日与圣人语堂奥，晏然自居，得《易》《艮》象时行时止，而其道<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164393", 1164393, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>光明</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164393_comment'></div>此阁下教之爱之之过实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164393_comment'></div>夫适其时而动静，使其道之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164393", 1164393, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>光明</span>，此大君子之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164393", 1164393, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>行藏</span>屈伸，非罪戾人之所可为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164393_comment'></div>本以不知时之可止而遂于行，蹈此机阱，今既止而虽欲行，莫可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164393_comment'></div>阁下前视卿辅之地不欲处，谦让引去，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164393", 1164393, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>偃息</span>籓镇，以閒放自喜，此正得时止之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164393_comment'></div>处此至静，益宜思念<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164393", 1164393, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>康世</span>尊本之术，充于胸中，因时而发，大庇天下，则其道卷舒而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164393", 1164393, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>光明</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164393_comment'></div>放废者安有此理？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164393_comment'></div>但守六五一爻之义而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164393_comment'></div>庶乎语言有序，悔吝稍亡，不贻知己者之所忧念耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164393_comment'></div>阁下其察之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1164393_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　有文。作品：复辨。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于庆历六左右。）</span><div id='poem_1164419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复辨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164419")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164419'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164419'>案《复卦》《彖》曰：「复亨，刚反，动而以顺行，是以出入无疾，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164419", 1164419, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>朋来</span>无咎，反复其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164419_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164419", 1164419, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>七日来复</span>，天行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164419_comment'></div>利有攸往，刚长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164419_comment'></div>复其见天地之心乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164419_comment'></div>王弼解云：「复者，反本之谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164419_comment'></div>天地以本为心，凡动息则静，静非对动者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164419_comment'></div>语息则默，默非对语者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164419_comment'></div>然则天地虽大，富有万物，雷动风行，运化万变，寂然至无，是其本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164419_comment'></div>故动息地中，乃天地之心见矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164419_comment'></div>予讨其意而窃惑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164419_comment'></div>夫复也者，以一阳始生而得名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164419_comment'></div>阳之始生，则有檗育万物之意，故《彖》曰「复其见天地之心」者，是由阳生而见之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164419_comment'></div>当群阴剥阳极尽之际，阴气张王，漠然无有生生之兆，则天地之心何见焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164419_comment'></div>及夫刚长天行，阳气下震，初九之爻布，而造物之意萌，则天地之心，虽微而已显矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164419_comment'></div>若谓以本为心，寂然至无，是其本，则变化之功何有焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164419_comment'></div>《彖》曰「刚反，动而顺行」，又曰「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164419", 1164419, "Clauses/51/Comments/2")'>朋来</span>」，又曰「天行」，又曰「刚长也」，安得谓寂然至无邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164419_comment'></div>安得谓动息耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164419_comment'></div>《象》曰：「雷在地中，复」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164419_comment'></div>盖雷者阳物也，动物也，今既名在地中，则是有阳动之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164419_comment'></div>辅嗣昧举卦之体，乃以寂然至无为复，斯失之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164419_comment'></div>夫复者，刚阳始萌，阴物衰谢，初包化生之心，潜而未运，唯圣人知其太始而言之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164419_comment'></div>盖神之所为，至精至变，非圣人孰能见之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164419_comment'></div>然天地虽以生万物为心，而万物莫见其为心之用，是冥然无有经营之迹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164419_comment'></div>故《系辞》云「显诸仁，藏诸用，鼓万物不与圣人同忧」，此之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164419_comment'></div>及乎雷奋雨润，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1164419", 1164419, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>勾达甲坼</span>，其仁则著矣，心则散而莫见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164419_comment'></div>是则蕴而妙用者之谓心，行而成功者之谓仁，在圣人则为几深，及乎通天下之志，成天下之务，则深与几何有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164419_comment'></div>《象》曰「后不省方」者，是先王察见天地造物之心而法象之，不亲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164419", 1164419, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>烦务</span>，而专以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164419", 1164419, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>沈谋研虑</span>，将以鼓舞天下之民，以行乎事业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164419_comment'></div>若云静其动，止其行，至于无事，则失之远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164419_comment'></div>又云「冬至阴之复，夏至阳之复」，何冬夏阴阳之不辨邪？</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1164419'></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1164419_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　有信答马永。作品：答马永书。<div id='poem_1164391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答马永书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164391")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164391'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164391'>放废幽居，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164391", 1164391, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>士友</span>罕顾，足下昧于平昔，猥以长书见投，充然其来尽士君子相见之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164391_comment'></div>窃观书意，论辨甚嘉，然似孰予之迹而未烛其里者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164391_comment'></div>谓予不以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164391", 1164391, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>得丧</span>累其所守，不为怨愤不怿之词，此固细节，悔过避害者能为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164391_comment'></div>又云：「巧辨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164391", 1164391, "Clauses/13/Comments/1")'>饰说</span>，言悲貌蹙，或舍其所修，而小人是从」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164391_comment'></div>此则夷狄之民之所为，乌足道之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164391_comment'></div>夫士之学经术，知道义，非所以贸易爵禄之来，无有以应之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164391_comment'></div>道胜而位丧，于道何伤而不乐邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164391_comment'></div>世有知道而居位者，尚或为众<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164391", 1164391, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>牵踬</span>，不得尽施其所学，忧道之削，处心甚危，内负于己，外愧于人，畏时刑而惧鬼诛，何所乐哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164391_comment'></div>然贤者必欲推己之乐以乐众，故虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164391", 1164391, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>焦苦</span>其身，而不舍爵位者，非己所乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164391_comment'></div>茍去其位，则道日益舒，宜其安而无闷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164391_comment'></div>是施于众则劳，而足于己则易，亦物理之常势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164391_comment'></div>周公，大圣智也，尚皇皇不暇食，使其退居环堵之中，鼓琴咏歌，以味先圣之道，何忧愤之可入也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164391_comment'></div>乃知古者至治之世，有其道而不见用，独居畎亩，乐以终身，盖亦多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164391_comment'></div>故韩退之谓颜子恶衣食于陋巷，而依于孔子，虽乐不足称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164391_comment'></div>又观其《感二鸟赋》，悲激顿挫，有骚人之思，疑其年壮气锐，欲发其藻章，以耀于世，非其所存也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164391_comment'></div>予年四十矣，志于道亦有年，岂一旦受谴而并弃之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164391_comment'></div>舍其所乐，自为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164391", 1164391, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>沮愤</span>，亦何益于事哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164391_comment'></div>足下但见今之庸人，得则轩然而愉，失则枯槁而吟，谓予当然而不者可取也，殊不以圣贤之道策予所未至，徒以众人而望于予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164391_comment'></div>尚虑足下始以是合，终将有所发焉，故不敢默默。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1164391_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　为程师孟之父作墓志铭。作品：大理评事程君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1164446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大理评事程君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164446")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164446'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164446'>有以纯孝笃行著于吴里中者，闻程君焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164446_comment'></div>亲疾，斋戒蔬食以祷，后因而不茹荤二十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164446_comment'></div>幼喜酒，病酲，而母戒之，自是终身不复饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164446_comment'></div>既老，得风痹之疾，药剂以有酒荐通行其力者，家人白之，君叹曰：「吾虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164446", 1164446, "Clauses/14/Comments/1")'>晚耄</span>，敢忘亲言乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164446_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164446_comment'></div>食饮，人欲之大，君能因亲以绝，可谓纯孝也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164446_comment'></div>里有骆生，尝以二宝带密寄于君，骆之死，君即归之，其子不敢取，又愿分一以为遗，公曰：「欺死受货，非吾所能为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164446_comment'></div>族人离其赀产，君悉不受，惟受诸女之孤鞠养之，长归士人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164446_comment'></div>吴人好鲜食，君独戒杀，又乐赈人急难，不间<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164446", 1164446, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>疏密</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164446_comment'></div>凡乡闾冠昏丧祭之法，多取中焉，君必随其丰约而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164446", 1164446, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>条处</span>其事，窭者或为资给之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164446_comment'></div>每观书史，必择仁厚之言，书于门墙，以诵服焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164446_comment'></div>卒之日，乡老皆为之泣下，斯可谓之笃行也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164446_comment'></div>君讳某，字某，于庆历七年月日终于家，寿六十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164446_comment'></div>曾祖某，新安人，仕钱氏为营田使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164446_comment'></div>祖某，徙籍于苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164446_comment'></div>父某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164446_comment'></div>皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164446", 1164446, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>高遁</span>不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164446_comment'></div>夫人刘氏，渊静有法则，奉承尊嫜，接姻旧，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164446", 1164446, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>庄顺</span>之色，夙夜不绝于颜面，族人称美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164446_comment'></div>君之懿行闻于人，夫人有助焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164446_comment'></div>庆历四年郊祀推恩，以君为大理评事，夫人为彭城县君，用子封也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164446_comment'></div>夫人享年六十有五，先于君百日而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164446_comment'></div>三子：长某；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164446_comment'></div>次某；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164446_comment'></div>次师孟，太常博士，知南康军，才敏有闻，所历著治状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164446_comment'></div>一女，嫁桐庐令乐某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164446_comment'></div>孙男女十七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164446_comment'></div>以明年某月某日，将合葬于苏之某乡，太常君与予同年登科，授状丐文，以识其窆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164446_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1164446'>士大夫可罔以名，乡人不可欺以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164446_comment'></div>诚久乃著，宜昌其盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164446_comment'></div>不在厥躬，岂不有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164446_comment'></div>寿弗夭阏，嗣则淑令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164446_comment'></div>族尊里荣，乃终有庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164446_comment'></div>刻文于窆，后世所證。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1164446'></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1164446_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　有信上文彦博。作品：上集贤文相书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（是年闰正月文彦博拜相后作。）</span><div id='poem_1164389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上集贤文相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164389")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164389'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164389'>昨因宴会，遂被废逐，即日榜舟东走，潜伏于江湖之上，困置<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>羁索</span>，日与鱼鸟同群，躬耕著书，不接世故，当日之事，绝不历于齿牙之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164389_comment'></div>或亲旧见过，往往闵恻而言，以谓某以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>非辜</span>遭废，天下之所共知，何久穷居默处，无一言以自辨，浩然若无意于世者，岂钝怯不晓者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164389_comment'></div>某绝不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>酬应</span>，且止其说，然内实有所待耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164389_comment'></div>夫为吏坐贿，国典之所永弃，人情之所不堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164389_comment'></div>某心膂血气人也，家世受朝廷重恩，庐墓在京师，平生厉名节，勤文墨，未尝一施胸中之才，岂云衔冤恨，困处无人之墟，以终此身乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164389_comment'></div>盖被罪一二年间，谤议汹汹，尚未宁息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164389_comment'></div>相中伤者，皆当路得志，某虽欲力自辨雪，徒重取困辱耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164389_comment'></div>故若死灰槁木，昏昏自放，而内实有所待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164389_comment'></div>去岁，闻天子驿召阁下入政事府，某久熟阁下之德望，中怀油然始有檗萌之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164389_comment'></div>俄又闻甘陵卒叛，结坞自守，环师十万，踰月未诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164389_comment'></div>议者谓暴兵日久，纪律弗严，必有他变相因而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164389_comment'></div>阁下慷慨请行，驰至城下，威令一发，士乐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>奋命</span>，即时破壁，擒其凶魁，使天下懦将骄卒，闻之皆震栗竦动，以自警饬，声压夷狄，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>消杀</span>异志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164389_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164389_comment'></div>非伟烈明果，乌能及此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164389_comment'></div>天子即时临轩发策，以大丞相印绶付使而往拜焉，阁下抗章<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>避让</span>，言论坚正，愤疾近世务相奔争，无廉让之节，因事见意，以教有位，风采凛凛，震动万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164389_comment'></div>是阁下武足戡难，文足表世，虽处将相之地，乃天子用之之明，阁下当之为宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164389_comment'></div>况让特一节，未若因朝廷之寄，舒事业以济生民之艰也，此古人之大君子之所留意也，既而果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164389_comment'></div>某虽在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/88/Comments/0")'>岩薮</span>之间，闻之不觉废书而起，弹冠摄衣，西向引领，思一侍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>几闼</span>，倾写冤愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164389_comment'></div>迹贱道远，未可得也，敢辄以尺纸少布下恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164389_comment'></div>盖有所待，积年累月，得遭其时，不忍自弃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164389_comment'></div>又幸当日搆陷者或死或出，故敢缕缕而言，以通左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164389_comment'></div>某下吏之初，喧传四出，好事多口者增饰其语，闻者不得不惑，时阁下在远镇，必不甚悉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164389_comment'></div>始者，御史府与杜少师、范南阳有语言之隙，其势相轧，内不自平，遂煽造<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/114/Comments/0")'>诡说</span>，上惑天听，全台<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/116/Comments/0")'>墙进</span>，取必于君，逆施罔罗，预立机械。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164389_comment'></div>既起大狱，不关执政，使狡吏穷鞫，榜掠以求滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164389_comment'></div>事亦既无状，遂用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/125/Comments/0")'>深文</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164389_comment'></div>此会以常年<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>醵率</span>吏人，燕集非类，某思之以为非便，遂与同监院刘巽出俸钱十缗，又于寻常公用卖故纸钱四五十索，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>相兼</span>使用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164389_comment'></div>此钱本由斥卖弃物，两曾奏闻本院，自来<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/134/Comments/0")'>支使</span>不系诸处帐籍，如外郡货卖杂物以充公用之类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164389_comment'></div>既以其祀神之馀，与馆阁同舍、本局群吏，饮食共费之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164389_comment'></div>推按甚明，具狱备在，无一物入己，而以监主自盗，减死一等定刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164389_comment'></div>法司前后断狱体例，及自有正条，并不引用，阁下察之，盖有由也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164389_comment'></div>某之偏言，似不足信，幸询于众论，及晓法而公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164389_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164389_comment'></div>国家制驭奸欺，示信天下者，今惟法律而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164389_comment'></div>盖法律著之于篇，众所共晓，茍一<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/159/Comments/0")'>倾挠</span>，人皆具知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164389_comment'></div>故太上钦慎，不敢自专，岂容有司自为轻重，茍快己志，以隳旧典，污辱善士，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/167/Comments/0")'>戕害</span>不辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164389_comment'></div>况本朝自祥符以来，一用宽典，吏有奸赃狼籍，未尝致于深刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164389_comment'></div>今上仁明爱物，度越前古，官吏一入人罪者，往往十馀年未尝升擢，或沈于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/176/Comments/0")'>铨调</span>，不与改官，此见圣心慎刑恶杀之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164389_comment'></div>而某被此冤滥，又有端由，但未为钜公开陈而建白之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164389_comment'></div>天聪一闻，玉色必悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164389_comment'></div>阁下以英伟之量，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/185/Comments/0")'>押领</span>魁柄，必以康济民物，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1164389", 1164389, "Clauses/187/Comments/0")'>湔涤</span>冤滞为己任，故某不避冒渎，以铺此言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164389_comment'></div>况某者潜心策书，积有岁月，前古治乱之根本，当今文武之方略，粗通一二，亦能施设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164389_comment'></div>废弃疏贱，不信于时，帷明公召而与言，资相其质，衡鉴之下，安可妄欺？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164389_comment'></div>敛之弃之，俯伏俟命，谨具手启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164389_comment'></div>云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1164389_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　有诗。作品：感兴。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于是年初春。）</span><div id='poem_495647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感兴三首<span class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495647'>后寝藏衣冠，前庙宅神主。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495647'>吾闻诸礼经，此制出中古。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495647'>秦嬴蚀先法，乃复祭于墓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495647'>汉衣以月游，于道盖无取。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495647'>宣帝尊祖庙，失制遍九土。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495647'>孝元酌前文，一旦悉除去。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495647'>魏帝乐铜台，遗令置歌舞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495647'>昏嗣竟从之，此事狂夫阻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495647'>唐制益纷华，诸陵锁嫔御。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495647'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_495647", 495647, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>旷女</span>日哀吟，于先亦奚补。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495647'>吾朝三圣人，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_495647", 495647, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>乘云</span>不可睹。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495647'>威灵已霄汉，嗣皇念宗祖。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495647'>绘事移天光，刻象肖神武。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495647'>功既即奉迎，法仗叠箫鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495647'>玩好择珍奇，目夺不可数。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495647'>三京佛老家，已有十数处。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495647'>朝家虽奉先，越礼古不许。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495647'>君不祭臣仆，父<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作又）</span>不祭支庶。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495647'>丹楹岂非孝，圣贬甚萧斧。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495647'>大祀当以时，寝庙即其所。<div id='poem_sentence_23_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_495647'>苍生何其愚，瞻叹走旁午。<div id='poem_sentence_24_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_495647'>贱子私自嗟，伤时泪如雨。<div id='poem_sentence_25_495647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_495647'></div><div id='poem_title_495649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495649?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1031年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495649'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495649'>瞽说圣所择，愚谋帝不罪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495649'>况乎言有文，<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_2_495649'>前日林书生，自谓胸臆大。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495649'>潜心摭世病，荣成谓可卖。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495649'>宗支若系囚，亲亲礼日杀。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_495649'>嗟乎林书生，生命不可再。<div id='poem_sentence_28_495649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_495649_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　有诗酬叶清臣。作品：某为世所弃困居于苏平生交游过门不顾长安侍读叶丈不以秦吴之远高下之隔悯此穷悴特贶以诗然韵险句奇不可攀续仰酬高谊强抉芜音。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于是年春。）</span><div id='poem_495828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495828?labeling=true' href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495828")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495828_comment'></div><div "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>剧权</span>，远嗟穷苦寄新篇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495828'>气雄迥出关河外，句险空惊鱼鸟前。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495828'>才愚荣悴皆殊绝，自笑相酬更斐然。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495828'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　有诗。作品：中秋松江新桥对月和柳令之作（月晃长江上下同）秋雨。秋怀。<span class='inlineComment2'>（当作于庆历七、八年。）</span>春睡。<div id='poem_225465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_225465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/225465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴淞江 其三<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>中秋对月</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29768, "北宋", "蒋堂", "poem_title_225465")'>蒋堂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_225465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_225465'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_225465'>月晃长江上下同，画桥横截冷光中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_225465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_225465'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_225465", 225465, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>云头</span>艳艳开金饼，水面沉沉卧彩虹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_225465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_225465'>佛氏解为银色界，仙家多住玉壶中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_225465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_225465'>地雄景胜言不尽，但欲追随乘晓风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_225465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_225465'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_225465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_content_495761'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495761'>院僻帘深昼景虚，轻风时见动竿乌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495761'>池中绿满鱼留子，庭下阴多燕引雏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495761'>雨后看儿争坠果，天晴同客曝残书。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495761'>幽栖未免牵尘事，身世相忘在酒壶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_495793'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495793'>吴天摇落奈愁何，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_495793", 495793, id='poem_sentence_1_495793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495793'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495793_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　在沧浪亭怀范师道。作品：沧浪亭怀贯之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_137868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_137868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/137868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沧浪亭怀贯之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_137868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_137868'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_137868'>沧浪独步亦无悰，聊上危台四望中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_137868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_137868'>秋色入林红黯澹，日光穿竹翠玲珑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_137868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_137868'>酒徒飘落风前燕，诗社凋零霜后桐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_137868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_137868'>君又暂来还径往<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄本、陈本作往）</span>，醉吟谁复伴衰翁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_137868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_137868'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_137868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_137868'><span class='label'>按：</span>以上《苏舜钦集》卷七<br /></div><div id='poem_note_137868_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　有诗。作品：沧浪静吟。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>秋夜。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>小酌。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>冬夕偶书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>遣闷。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>沧浪观鱼。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>西轩垂钓偶作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>夜闻笮酒有声因而成咏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>览照。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>夜中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>苦调。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>吴江岸（晓色兼秋色）<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span>顶破二山诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_137869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_137869' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　有诗答章傅。作品：答章傅。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于庆历五年四月至庆历八年十二月旅居苏州期间，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_495713' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495713' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495713?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答章傅</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_495713_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495713'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495713'>废官旅吴门，迹与世俗扫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495713'>构亭沧浪间，筑室乔树杪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495713'>穷径交圣贤，放意狎鱼鸟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495713'>志气内自充，藜藿日亦饱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495713'>不图名利场，有士同所好。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495713'>南闽章其氏，傅名字传道。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495713'>清晨闯予门，<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_7_495713'>大篇随自出，烂熳风力老。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495713'>安敢当所褒，读之俗惊倒。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495713'>开轩延与语，指亦有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_495713", 495713, class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495799'>犹得云山开醉眼，可无俗物挠冲襟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495799'>鵩来閒暇何须怪，鬼见揶揄岂易禁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495725'>步<span class='inlineComment2'>（李本作捕）</span>虎南山隈，气立<span id='poem_sentence_1_495668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495668'>男儿生世间，有如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495668", 495668, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>绝壑</span>松。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495668'>误为风雷伤，不与匠石逢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495668'>哀哉千尺干，摧折似<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>秋蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495668'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_495668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495668'><span class='label'>按：</span>以上《苏舜钦集》卷一<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_495668_0'>⑴ 原作以，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495668_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　复官后作谢启。作品：上执政启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（是年下年复官后作。）</span><div id='poem_1164406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上执政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164406")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164406'>近者，被中宸之书，叨上佐之命，起于放废，仍获便安，是为异恩，曷胜感惕！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164406_comment'></div>伏念某幼而向学，长则多忧，场屋十年，闲关四举，才叨科级，连被凶艰，血属沦亡，生理凋尽，仅存残息，勉就小官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164406_comment'></div>还台之初，辱上公之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164406_comment'></div>给笔以试，预道山之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164406_comment'></div>素为忧患之所丛，遂以畏慎而成性，言皆三复，动必再思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164406_comment'></div>且留邸之祀神，缘常岁而为会，馂馀共享，京局皆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164406_comment'></div>窃谓前规有所未便，起无名之率，会不肖之徒，且醵敛吏人，岂如斥卖弃物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164406_comment'></div>啸聚非类，岂如宴集同僚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164406_comment'></div>更出私钱，以助公费，馀循旧贯，先即上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164406_comment'></div>岂意谤諠台中，章彻宸极，因猜嫌而生隙，谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164406", 1164406, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>猥亵</span>以当惩，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164406", 1164406, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>造谖</span>以动上聪，持必以变朝论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164406_comment'></div>捽首就吏，虽具狱而无他；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164406_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164406", 1164406, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>刺骨</span>定刑，终削籍而见弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164406_comment'></div>素承清白之训，枉被盗贼之名，近戚当涂，陈冤无路，徊徨去国，举动畏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164406_comment'></div>僒尔羁旅之囚，漂然江海之上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164406_comment'></div>出则鬼揶揄而见笑，居则鵩閒暇以相窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164406_comment'></div>不及虫鼠之生，仅与草木为伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164406_comment'></div>三逢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164406", 1164406, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>恩沾</span>，四换岁纪，弗敢自述，已分陆沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164406_comment'></div>不图特降命书，复登仕版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164406_comment'></div>此盖相公<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1164406", 1164406, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>运斡</span>元化，翕张洪炉，赞天地生育之私，布朝廷宽大之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164406_comment'></div>虑一物之失，适万物之宜，顾惟摈斥之微，亦预甄陶之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164406_comment'></div>谓诛意无害，且论法本轻，取宣尼观过之言，酌《春秋》原情之义，度此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1164406", 1164406, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>衅累</span>，渐而收效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164406_comment'></div>古人睹道上之遗簪，为之泣涕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164406_comment'></div>匠者得沟中之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1164406", 1164406, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>断木</span>，饰以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1164406", 1164406, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>青黄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164406_comment'></div>是为不忍遐遗，有所倡劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164406_comment'></div>誓固困穷之节，上酬提品之私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1164406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年11月5日</a>　应僧惠源乞文作。作品：苏州洞庭山水月禅院记。<div id='poem_1164425' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164425' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164425?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏州洞庭山水月禅院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年11月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164425")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164425_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164425'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164425'>予乙酉岁夏四月，来居吴门，始维舟，即登灵岩之颠，以望太湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164425_comment'></div>俯视洞庭山，崭然特起，霞云采翠，浮动于沧波之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164425_comment'></div>予时据阑竦首，精爽下堕，欲乘清风，跨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164425", 1164425, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>落景</span>，以翱翔乎其间，莫可得也，自尔平居，缅然思于一到，惑于险说而未果行，则常若有物腷塞于胸中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164425_comment'></div>是岁十月，遂招徐、陈二君，浮轻舟，出横金口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164425_comment'></div>观其洪川荡潏，万顷一色，不知天地之大所能并容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164425_comment'></div>水程溯洄，七十里而远，初宿社下，踰日乃至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164425_comment'></div>入林屋洞，陟毛公坛，宿包山精舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164425_comment'></div>又泛明月湾，南望一山，上摩苍烟，舟人指云：「此所谓缥缈峰也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164425_comment'></div>即岸，步自松间，出数里，至峰下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164425_comment'></div>有佛庙号水月者，阁殿甚古，像设严焕，旁有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164425", 1164425, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>澄泉</span>，洁清甘凉，极旱不枯，不类他水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164425_comment'></div>梁大同四年始建佛寺，至隋大业六年遂废不存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164425_comment'></div>唐光化中，有浮屠志勤者，历游四方，至此，爱而不能去，复于旧址结庐诵经，后因而屋之，至数十百楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164425_comment'></div>天祐四年，刺史曹圭以「明月」名其院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164425_comment'></div>勤老且死，其徒嗣之，迄今七世不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164425_comment'></div>国朝大中祥符初，有诏又易今名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164425_comment'></div>予观震泽受三江，吞齧四郡之封，其中，山之名见图志者七十有二，惟洞庭称雄其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164425_comment'></div>地占三乡，户率三千，环四十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164425_comment'></div>民俗真朴，历岁未尝有诉讼至于县吏之庭下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164425_comment'></div>皆以树桑栀甘柚为常产，每秋高霜馀，丹苞朱实，与长松茂树相参差，间于岩壑间望之，若图绘金翠之可爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164425_comment'></div>缥缈峰又居山之西北深远处，高耸出于众山，为洞庭胜绝之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164425_comment'></div>居山之民以少事，尚其岁时织紃、树艺、捕采之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164425_comment'></div>浮屠氏本以清旷远物事，已出中国礼法之外，复居湖山深远胜绝之地，壤断水慑，人迹罕至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164425_comment'></div>数僧宴坐，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1164425", 1164425, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>寂嘿</span>于泉石之间，引而与语，殊无纤介世俗间<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1164425", 1164425, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>气韵</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164425_comment'></div>其视舒舒，其行于于，岂上世之遗民者邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164425_comment'></div>予生平病闷郁塞，至此，喝然破散无复馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164425_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1164425", 1164425, "Clauses/102/Comments/0")'>反复</span>身世，惘然莫知，但如蜕解俗骨，傅之羽翰，飞出于八荒之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164425_comment'></div>吁，其快哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164425_comment'></div>后三年，其徒惠源造予乞文，识其居之废兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164425_comment'></div>欣其见请，揽笔直述，且叙昔游之胜焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164425_comment'></div>庆历七年十一月五日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1164425_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

杭州

ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495772")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495772_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495772'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495772'>支肘听潮声，喧豗久未停。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495772'>随风过渔浦<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：江东地名。）</span>，伴月出沧溟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495772'>䲡穴浚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>时满，胥神果有灵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495772'>连天卷云雾，彻晓下雷霆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495772'>舍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>楫游心倦，凭阑醉魄醒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495772'>谁穷造物意，拟访郦元经。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 黄本、陈本作后，四库本作候</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_495772_0'>⑵ 原作拾，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495772_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ea8c84b5613749248019d899c8348a73_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ea8c84b5613749248019d899c8348a73");'><span id='ea8c84b5613749248019d899c8348a73_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>，39岁</div><div id='ea8c84b5613749248019d899c8348a73' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>浙东之行作。作品：关都官孤山四照阁。清轩。<div id='poem_495826' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495826' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495826?labeling=true' target='_blank'>关都官孤山四照阁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495826")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495826_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495826'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495826'>势压苍崖险可惊，攀云半日到<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_495826", 495826, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>轩楹</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495826_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495826'>旁观竹树<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_495826", 495826, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>回环</span>翠，下视湖山表里清。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495826_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495826'>惭觉愁随烟霭散，只疑身有羽翰生。<div "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>蜡屐</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495826", 495826, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>邛枝</span>伴此行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495827'>我公亦为留奇句，此地人间合有灵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='892d618644554a3a833ff5211267a326_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("892d618644554a3a833ff5211267a326");'><span id='892d618644554a3a833ff5211267a326_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>奔母丧至会稽后作。作品：越州云门寺。<div id='poem_495675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495675?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_495675'>老松偃蹇若傲世，飞泉喷薄如避人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495675'>苍猿啸断夜月古，丹花开遍阳崖春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495770'>殿阁北垂连禹庙，松筠东去入稽山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
淮安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='964ea6a723c64b21a881d631a5f55700_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("964ea6a723c64b21a881d631a5f55700");'><span id='964ea6a723c64b21a881d631a5f55700_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，34岁</div><div id='964ea6a723c64b21a881d631a5f55700' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　与朱处仁遇于山阳，为其父撰墓铭。作品：歙州黟县令朱君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1164441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>歙州黟县令朱君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164441")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164441'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164441'>沛国朱处仁表臣，少从予游，长又同登进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164441_comment'></div>表臣宦于楚，予适越，遇表臣，喜语，既且泣曰：「仆将葬祖、父于真，有期矣，敢以铭烦于君，其毋拒」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164441_comment'></div>予诺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164441_comment'></div>表臣遂状其世曰：先君讳咸熙，字某，其先宣城人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164441_comment'></div>曾祖训，唐末事李氏至歙州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164441_comment'></div>生景勋，弘毅尚气节，阴知世将有变，遂徙其孥山东，占营丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164441_comment'></div>生保衡，少明孔氏《尚书》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164441_comment'></div>太平兴国中登本科，授冀州司理参军，再选达州东乡主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164441_comment'></div>时贼顺骚两川，邻城不守，邑令吕弃印以逸，主簿独闭壁坚守，势诎遇害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164441_comment'></div>时先君侍，年才十三，度不能力，遂挺身脱贼刃下，日夜踔数舍，冒没于凶党中，变名姓，作蜀俚人语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164441_comment'></div>谍知官军至开州，趣出主帅前，泣曰：「我东乡主簿之子，不幸父以贼死，而家有母妹在青州，相去数千里，不能自通，幸挈出死境，使归奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164441", 1164441, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>偏亲</span>以养，惠施大矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164441_comment'></div>帅哀怜之，使骑于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164441_comment'></div>贼平，道华之渭南，逢吕令居焉，语曰：「汝父戕于难，今汝幼又孤，能至此以遇我，天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164441_comment'></div>山东道阻，当留无往，必教育使汝成而后行，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164441_comment'></div>从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164441_comment'></div>吕令嘉其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164441", 1164441, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>谨强</span>向学，善视若诸子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164441_comment'></div>遂许以女妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164441_comment'></div>后六年，同至都下自论，敕赐同学究出身，时咸平三年冬十一月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164441_comment'></div>还家拜亲，喜极哀动，乃侍奉赴调，授濠州定远主簿、绵州司法参军、博州司理、濠州录事、耀州淳化令，五任十有五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164441_comment'></div>据法平直不挠，未尝过差，然不肯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1164441", 1164441, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>悒纳</span>上官，故无有通荐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164441_comment'></div>天禧三年秋，罢官淳化，因类刑书，主司为奏御，求补法寺吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164441_comment'></div>未报得疾，踰年弗平，勉授歙州黟县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164441_comment'></div>夏五月，舟至宋，疾甚，叹曰：「吾出险艰，得官以庇族，洁躬奉法，不敢以欺，死固有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164441_comment'></div>然子幼，家无资，何以奉母？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164441_comment'></div>幸外舅官于泗，可亟往，以吾诚告之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164441_comment'></div>言毕而逝，时五月朔也，享年三十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164441_comment'></div>踰宿至泗，遂稿葬于佛庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164441_comment'></div>徙旅于真，诸孤家白沙，从吕舅之庇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164441_comment'></div>夫人后君一年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164441_comment'></div>母李氏，后三年亦殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164441_comment'></div>四子：长即处仁，泗州判官，监楚州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164441_comment'></div>次处约，登进士甲科，知南安军上犹县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164441_comment'></div>处中、处厚，皆夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164441_comment'></div>予见前人罹祸患，虽奴辱折屈，茍活而不自羞，卒能奋起，以成勋名，盖独虑其亡躯耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164441_comment'></div>长官幼齿，而遂合此术，呜呼贤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164441_comment'></div>向使如常童<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1164441", 1164441, "Clauses/136/Comments/0")'>悲慕</span>不能自引去，徒血凶锋，于祸无所转，则家君死难之节不表，而朱氏之祀殄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164441_comment'></div>今二子皆成名，干而有文采，赫大门闾，安可涯涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164441_comment'></div>长官没踰二十年，仁、约以俸卜葬于真州某县某乡，举夫人以祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164441_comment'></div>又复东乡之魂，以大王母李氏合葬于兆之北，中与厚又属其旁，以某年月日之吉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164441_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1164441'>东乡死官，忠节较然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164441_comment'></div>君脱凶难，可以孝言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164441_comment'></div>命狭禄小，世嗟其贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164441_comment'></div>二子是似，此其曰天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164441_comment'></div>葬得吉壤，冈趋水旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164441_comment'></div>濯濯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1164441", 1164441, "Clauses/163/Comments/0")'>灵魄</span>，安此万年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1164441_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a9f4dfbb04864f32b62251f09cc79ea0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a9f4dfbb04864f32b62251f09cc79ea0");'><span id='a9f4dfbb04864f32b62251f09cc79ea0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1043')">1042-1043年</a>，35-36岁</div><div id='a9f4dfbb04864f32b62251f09cc79ea0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　聚族寓居山阳守制。作品：寄富彦国。观放牐。东京宝相禅院新建大悲殿记。答杜公书。<div id='poem_495679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄富彦国</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495679")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495679'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495679'>自古猾者胡与羌，胡羌相连动朔方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495679'>奸谋阴就一朝发，直欲截割吾土疆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495679'>遣使持书至阙下，四方物论如沸汤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495679'>天子仄席旰未尝，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495679", 495679, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>相君</span>日暮犹庙堂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495679'>彦国感慨请奉使，誓将摧折其锋铓。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495679'>受诏驱马出都门，都人走观叹且伤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495679'>猾胡闻风已<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_495679", 495679, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>厌伏</span>，聚听大议羞乱常。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495679'>愿如故约不敢妄，脱甲争献宝玉觞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495679'>旆旌威迟还上国，所至观者如倾江。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495679'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_495679", 495679, "Clauses/18/Comments/1")'>杖父</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作丈夫）</span>奔蹶喜出泣，妇女聚语气激昂。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495679'>至尊虚怀坐赭床，中人催入见未央。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495679'>对久赤日下辇道，翠华影转熏风凉。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495679'>归来堂上拜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_495679", 495679, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>寿母</span>，宾车塞破甘泉坊。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495679'>衣尘未涤又出使，往来绝域如门墙。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495679'>已知高贤抱器识，因时与国为辉光。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495679'>不烦一甲屈万众，以此可见才短长。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495679'>彦国本为廊庙器，何祗口舌平强梁。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495679'>使之当国柄天下，夷狄岂复能猖狂。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495679'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_495679_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_495718' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495718' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495718?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观放闸</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495718")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495718_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495718'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495718'>沈沈沧淮口，植木限众流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495718'>启闭固有时，出纳千万舟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495718'>眷予<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>怀抱昏，羁别相牵钩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495718'>观此巨派注，颇觉滞闷瘳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495718'>喧豗怒霆起，始骇久不收。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495718'>既前目眩转，足缩不敢留。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495718'>朔雪下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_495718", 495718, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>喷薄</span>，散为白雾浮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495718'>上悬赤油幕，旁断缥玉旒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495718'>恐激地轴转，人有鱼鳖忧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495718'>惊嗟势力壮，孰谓此物柔。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495718'>吾思作至监，实以处上游。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495718'>又欲接之口，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_495718", 495718, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>沃荡</span>胸中愁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495718'>俄然渐枯涸，哮尔空泥沟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495718'>渟滀既因人，开泄岂自由。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495718'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_495718", 495718, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>立间</span>见底里，咄哉为尔羞。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495718'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_495718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495718'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_495718_0'>⑴ 原作卷子，据黄本、陈本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495718_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1164422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东京宝相禅院新建大悲殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年4月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164422")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164422'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164422'>京城之西南，有佛庙曰宝相院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164422_comment'></div>中有层阁，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164422", 1164422, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>杰然</span>以庇大像，其像高数十百尺，而阁又加是，世传隋大业中所为，盖亦可信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164422_comment'></div>大业于今，年祀虽远，阁与像甚完，是必少坏，后人随而葺之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164422_comment'></div>国朝祥符中，有诏葺之，完矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164422_comment'></div>天圣戊辰岁，浮屠庆祥者又欲于阁之阴，以铁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164422", 1164422, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>范像</span>，号大悲，而又阁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164422_comment'></div>事暴闻上，上为命入内押班江德明、入内供奉官、勾当御药院德用、入内高品邓惟素三人往司之，又诏有司给铁及薪炭十馀万斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164422_comment'></div>明年夏五月，庆祥卒，德淮嗣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164422_comment'></div>庚午秋，始作巨冶大櫜，一鼓而就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164422_comment'></div>手目千数，较无一阙，侍卫跗坐，严正森立，如有神物阴为之容，虽刻绘之工所不能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164422_comment'></div>明肃庄献皇后崩，阁废不作，已而又命入内供奉官赵用志、朱文用易阁以殿，景祐元年又罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164422_comment'></div>德淮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1164422", 1164422, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>隳懈</span>自劾去，众以今智圆大师方益主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164422_comment'></div>三年，入内都知王惟忠列章以白，上旨可焉，以谏官言又罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164422_comment'></div>四年，方益挝鼓以闻，乃赐禁钱四百万，以入内供奉官、勾当御药院张承吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164422_comment'></div>入内黄门冯正己籍用之，踰年遂就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164422_comment'></div>予始闻之，疑其久而后能成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164422_comment'></div>及观其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164422", 1164422, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>闳豁</span>奥大，然后叹息焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164422_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164422_comment'></div>在昔圣人因人情而制礼也，是故宫室服用必有度，上下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1164422", 1164422, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>等杀</span>各安其分限，而无流暴之患，此三代之所以为盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164422_comment'></div>自汉以下无制作，幸而识其流风，监以自足乎一世，故颇亦有所放矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164422_comment'></div>佛氏之教入中国，当其无制之世，其宫室服用之作，隘者犹能上王者一等，后世奉之益炽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164422_comment'></div>今民远于三代，而但见隋唐之事，以为古可法，奔于夸胜之境，莫知其纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164422_comment'></div>是以朝廷杀阁以室屋，而又滞留，久之而不亟为，始于戊辰，而讫于景祐戊寅，十馀年间，三以废格，是亦监而有意焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164422_comment'></div>非中寺之赞，方益之悫，而事其事，则乌能成之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164422_comment'></div>盖欲识其始以永于后，故求予文，琢于石云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164422_comment'></div>时庆历二年四月五日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1164422_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1164395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答杜公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164395")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164395'>伏捧十一月十七日病告中所遣书教，笔墨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>精劲</span>，慰谕曲折，深开<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>忧灼</span>烦苦之抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164395_comment'></div>所示梦有求解之劝，此乃区区之心，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>积诚</span>有所上通也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164395_comment'></div>抑又有说焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164395_comment'></div>丈人才略闳远，而跻位至此，复值朝廷多事之时，必将开发素蕴，以尊主康民，使天下想望风采，讴歌德业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164395_comment'></div>而后世<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>法则</span>其所为，以拯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>弊乱</span>，虽数百千年，赫赫不忘，凛然尚有生气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164395_comment'></div>此大君子之事业，丈人之所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>夙怀</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164395_comment'></div>古人常患天不与之全，茍得其全，径可至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164395_comment'></div>盖或得其位而无其才，有其才而无其时者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164395_comment'></div>丈人才位如此，而又当有为之时，是天付之全，而使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>施设</span>才业之秋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164395_comment'></div>设丈人有此才，逢此时，而不得此位，则某必当叹息<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>泣涕</span>而相吊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164395_comment'></div>今丈人其位其才其时，而某反数数有求解之劝，是不愚则狂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164395_comment'></div>然以丈人自入枢府，于今二年馀矣，虽天下共知丈人于朝廷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>谟谋</span>论议，日有所补，然未厌天下之所以望丈人之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164395_comment'></div>盖贤者未甚进，不肖者未甚退，二边猖炽，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>兵帅</span>数败，科率诛敛，天下骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164395_comment'></div>丈人虽抱雄才，处高位，反为人牵制，上下踬碍而不能尽伸，徒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>卷缩</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/53/Comments/1")'>忧郁</span>，成疾病于胸中，内损天和，外隳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>物望</span>，生平辛苦为善得令名，至此而削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164395_comment'></div>以此论之，较其得失轻重，是不若解之之当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164395_comment'></div>或以谓某呶呶烦辞劝解者，以丈人当涂而己不得进，此庸人之说，恐或有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164395_comment'></div>若丈人得尽其才，使天下和平，某虽老死圳亩，终身不入仕宦，如在三旌之位也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164395_comment'></div>所可痛者，丈人之心与古人通，而其才可以治世成务，而不得尽发以救艰急，此义夫烈士之所感激而恸哭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164395_comment'></div>日月可惜，功名易隳，处虽为难，退亦未易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164395_comment'></div>今虽能倖然引去，无补于时，亦安足以为嘉事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164395_comment'></div>昔夫子、孟氏无位，尚屑屑走列国，见其陪臣，虽甚鄙恶者，犹皆以言语感动，庶乎一行其所言，以休乎生民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164395_comment'></div>况今太上好谏乐善，丈人日对<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1164395", 1164395, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>天光</span>，故未可与彼同年而语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164395_comment'></div>今若能挺然不顾，竭力尽忠，使言行策施，则天下被其赐，与夫默默全身而去者万里矣，茍不得已，则荐贤代己，逡巡而退，亦不失古人去就之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164395_comment'></div>此必丈人夙昔之所在念，然尚恐为佞谀之言，上惑高明，故不避缕述也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164395_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1164395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　聚族寓居山阳守制，韩绛前来慰问，有诗送别。作品：送韩三子华还家。<div id='poem_495717' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495717' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495717?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送韩三子华还家</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495717")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495717_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495717'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495717'>人在天壤间，共为气躯逐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495717'>岁月自崩奔，冉冉若转毂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495717'>荣乐随云烟，凋零共草木。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495717'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_495717", 495717, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>亨屯</span>固常物，达者安可速。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495717'>奈何此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_495717", 495717, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>躯骸</span>，未免混世俗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495717'>前年奔大凶，况复堕手足。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495717'>嗟我颜色枯，须苍鬓又秃。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　聚族寓居山阳守制，有诗送陈进士。作品：送陈进士游江南。<div id='poem_495744' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495744' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_495744_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　聚族寓居山阳守制，有记。作品：涟水军新牐记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑守制山阳时作。）</span><div id='poem_1164428' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164428' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164428?labeling=true' target='_blank'>涟水军新闸记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_1164428")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164428_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164428'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164428'>古之障川，有防猪庸遂列浍之法，以既见于经也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164428_comment'></div>堰埭堤阏、作堋树栅之制，见于旧史也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164428_comment'></div>然未闻为闸之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164428_comment'></div>盖精思者缘古而作，兴于近世，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164428", 1164428, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>通漕</span>最为便，惜乎无所述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164428_comment'></div>被淮之邦，襄贲为之近，有渠由郡入东海，尾受于淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164428_comment'></div>其间县官立四场，斡盐榷茗，岁转数十百万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164428_comment'></div>民鲜鱐蟹稻之饶，以是舟相衔不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164428_comment'></div>淮口北走一里，有埭以壅渠，每潮汐暴至乃可过，并海长落甚驶，而又石沙填溃，不可疏，与淮等，故多反壤以败舟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164428_comment'></div>至者必淹旬旷月，不得遽去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164428_comment'></div>或谓埭下切淮，辖木为之闸，使渟泄启闭，相潮上下，则无复留行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164428_comment'></div>前人视习，绝不置论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164428_comment'></div>司勋员外郎刘君署郡之日，竦然念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164428_comment'></div>以地褊役大，稍难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164428_comment'></div>会转运使、按部继至，令倡其利，即时以闻，上指可之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164428_comment'></div>于是规括旁郡羡材冗兵，兴于庆历三年二月丙午，踰月而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164428_comment'></div>薪石一种之费，不诛于民间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164428_comment'></div>东汉王景绝水立门，去浚渠之患，号省费役，犹以百亿计，当时增秩，史氏与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164428_comment'></div>今三君之为，不劳于民，而休于民事，应古可纪，表之宜无愧也<span class='inlineComment2'>（《苏学士文集》卷一三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164428_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1164428'>入：原空，据沈校本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1164428_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　聚族寓居山阳守制，有诗送施秀才。作品：送施秀才。<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑守制山阳时作。）</span><div id='poem_495716' class='_poem'><div href='/Writing/238934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和子履雍家园<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_238934_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_238934_0'>① 原按：此诗亦见《欧阳文忠公集》外集卷七，题和子履游泗上雍家园。欧阳修辑录苏集，并为作序，不应杂入己作，此必苏诗无疑。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_238934'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_238934'>长桥南走群山间，中有雍子之名园。<div id='poem_sentence_0_238934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_238934'>苍云蔽天竹色净，暖香<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>扑地花气繁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_238934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_238934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_238934'>我来踞石弄琴瑟，唯恐日暮登归轩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_238934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_238934'>尘纷剥落耳目异，只疑梦入仙家村。<div id='poem_sentence_5_238934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_238934'>君之<span class='link' "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>闳放</span>莫可攀。<div id='poem_sentence_6_238934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_238934'>高篇绝景两不及，久之想像空<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_238934", 238934, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>冥烦</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_238934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495698")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495698_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495698'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495698'>落照满长河，流水暖冲融。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495698'>中有凫鹜群，上下随和风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495698'>徊徨但搔首，叹息无所容。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 无锡

<div class='label1' id='c059996ffd054c21944aed95a9e985b1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c059996ffd054c21944aed95a9e985b1");'><span id='c059996ffd054c21944aed95a9e985b1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>，38岁</div><div id='c059996ffd054c21944aed95a9e985b1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　游无锡，有诗。作品：无锡惠山寺。<span class='inlineComment2'>（是年秋作。）</span><div id='poem_495765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495765' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495765?labeling=true' target='_blank'>无锡惠山寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495765")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495765_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495765'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495765'>寺古名传唐相诗，三伏奔迸予何之。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495765'>云山相照翠会合，殿阁对走<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>凉参差。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495765'>清泉绝无一尘染，长松自是拔俗姿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495765'>二边羌胡日斗格，释子宴坐殊不知。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495765'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495765'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_495765_0'>⑴ 黄本、陈本作定，钱校作起</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495765_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
慈溪
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d1ae2b29c9aa4ee6aa8df29ad56eaaf0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d1ae2b29c9aa4ee6aa8df29ad56eaaf0");'><span id='d1ae2b29c9aa4ee6aa8df29ad56eaaf0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>，39岁</div><div id='d1ae2b29c9aa4ee6aa8df29ad56eaaf0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　浙东之行作。作品：重过句章郡。<div id='poem_495763' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495763' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495763?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重过句章郡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29828, "北宋", "苏舜钦", "poem_title_495763")'>苏舜钦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495763_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495763'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495763'>曾随使旆此东归，日日登临到落晖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495763'>畴昔侍行犹总角，如今重过合沾衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495763'>窥鱼翠碧忘形坐，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_495763", 495763, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>趁伴</span>蜻蜓照影飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495763'>风物依然皆自得，岁华飘忽赏心违。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495763'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495763'><span class='label'>按：</span>以上《苏舜钦集》卷六<br /></div><div id='poem_note_495763_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
